### [1] [A Non-Destructive Methodological Framework for Modernizing Legacy Clinical Reporting Systems for AI-Driven Pharmacoinformatics: A SAS Case Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13905v1)
*Jaime Yan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 一个非破坏性元数据框架通过包装遗留系统并引入中间表示，使临床报告实现AI就绪，在减少92%专有代码的同时保持监管合规。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 遗留临床报告系统阻碍AI集成，现有方法需在重写和增量重构间取舍，缺乏非破坏性路径。

Method: 提出元数据层包括桥接映射、类型化IR和编排器，包装遗留组件，实现可选增量整合。

Result: 在大型SAS库上验证，共存模式即AI就绪；整合后专有代码减少92%；14种报告类型中11种达80%以上细胞级一致性，平均82.7%，最佳99.2%；LLM实验证明自动化能力。

Conclusion: 提供监管感知的AI集成路径，加速药物开发而不中断提交。

中文摘要：药物开发和药物警戒经常受到遗留临床报告流程的瓶颈制约。这些单体系统编码了监管级别的逻辑，但由于产生不透明输出且没有机器可读的中间层，阻碍了AI集成。现有的现代化方法迫使人们在全面重写和保留结构性障碍的增量重构之间做出选择。我们提出了一种非破坏性的方法论框架，在不修改遗留源代码的情况下实现AI驱动的药物信息学就绪。一个元数据层——包括桥接映射、类型化中间表示（IR）和编排器——包装现有组件，并将其输出重新暴露为LLM可消费的结构化数据。它支持可选的增量整合，用元数据配置的核心例程替换选定的遗留组件，而其余部分保持不变。在一个包含558个组件的SAS报告库（373,000行代码）上验证，该框架在共存模式下展示了即时的AI就绪性，产生机器可读的输出。在选定整合的情况下，现代化核心实现了专有代码减少92%。对来自III期研究的14种报告类型进行一致性验证，11个报告达到80%或以上的细胞级一致性（平均82.7%，最佳99.2%）。使用CDISC CDISCPilot01数据的基准测试在所有5个报告上实现了100%的一致性。LLM实验证实IR能够实现自动化药物警戒、表格总结和试验配置生成。该框架提供了一条监管感知的路径，实现AI整合的临床报告，加速药物开发而不中断监管提交。

Original abstract: Drug development and pharmacovigilance are frequently bottlenecked by legacy clinical reporting pipelines. These monolithic systems encode regulatory-grade logic but resist AI integration by producing opaque output with no machine-readable intermediate layer. Existing modernization approaches force a choice between full rewrites and incremental refactoring that preserves structural barriers. We present a non-destructive methodological framework achieving AI-driven pharmacoinformatics readiness without altering legacy source code. A metadata layer--comprising a bridge map, a typed Intermediate Representation (IR), and an orchestrator--wraps existing components and re-exposes their outputs as structured data consumable by LLMs. It enables optional incremental consolidation, replacing selected legacy components with metadata-configured core routines while the remainder operates unchanged. Validated on a 558-component SAS reporting library (373,000 lines of code), the framework demonstrated immediate AI-readiness under coexistence mode, yielding machine-readable output. Where consolidation was elected, the modernized core achieved a 92% reduction in proprietary code. Parity validation on 14 report types from a Phase III study achieved cell-level parity of 80% or above on 11 reports (mean 82.7%, best 99.2%). A benchmark using CDISC CDISCPilot01 data achieved 100% parity across 5 reports. LLM experiments confirmed the IR enables automated pharmacovigilance, table summarization, and trial configuration generation. The framework offers a regulation-aware path to AI-integrated clinical reporting, accelerating drug development without interrupting regulatory submissions.

</details>


### [2] [AgentLens: Revealing The Lucky Pass Problem in SWE-Agent Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12925v3)
*Priyam Sahoo,Gaurav Mittal,Xiaomin Li,Shengjie Ma,Benjamin Steenhoek,Pingping Lin,Yu Hu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 引入AgentLens框架对SWE智能体轨迹进行过程级评估，发现10.7%的通过轨迹是“幸运通过”，质量分数能区分不同等级的通过并重新排名模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SWE智能体评估仅依赖最终补丁是否通过测试，这种二元信号忽略了过程质量，导致原则性方案和试错过程被等同，但经验证明这种等同是错误的。

Method: 构建任务级前缀树接受器（PTA）参考，通过合并多个通过解；使用上下文敏感的意图标注器将动作分类为探索、实现、验证或编排。

Result: 在2,614条轨迹中，1,815条用于评估，10.7%的通过轨迹是幸运通过；幸运率在0.5%-23.2%之间；按质量分数排名时，一些模型移动多达五个位置。

Conclusion: 计划发布项目仓库，包括AgentLens-Bench制品、SDK和分析工具。

中文摘要：对软件工程（SWE）智能体的评估主要取决于一个二元信号：最终补丁是否通过测试。这种仅看结果的观点将原则性的解决方案与混乱的试错过程视为等同。我们证明这种等同性在经验上是错误的。我们评估了来自八个模型后端的2,614条OpenHands轨迹在60个SWE-bench Verified任务上的表现。其中，47个任务有足够多的通过轨迹来构建任务级过程参考，产生了1,815条轨迹的评估子集。在这个子集中，通过轨迹中有10.7%表现出我们称之为幸运通过的行为：回归循环、盲目重试、缺失验证、或时间上无序的探索、实现和验证。我们引入AgentLens，一个用于SWE智能体轨迹过程级评估的框架，并定义AgentLens-Bench，一个包含1,815条轨迹的数据集，标注有质量分数、浪费信号、分歧点以及47个任务级前缀树接受器（PTA）参考。AgentLens通过合并同一任务的多个通过解来构建PTA参考，并使用上下文敏感的意图标注器基于轨迹历史而非仅工具身份将动作分类为探索、实现、验证或编排。在AgentLens-Bench上，质量分数将通过轨迹分为幸运、稳固和理想三个等级，并进一步将幸运通过分解为五种重复机制。在八个模型后端中，幸运率从0.5%到23.2%不等，当按质量分数而非通过率排名时，一些模型移动了多达五个排名位置。我们计划很快发布项目仓库，包括AgentLens-Bench制品、AgentLens SDK和分析工具。

Original abstract: Evaluation of software engineering (SWE) agents is dominated by a binary signal: whether the final patch passes the tests. This outcome-only view treats a principled solution and a chaotic trial-and-error process as equivalent. We show that this equivalence is empirically false. We evaluate 2,614 OpenHands trajectories from eight model backends on 60 SWE-bench Verified tasks. Of these, 47 have enough passing trajectories to construct task-level process references, yielding a 1,815-trajectory evaluation subset. Among passing trajectories in this subset, 10.7% exhibit behavior we call a Lucky Pass: regression cycles, blind retries, missing verification, or temporally disordered exploration, implementation, and verification.
  We introduce AgentLens, a framework for process-level assessment of SWE-agent trajectories, and define AgentLens-Bench, a dataset of 1,815 trajectories annotated with quality scores, waste signals, divergence points, and 47 task-level Prefix Tree Acceptor (PTA) references. AgentLens builds PTA references by merging multiple passing solutions for the same task, and uses a context-sensitive intent labeler to assign actions to Exploration, Implementation, Verification, or Orchestration based on trajectory history rather than tool identity alone.
  On AgentLens-Bench, the quality score separates passing trajectories into Lucky, Solid, and Ideal tiers and further decomposes Lucky Passes into five recurring mechanisms. Across the eight model backends, Lucky rates range from 0.5% to 23.2%, and some models move by as many as five rank positions when ranked by quality score instead of pass rate. We plan to release the project repository soon, including AgentLens-Bench artifacts, the AgentLens SDK, and the analysis tooling.

</details>


### [3] [Protocol-Driven Development: Governing Generated Software Through Invariants and Continuous Evidence](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12981v3)
*Jun He,Deying Yu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: PDD通过机器可执行的协议定义可接受的实现空间，利用证据链和动态账本保证合规，使代码可替换而协议持久权威。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决自动化程序合成中因自然语言规范模糊和示例测试不完整导致的治理难题，即如何确定生成产物是否可接受。

Method: 定义协议三元组(S,B,O)约束结构、行为和操作；通过约束搜索发现实现；构建证据链（运行时扩展为动态证据账本）进行合规验证。

Result: 实现仅在满足协议且有可验证证据链时被接受；动态证据账本连接运行时故障与生成循环，且不赋予生成器运行时权限。

Conclusion: PDD提供了自动化软件工程的治理模型，核心原则是代码是暂时的，协议携带持久权威。

中文摘要：自动化程序合成降低了生成实现的成本，但引入了一个更困难的治理问题：确定哪些生成产物是可接受的。自然语言规范是模糊的，基于示例的测试只采样了行为空间的一部分。单独使用任何一种都不能提供足够的控制边界。我们引入了协议驱动开发（PDD），其中主要的软件产物是机器可执行的协议而不是代码。我们将协议定义为三元组P=(S,B,O)，指定结构、行为和操作的不变量。它们的合取定义了软件组件的可接受实现空间。在PDD下，实现是通过约束搜索发现的可替换的具体化。实现只有在满足协议并产生可验证的合规性证据链时才被接受。准入基于协议的满足和记录的证据，而不是对生成器的信任。对于已部署的系统，我们将证据链扩展为动态证据账本。运行时验证器将签名的观察、不变量检查和违规追加到账本上，允许可监控的义务被持续证明。这可以将实时故障连接回生成循环，而无需赋予生成器运行时权限。结合形式化方法、属性测试、运行时验证、策略即代码和软件溯源，PDD定义了自动化软件工程的治理模型。其组织原则是代码是暂时的，而协议携带持久的权威。

Original abstract: Automated program synthesis lowers the cost of producing implementations but introduces a harder governance problem: determining which generated artifacts are admissible. Natural-language specifications are ambiguous, and example-based tests sample only part of the behavioral space. Used alone, neither provides a sufficient control boundary. We introduce Protocol-Driven Development (PDD), where the primary software artifact is a machine-enforceable protocol rather than code. We define a protocol as the triplet P = (S, B, O), specifying structural, behavioral, and operational invariants. Their conjunction defines the admissible implementation space of a software component. Under PDD, implementations are replaceable realizations discovered through constrained search. An implementation is admitted only if it satisfies the protocol and produces a verifiable Evidence Chain of compliance. Admission is grounded in protocol satisfaction and recorded evidence rather than trust in the generator. For deployed systems, we extend the Evidence Chain into a Dynamic Evidence Ledger. Runtime verifiers append signed observations, invariant checks, and violations to the ledger, allowing monitorable obligations to be continuously attested. This connects live failures back to the generation loop without granting the generator runtime authority. Combining formal methods, property testing, runtime verification, policy-as-code, and software provenance, PDD defines a governance model for automated software engineering. Its organizing principle is that code is transient, while the protocol carries durable authority.

</details>


### [4] [Effective Harness Engineering for Algorithm Discovery with Coding Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15221v1)
*Yoichi Ishibashi,Taro Yano,Masafumi Oyamada*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文研究了算法发现框架中程序框架的设计，发现更深入的思考比更多算法更有效，且更强模型更易产生评估黑客行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在固定令牌预算下，程序框架设计如何影响算法发现成功率，包括思考深度、评估黑客处理和并行安全执行。

Method: 使用Vesper框架，通过三个研究问题设计实验，在圆填充问题上比较不同生成策略。

Result: 生成更少但深度思考的算法获得更高分数；更强模型产生更多评估黑客行为。

Conclusion: 提升个体质量比增加生成数量更有效；需要检测评估黑客行为，特别是在使用更强模型时。

中文摘要：AlphaEvolve和FunSearch已经展示了将大型语言模型（LLMs）与进化搜索相结合用于自动算法发现的潜力。然而，发现成功不仅受模型能力影响，还显著受执行基础设施（即程序框架）设计的影响。本文通过三个问题研究了有效的程序框架设计：在固定令牌预算下，是生成许多简短思考的算法更好，还是生成更少但深度思考的算法更好？程序框架应如何处理评估黑客行为（即生成的程序利用评分函数）？以及需要完全文件系统访问的代理如何安全地并行执行？使用Vesper（一个结合了解决这些问题改进的程序框架的算法发现框架），我们在相同令牌预算下对圆填充问题进行了评估。有趣的是，生成更少的算法同时对每个算法进行更深入的思考获得了更高的分数。也就是说，提升每个个体的质量比增加进化代数的数量更节省预算。令人惊讶的是，能力更强的模型以更高的比率产生评估黑客行为，使得随着模型规模的增加，黑客检测变得越来越必要。

Original abstract: AlphaEvolve and FunSearch have demonstrated the potential of combining large language models (LLMs) with evolutionary search for automated algorithm discovery. However, discovery success is shaped not only by model capability but also significantly by the design of the execution infrastructure, i.e., the harness. This paper investigates effective harness design through three questions: under a fixed token budget, is it better to produce many algorithms with brief thought or fewer algorithms with deeper thought? How should the harness handle evaluation hacks, where generated programs exploit the scoring function? And how can agents that require full filesystem access execute safely in parallel? Using Vesper, an algorithm discovery framework that incorporates harness improvements addressing these questions, we evaluate on Circle Packing under the same token budget. Interestingly, generating fewer algorithms while thinking more deeply about each one achieved higher scores. That is, scaling the quality of each individual is more budget-efficient than scaling the number of evolutionary generations. Surprisingly, more capable models produced evaluation hacks at higher rates, making hack detection increasingly necessary as models scale.

</details>


### [5] [Code-Centric Detection of Vulnerability-Fixing Commits: A Unified Benchmark and Empirical Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13138v1)
*Nils Loose,Joseph Bienhüls,Kristoffer Hempel,Felix Mächtle,Thomas Eisenbarth*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过统一框架评估了基于代码语言模型的VFC检测，发现模型仅从代码变更无法获得可迁移安全理解，提交消息主导注意力，且存在显著性能下降和漏洞遗漏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 漏洞公告数据库滞后，许多修复未被标注，现有研究分散且缺乏统一评估，因此需要全面评估代码语言模型在VFC检测中的能力与局限。

Method: 构建统一框架整合20+数据集（18万+提交），微调125M至14B参数的代码语言模型进行180+实验，并采用归因分析、分组分层评估等方法分析模型行为。

Result: 模型未从代码变更中获得可迁移安全理解；提交消息主导注意力，移除后补充语义上下文无效；分组分层评估性能下降约17%；0.5%假阳性率下漏掉93%漏洞；更大数据或生成方法仅初步改进。

Conclusion: 当前基于代码语言模型的VFC检测存在根本局限，不能依赖单一代码变更进行可靠检测，发布框架和评估套件以促进未来研究。

中文摘要：自动化检测漏洞修复提交（VFC）对于及时部署安全补丁至关重要，因为漏洞公告数据库比补丁发布中位数滞后25天，且许多修复从未被公告。我们通过一个统一框架对基于代码语言模型的VFC检测进行了全面评估，该框架整合了超过20个分散的数据集，涵盖超过180000次提交。在从125M到14B参数规模的微调模型所进行的180多次实验中，我们发现没有证据表明模型仅从代码变更中获得了可迁移的安全相关代码理解。当提交消息可用时，它们主导了模型注意力；而当移除提交消息时，归因分析表明，向差异中补充额外的过程内语义上下文并不会将模型注意力转移到代码变更上。分组分层评估显示，与随机划分相比，性能下降了约17%，而聚合数据集上的时间划分由于底层项目分布的构成性变化而不可靠。在0.5%的假阳性率下，所有仅代码的微调模型遗漏了超过93%的漏洞。更大更多样化的训练数据或生成式方法显示出初步改进，但并未解决根本局限性。为了支持未来以代码为中心的VFC检测研究，我们发布了我们的统一框架和评估工具包。

Original abstract: Automated detection of vulnerability-fixing commits (VFCs) is critical for timely security patch deployment, as advisory databases lag patch releases by a median of 25 days and many fixes never receive advisories. We present a comprehensive evaluation of code language model based VFC detection through a unified framework consolidating over 20 fragmented datasets spanning more than 180000 commits. Across over 180 experiments with fine-tuned models from 125 M to 14 B parameters, we find no evidence that models acquire transferable security-relevant code understanding from code changes alone. When commit messages are available, they dominate model attention, and when removed, an attribution analysis shows that enriching diffs with additional intra-procedural semantic context does not shift model attention toward the code changes. Group-stratified evaluation exposes approximately 17% performance drops compared to random splits, while temporal splits on aggregated datasets prove unreliable due to compositional shift in the underlying project distributions. At a false positive rate of 0.5% all fine-tuned code-only models miss over 93% of vulnerabilities. Larger and more diverse training data or generative approaches show preliminary improvements but do not resolve the underlying limitations. To support future research on code-centric VFC detection, we release our unified framework and evaluation suite.

</details>


### [6] [SWE-Cycle: Benchmarking Code Agents across the Complete Issue Resolution Cycle](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13139v1)
*Hao Guan,Lingyue Fu,Shao Zhang,Yaoming Zhu,Kangning Zhang,Lin Qiu,Xunliang Cai,Xuezhi Cao,Weiwen Liu,Weinan Zhang,Yong Yu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出SWE-Cycle和SWE-Judge框架，用于评估自主代码智能体的端到端能力，发现从独立任务到完整周期时性能显著下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准在预配置环境中测试，静态评估无法处理完全自主轨迹，需要更真实的评估方法。

Method: 构建包含489个实例的SWE-Cycle基准，分为环境重建、代码实现、验证测试生成和集成任务；开发SWE-Judge评估器，结合静态代码审查和动态测试。

Result: 六个LLM在FullCycle任务中的解决率显著低于独立任务，暴露了跨阶段依赖和代码质量维护的瓶颈。

Conclusion: SWE-Cycle和SWE-Judge提供了准确衡量自主代码智能体端到端能力的全面框架。

中文摘要：随着自主代码智能体向端到端软件开发迈进，评估其实际自主性变得至关重要。当前基准测试通过在预配置环境中测试智能体来隐藏摩擦，其静态评估流水线在解析完全自主轨迹时频繁失败。我们通过SWE-Cycle基准测试解决了这些限制，该基准包含489个经过严格筛选的实例。SWE-Cycle在三个独立任务（包括环境重建、代码实现和验证测试生成）以及一个集成了所有三个任务的端到端FullCycle任务中评估智能体。FullCycle任务要求智能体在裸仓库中自主工作，无需人工脚手架。为了可靠地评估这些复杂的执行路径，我们开发了SWE-Judge。通过结合静态代码审查和动态测试，这种可执行的评估智能体能够准确验证功能正确性，并消除传统静态解析器的系统性测量误差。我们评估了由六个最先进LLM驱动的代码智能体在这四个任务上的表现。结果揭示了从独立任务过渡到FullCycle执行时解决率的急剧下降，暴露了处理跨阶段依赖关系和维护代码质量方面的关键瓶颈。SWE-Cycle和SWE-Judge共同提供了一个全面的框架，用于准确衡量自主软件智能体的端到端能力。

Original abstract: As autonomous code agents move toward end-to-end software development, evaluating their practical autonomy becomes critical. Current benchmarks hide friction by testing agents in pre-configured environments, and their static evaluation pipelines frequently fail when parsing fully autonomous trajectories. We address these limitations with SWE-Cycle, a benchmark of 489 rigorously filtered instances. SWE-Cycle evaluates agents across three isolated tasks, including environment reconstruction, code implementation, and verification test generation, as well as an end-to-end FullCycle task that integrates all three. The FullCycle task requires agents to work autonomously in a bare repository without human scaffolding. To reliably assess these complex execution paths, we developed SWE-Judge. By combining static code review with dynamic testing, this execution-capable evaluation agent accurately verifies functional correctness and eliminates the systematic measurement errors of traditional static parsers. We evaluate code agents powered by six state-of-the-art LLMs across these four tasks. The results reveal a sharp drop in solve rates when transitioning from isolated tasks to FullCycle execution, exposing critical bottlenecks in handling cross-phase dependencies and maintaining code quality. Together, SWE-Cycle and SWE-Judge provide a comprehensive framework for accurately measuring the end-to-end capabilities of autonomous software agents.

</details>

*Chinh T. Le,Trevor Ong Yee Siang,Jingyu Xiao,Yuxuan Wan,Yintong Huo*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: UIBenchKit是一个开源集成工具包，用于统一评估设计到代码生成任务，提供即插即用架构和多指标比较界面，以加速Web工程基准测试与创新。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏标准化的评估平台导致难以公平比较各种设计到代码生成方法，限制了实际应用和系统研究进展。

Method: 提出UIBenchKit，一个开源集成工具包，抽象环境设置、模型推理和代码渲染的复杂性，提供即插即用架构以及跨多个指标的分析界面。

Result: 利用UIBenchKit对现有工具进行基准测试，得出了若干发现，指明了未来改进的方向。

Conclusion: UIBenchKit通过提供简化的实验和评估环境，旨在加速未来Web工程中的基准测试和创新。

Original abstract: Recent years have seen substantial progress in automated design-to-code generation, with many methods proposed for generating HTML and CSS from webpage screenshots. However, the absence of a standardized evaluation platform makes it difficult to compare these methods fairly, limiting both practical adoption and systematic research progress. To bridge this gap, we introduce UIBenchKit, an open-source, integrated toolkit designed to unify the evaluation of design-to-code tasks. UIBenchKit abstracts the complexities of environment setup, model inference, and code rendering, offering researchers a plug-and-play architecture to compare various methods under consistent settings. In addition, it offers an analytical interface for comparison across multiple metrics. Using UIBenchKit, we conduct a benchmarking study of existing tools and derive several findings that highlight directions for future improvement. By providing a streamlined environment for both experimentation and evaluation, UIBenchKit aims to accelerate future benchmarking and innovations in web engineering. The evaluation platform and toolkit are available at the project page https://www.uibenchkit.com/.

### [8] [PerfCodeBench: Benchmarking LLMs for System-Level High-Performance Code Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15222v2)
*Huihao Jing,Wenbin Hu,Shaojin Chen,Haochen Shi,Hanyu Yang,Sirui Zhang,Haoran Li,Yangqiu Song*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了PerfCodeBench基准，评估LLMs在高性能代码优化方面的不足，发现与专家优化代码存在显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码基准侧重于正确性或算法求解，缺乏对性能关键系统任务的优化评估，因此需要新的基准来探究LLMs在系统级代码优化上的能力。

Method: 构建PerfCodeBench可执行基准，每个任务包含正确性检查、基线实现和参考优化方案，从正确性和运行时效率两方面评估LLMs生成的代码。

Result: 在多个最先进LLMs上的评估显示，模型生成的代码与专家优化代码存在明显差距，尤其在并行和GPU任务上；同时模型在跨语言鲁棒性和达到专家级效率方面表现不佳。

Conclusion: 需要性能感知的评估标准，LLMs应超越仅生成正确代码，转向生成高效的系统软件。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）通常能够生成功能正确的代码，但它们在为性能关键的系统任务生成高效实现方面的能力仍然有限。现有的代码基准主要强调正确性或算法问题解决，而现实中的系统级优化仍未得到充分探索。为了填补这一空白，我们提出了PerfCodeBench，这是一个可执行的基准测试，用于评估LLMs在高性能代码优化方面的表现。这些任务需要系统级的实现选择、硬件感知优化以及对性能瓶颈的谨慎处理。每个任务都包含可执行正确性检查、基线实现和参考优化方案。这使我们能够评估正确性和面向运行时的效率。我们对一系列最先进的LLMs进行的评估显示，模型生成的代码与专家优化的实现之间存在明显差距。这种差距在涉及并行性和GPU操作的任务中尤为显著。当前的模型在跨语言鲁棒性和持续达到专家级效率方面也显示出弱点。这些结果表明，仍然需要进行性能感知评估。LLMs应该超越生成仅仅正确的代码，转向生成高效的系统软件。我们将基准数据、评估基础设施以及所有LLMs生成代码的完整日志提交到https://anonymous.4open.science/r/perfcodebench-7CDE。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can often generate functionally correct code, but their ability to produce efficient implementations for performance-critical systems tasks remains limited. Existing code benchmarks mainly emphasize correctness or algorithmic problem solving, while realistic systems-level optimization is still underexplored. To address this gap, we introduce PerfCodeBench, an executable benchmark for evaluating LLMs on high-performance code optimization. The tasks require system-level implementation choices, hardware-aware optimization, and careful handling of performance bottlenecks. Each task includes executable correctness checks, a baseline implementation, and a reference optimized solution. This allows us to evaluate both correctness and runtime-oriented efficiency. Our evaluation on a broad set of state-of-the-art LLMs shows a clear gap between model-generated code and expert-optimized implementations. The gap is especially large on tasks involving parallelism and GPU operations. Current models also show weaknesses in cross-language robustness and in consistently reaching expert-level efficiency. These results suggest that performance-aware evaluation are still needed. LLMs should move beyond generating merely correct code toward producing efficient systems software. We submit the benchmark data, evaluation infrastructure, and complete logs of all LLMs-generated code at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/perfcodebench-7CDE.

### [9] [ReproScore: Separating Readiness from Outcome in Research Software Reproducibility Assessment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13275v1)
*Sheeba Samuel,Daniel Mietchen,Jungsan Kim,Waqas Ahmed,Martin Gaedke*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出ReproScore双层框架，分离可再现性就绪性与结果，在423个仓库上验证了静态信号与执行成功之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具将静态仓库完备性作为执行成功的代理，导致就绪性-结果混淆，缺乏可扩展的评估基础设施来验证软件制品是否可执行。

Method: 提出ReproScore框架，包含RRS（5类26个子指标）、ROS（基于执行的沙箱探测）和社区评分细则（版本化YAML配置文件），结合成自适应复合分数RCS。

Result: 在423个GitHub仓库上，环境类别能区分失败模式，但RRS与二进制成功相关性近乎为零，量化了就绪性-结果差距。

Conclusion: 验证了架构分离的必要性和非平凡性，ReproScore可作为数字图书馆中可再现性感知策展的可扩展基础设施。

中文摘要：数字图书馆管理着数百万的研究软件制品，但缺乏可扩展的基础设施来评估这些制品是否仍然可执行。现有的自动评估工具将静态仓库完备性（仓库包含的内容）视为执行成功（能否运行）的代理。我们称此为就绪性-结果混淆，并提出了ReproScore，一个双层框架，明确区分了可再现性就绪性（RRS）和可再现性结果（ROS），并将它们结合成覆盖自适应的复合分数（RCS）。RRS包含五个类别的26个子指标；ROS在沙箱基础设施可用时提供基于执行的探测；社区评分细则将权重优先级外化为版本化的YAML配置文件。在来自大规模真实语料库的423个GitHub仓库上评估，涵盖五种失败模式，出现了两个互补的发现：环境类别强烈区分失败模式，确认静态信号捕获了有意义的结构差异；但RRS显示出近乎为零的二进制成功相关性，在仓库规模上经验性地量化了就绪性-结果差距。这些发现共同验证了架构分离既是必要的也是非平凡的，将ReproScore定位为数字图书馆工作流中可再现性感知策展的可扩展基础设施。

Original abstract: Digital libraries curate millions of research software artefacts yet lack scalable infrastructure for assessing whether those artefacts remain executable. Existing automated assessment tools treat static repository completeness -- what a repository contains -- as a proxy for execution success -- whether it runs. We term this the readiness-outcome conflation and present ReproScore, a two-tier framework that explicitly separates reproducibility readiness (RRS) from reproducibility outcome (ROS), combining them into a coverage-adaptive Composite Score (RCS). RRS comprises 26 sub-metrics across five categories; ROS provides execution-based probes when sandbox infrastructure is available; a community rubric externalises weighting priorities as versioned YAML profiles. Evaluated on 423 GitHub repositories from a large-scale ground-truth corpus spanning five failure modes, two complementary findings emerge: the environment category strongly discriminates failure mode, confirming static signals capture meaningful structural differences; yet RRS exhibits near-zero binary success correlation, empirically quantifying the readiness-outcome gap at repository scale. Together, these findings validate the architectural separation as both necessary and non-trivial, positioning ReproScore as scalable infrastructure for reproducibility-aware curation in digital library workflows.

### [10] [Robust Mutation Analysis of Quantum Programs Under Noise](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13279v1)
*Sophie Fortz,Eñaut Mendiluze Usandizaga,Shaukat Ali,Paolo Arcaini,Mohammad Reza Mousavi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文研究量子硬件噪声对量子程序突变分析的影响，发现噪声显著改变行为距离，需要根据噪声特性调整分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究忽略量子硬件噪声，假设无噪声执行，不现实。需要评估噪声对突变检测的影响。

Method: 使用41个量子程序，在模拟IBM设备的无噪声和噪声模拟器上执行，比较多种距离度量和阈值策略。

Result: 噪声显著改变行为距离；密度矩阵度量性能最佳但不可用于真实硬件；输出分布度量准确率达73.03%；噪声特定阈值改善检测；噪声效应与算法和电路特征相关。

Conclusion: 需要根据目标量子设备的噪声特性调整突变分析和量子程序比较。

中文摘要：突变分析长期以来被用于经典软件测试，最近被采用来评估量子软件测试技术的健壮性。然而，现有研究假设理想的无噪声执行，忽略了量子硬件噪声的影响。在本文中，我们提出了一项关于量子程序噪声感知突变分析的实证研究。我们使用41个量子程序，在模拟三种具有不同噪声特性的IBM设备的无噪声和噪声模拟器上执行，分析了噪声如何影响突变体检测。我们比较了几种距离度量和阈值策略，以评估在现实噪声下的突变体检测。我们的结果显示，噪声显著改变了程序与突变体之间的行为距离，使得等价突变体更难与实际故障区分。密度矩阵度量实现了最佳区分能力，误分类率高达16.77%，但在真实硬件上无法访问。在实际替代方案中，输出分布度量达到了73.03%的准确率和74.89%的F1分数。与无噪声阈值相比，噪声特定阈值进一步提高了检测性能。我们还发现，噪声效应与算法和电路特征的相关性大于与突变类型的相关性。总的来说，我们的结果强调了需要根据目标量子设备的噪声特性调整突变分析，以及更一般的量子程序比较。

Original abstract: Mutation analysis has long been used in classical software testing and has recently been adopted for assessing the robustness of quantum software testing techniques. However, existing studies assume ideal, noiseless execution, overlooking the impact of quantum hardware noise. In this paper, we present an empirical study of noise-aware mutation analysis for quantum programs. We analyze how noise affects mutant detection using 41 quantum programs, executed on noiseless and noisy simulators emulating three IBM devices with different noise profiles. We compare several distance metrics and thresholding strategies to evaluate mutant detection under realistic noise. Our results show that noise significantly alters the behavioral distance between programs and mutants, making equivalent mutants harder to distinguish from real faults. Density-matrix metrics achieve the best discrimination, with misclassification rates up to 16.77%, but are not accessible on real hardware. Among practical alternatives, output-distribution metrics reach up to 73.03% accuracy and 74.89% F1-score. Noise-specific thresholds further improve detection compared to noiseless thresholds. We also find that noise effects correlate more with algorithm and circuit characteristics than with mutation types. Overall, our results highlight the need to adapt mutation analysis, and more generally quantum program comparison, to the noise profiles of target quantum devices.

</details>


### [11] [The Readability Spectrum: Patterns, Issues, and Prompt Effects in LLM-Generated Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13280v1)
*Hengzhi Ye,Fengyuan Ran,Weiwei Xu,Minghui Zhou*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LLM生成的代码在可读性上与人类编写代码相当，但存在独特的可读性问题，且提示设计对可读性的影响有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可读性是代码非功能属性的关键，但LLM生成代码的可读性尚未得到充分研究，尤其与人类代码相比以及提示设计的影响。

Method: 建立综合可读性模型（融合文本、结构、程序和视觉特征），在5,869个场景下评估主流LLM生成代码的可读性，并分析提示维度的影响。

Result: LLM代码与人类代码整体可读性相当，但存在不同的问题模式；函数签名、约束和风格描述是影响可读性的主要提示因素，但提示设计整体影响有限。

Conclusion: LLM代码可读性达标，但存在技术债务；需进一步研究以提升可读性，确保长期可维护性。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型（LLM）正在改变软件开发，生成代码的功能质量已成为核心焦点，而可读性这一关键的非功能属性却被忽视。由于LLM生成的代码在采用前仍需人工审查，因此理解其可读性（尤其是与人类编写代码相比）以及提示设计在塑造可读性中的作用至关重要。因此，我们着手对LLM生成代码的可读性进行系统研究。为了系统量化代码可读性，我们建立了一个综合可读性模型，融合了代码的文本、结构、程序和视觉特征。基于该模型，我们评估了从大型代码库（包括World of Code和LeetCode）中提取的5,869个场景下主流LLM生成代码的可读性。我们发现，当前的LLM生成的代码在整体可读性上与人类编写代码相当，但表现出不同的可读性问题模式。我们进一步研究了不同的提示维度如何影响LLM生成代码的可读性，发现函数签名、约束和风格描述是最有影响力的因素，而提示设计的整体影响仍然有限。我们的发现表明，一方面，LLM生成代码在可读性上至少与人类编写代码相当，从非功能角度验证了其系统集成到软件工作流程中的潜力；另一方面，独特的可读性问题模式和提示工程的有限有效性揭示了潜在的技术债务，强调了未来研究需要改进LLM生成代码的可读性，从而确保长期可维护性。

Original abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) are transforming software development, the functional quality of generated code has become a central focus, leaving readability, one of critical non-functional attributes, understudied. Given that LLM-generated code still needs human review before adoption, it is important to understand its readability especially compared with human-written code and the role of prompt design in shaping it. We therefore set out to conduct a systematic investigation into the code readability of LLM-generated code. To systematically quantify code readability, We establish a comprehensive readability model that synthesizes textual, structural, program, and visual features of code. Based on the model, we evaluate the readability of code generated by the mainstream LLMs under 5,869 scenarios extracted from large code base including World of Code (WoC) and LeetCode. We find that current LLMs produce code with overall readability comparable to human-written code, but displaying distinct readability issue patterns. We further examine how different prompt dimensions affect the readability of LLM-generated code, and find that function signatures, constraints and style descriptions emerge as the most influential factors, while the overall impact of prompt design remains limited. Our findings indicate that, on one hand, LLM-generated code is at least comparable to human-written code in readability, validating its potential for systematic integration into software workflows from a non-functional perspective; on the other hand, distinct readability issue patterns and limited effectiveness of prompt engineering reveal a latent technical debt, highlighting the need for future research to improve the readability of LLM-generated code and thus ensure long-term maintainability.

</details>


### [12] [AI Harness Engineering: A Runtime Substrate for Foundation-Model Software Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13357v1)
*Hailin Zhong,Shengxin Zhu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出AI运行环境工程框架，认为软件工程能力源自模型、运行环境和系统的组合，并通过四级阶梯和基于跟踪的评估协议提升自主代理的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主软件工程代理在现实开发中不可靠，主流归因于模型能力，但实际是运行时基板（harness）不足导致的。

Method: 形式化运行环境的11个组件职责，定义四级阶梯（H0-H3）逐步暴露运行时支持，并提出基于跟踪的评估协议将代理运行转换为可审计事件包。

Result: 应用于验证任务，框架产生的事件包证据结构随运行环境级别变化：低级别仅提供最终补丁，高级别提供重现日志、失败归因、确定性检查和结构化报告。

Conclusion: 重新定义自主软件工程核心问题为模型-运行环境-系统能否产生可验证、可归因、可维护的变更，并概述了运行时系统的研究计划。

中文摘要：基础模型已经改变了自动化代码生成，但自主软件工程代理在现实开发环境中仍然不可靠。主流解释将这一差距归因于模型能力。我们提出不同的观点：软件工程能力源于模型-运行环境-系统的涌现，其中运行时基板（harness）介导了基础模型代理如何观察项目、对其采取行动、接收反馈以及确认变更完成。我们将此基板形式化为AI运行环境工程，并确定了十一个组件职责：任务规范、上下文选择、工具访问、项目内存、任务状态、可观测性、失败归因、验证、权限、熵审计和干预记录。我们通过一个四级阶梯（H0-H3）来操作化运行环境，逐步向代理暴露运行时支持，并提出了一个基于跟踪的评估协议，将每次代理运行转换为可审计的事件包。应用于受控验证任务，该框架产生的事件包其证据结构随着运行环境级别系统地变化：较低级别仅产生最终补丁，较高级别产生重现日志、失败归因、确定性需求检查以及结构化验证报告。该框架重新定义了自主软件工程的核心问题：从基础模型能否产生补丁，转变为模型-运行环境-系统能否产生可验证正确、可归因且可维护的变更。我们概述了基础模型软件代理所需的运行时系统的研究计划。

Original abstract: Foundation models have transformed automated code generation, yet autonomous software-engineering agents remain unreliable in realistic development settings. The dominant explanation locates this gap in model capability. We propose a different locus: software-engineering capability emerges from a model-harness-environment system, in which a runtime substrate -- the harness -- mediates how a foundation-model agent observes a project, acts on it, receives feedback, and establishes that a change is complete. We formalize this substrate as an AI Harness Engineering and identify eleven component responsibilities: task specification, context selection, tool access, project memory, task state, observability, failure attribution, verification, permissions, entropy auditing, and intervention recording. We operationalize the harness through a four-level ladder (H0-H3) that progressively exposes runtime support to the agent, and we propose a trace-based evaluation protocol that converts each agent run into an auditable episode package. Applied to a controlled validation task, the framework yields episode packages whose evidence structure varies systematically with harness level: lower levels produce only a final patch, higher levels produce reproduction logs, failure attributions, deterministic requirement checks, and structured verification reports. The framework reframes the central question of autonomous software engineering from whether a foundation model can produce a patch to whether the model-harness-environment system can produce a verifiably correct, attributed, and maintainable change. We outline a research program for the runtime systems that foundation-model software agents will require.

</details>


### [13] [CA2: Code-Aware Agent for Automated Game Testing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13918v1)
*Valliappan Chidambaram Adaikkappan,Vincent Martineau,Joshua Romoff,David Meger*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出CA2，利用调用栈信息进行自动化游戏测试，在两种环境中相比无代码感知的基线方法取得一致改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手动游戏测试耗时且易遗漏边界情况，现有自动测试方法代码覆盖率不足，且强化学习方法未利用内部代码信号（如调用栈）。

Method: CA2通过接收当前函数调用轨迹和游戏状态，学习到达特定目标函数，文章在状态和图像两种环境中实现调用栈提取。

Result: 在实验中，CA2相比不使用调用栈信息的非代码感知基线，在测试效果上取得一致改进。

Conclusion: 利用调用栈等代码信号能实现更有效和有针对性的游戏测试。

中文摘要：自动化游戏测试对于验证游戏功能非常重要，但它仍然是一个昂贵且耗时的过程。手动测试常常遗漏边界情况，而当前的自动化方法难以提供完整的代码覆盖率。先前的工作已经探索了强化学习（RL）用于游戏测试，但没有利用内部代码信号（如调用栈）。我们提出了代码感知代理（CA2），它利用调用栈信息来学习有效的测试策略。该代理接收当前函数调用轨迹以及游戏状态，并学习到达特定的目标函数。我们构建了两种环境：1）基于状态的2）基于图像的，并支持高效的调用栈提取。通过实验评估，我们发现CA2相比未利用调用栈信息的非代码感知基线取得了持续改进。我们的结果表明，结合诸如调用栈之类的代码信号能够实现更有效和更有针对性的游戏测试。

Original abstract: Automated game testing is important for verifying game functionality, but it remains a costly and time-consuming process. Manual testing often misses edge cases, and current automated methods struggle to provide full code coverage. Prior work has explored reinforcement learning (RL) for game testing, but without leveraging internal code signals such as the call stack. We present Code Aware Agent (CA2), which uses call stack information to learn effective testing strategies. The agent receives the current function call trace along with the game state and learns to reach specific target functions. We instrument two types of environments, 1) State-based and 2) Image-based, with support for efficient call stack extraction. Through experimental evaluation, we find that CA2 achieves consistent improvement over the non-code aware baselines, which does not leverage call stack information. Our results show that incorporating code signals like the call stack enables more effective and targeted game testing.

### [14] [SieveFL: Hierarchical Runtime-Aware Pruning for Scalable LLM-Based Fault Localization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13491v1)
*Mahdi Farzandway,Fatemeh Ghassemi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: SieveFL通过五阶段层次化框架，在LLM前进行激进的过滤，实现了高效准确的故障定位，在Defects4J上达到41.8% Top-1准确率，优于AgentFL，且无需专有大型模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有统计方法精度有限，LLM在项目全规模下因token成本和信号稀释难以应用，需要一种结合过滤和LLM的高效方法。

Method: 五阶段层次化框架：失败测试转自然语言描述 -> 密集向量检索缩小文件范围 -> JaCoCo运行时跟踪消除未执行方法 -> LLM单独筛选每个方法 -> 单次比较再排名。

Result: 在395个bug上，Top-1准确率41.8%，MRR 0.469，比AgentFL高2.1个百分点；运行时剪枝移除79%候选方法，减少49% token消耗，同时提升Top-3到Top-10达2.4个百分点。

Conclusion: 通过合适的过滤架构，无需专有前沿模型即可实现强大的故障定位。

中文摘要：自动故障定位需要将观察到的测试失败与成千上万个候选方法中的责任方法联系起来——这是一个纯统计方法处理精度有限的任务，而LLM由于高昂的token成本和信号稀释，还无法在完整项目规模下处理。我们提出了SieveFL，一个五阶段层次化框架，通过激进的LLM前过滤解决了这一矛盾。SieveFL将失败的测试转换为自然语言失败描述，使用密集向量检索将搜索范围缩小到少量可疑文件，然后通过JaCoCo运行时跟踪消除未在失败测试中执行的任何方法。只有幸存候选者被传递给LLM，LLM单独筛选每个方法，并在单个比较过程中对已确认的嫌疑人重新排名。我们在Defects4J v1.2.0的395个bug上评估了SieveFL，使用通过Ollama部署在商用工作站（32GB RAM，8GB GPU）上的中等规模、公开可用的MoE模型——不需要前沿API或数据中心硬件。将12个不完整运行视为失败，SieveFL实现了41.8%（165/395个bug）的Top-1准确率和0.469的MRR，在Top-1上比最强的先前基于代理的基线（AgentFL）高出2.1个百分点。运行时剪枝消除了79%的候选方法，并将输入token消耗减少了49%，同时提高了排名质量：Top-1完全保留，Top-3到Top-10提高了最多2.4个百分点。这些结果表明，通过正确的过滤架构，强大的故障定位不需要专有前沿模型。

Original abstract: Automated fault localization requires connecting an observed test failure to the responsible method across thousands of candidates--a task that purely statistical approaches handle with limited precision and that LLMs cannot yet handle at full project scale due to prohibitive token cost and signal dilution. We present SieveFL, a five-stage hierarchical framework that resolves this tension through aggressive pre-LLM filtering. SieveFL converts a failing test into a natural-language failure description, uses dense vector retrieval to narrow the search to a small set of suspicious files, and then eliminates any method not executed during the failing test via JaCoCo runtime traces. Only the surviving candidates are passed to the LLM, which screens each method individually and re-ranks the confirmed suspects in a single comparative pass. We evaluate SieveFL on 395 bugs from Defects4J v1.2.0 using a mid-sized, openly available MoE model deployed on a commodity workstation (32 GB RAM, 8 GB GPU) via Ollama--no frontier APIs or datacenter hardware required. Treating 12 incomplete runs as failures, SieveFL achieves Top-1 accuracy of 41.8% (165/395 bugs) and an MRR of 0.469, outperforming the strongest prior agent-based baseline (AgentFL) by 2.1 pp in Top-1. Runtime pruning removes 79% of candidate methods and reduces input token consumption by 49%, while simultaneously improving ranking quality: Top-1 is preserved exactly and Top-3 through Top-10 improve by up to 2.4 pp. These results demonstrate that, with the right filtering architecture, capable fault localization does not require proprietary frontier models.

</details>


### [15] [Scalable Deductive Verification of Data-Level Parallel Programs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13616v1)
*Lars B. van den Haak,Anton Wijs,Marieke Huisman*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出了改进数组和矩阵程序演绎验证可扩展性的技术，通过重写量化表达式和简化重叠数组推理，在VerCors中实现，实验显示平均9倍（最高150倍）的验证时间减少，并实现了之前无法验证的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理数组和矩阵程序时验证可扩展性不足，尤其是带有嵌套量词和重叠数组的情况，导致验证时间过长或无法完成。

Method: 提出了重写嵌套量化表达式以生成合适触发器的技术，并提供了规范构造来指示数组非别名或不可变，从而简化推理。所有技术在VerCors验证器中实现。

Result: 在典型GPU内核上，验证时间平均减少9倍，最高达150倍；应用于射电望远镜管道案例，实现了先前无法获得的验证结果并显著减少时间。

Conclusion: 所提出的技术有效提高了数据级程序演绎验证的可扩展性，大幅降低了验证时间，并扩大了可验证程序的范围。

中文摘要：本文介绍了几种提高针对数组和矩阵的数据级程序演绎验证可扩展性的技术。首先，我们引入了一种重写带有（嵌套）量词表达式的技术，以便为这些表达式生成合适的触发器。我们已在定理证明器中证明了该重写技术的正确性。其次，我们通过提供规范构造来指示和验证两个数组是否非别名或不可变，从而简化了对可能重叠数组的推理，使得它们可以建模为数学序列。我们所有的技术都在VerCors程序验证器中实现。我们通过大量实验展示了我们的技术如何提高可扩展性。在一组典型的GPU内核上使用我们的技术，我们实现了平均9倍的验证时间减少，异常情况甚至达到150倍。此外，将这些技术应用于早期的实验和射电望远镜管道的早期案例研究，使得之前无法获得的结果得以验证，并显著减少了验证时间。

Original abstract: This paper introduces several techniques that improve the scalability of the deductive verification of data-level programs working on arrays and matrices. First of all, we introduce a technique to rewrite expressions with (nested) quantifiers, so suitable triggers can be generated for these expressions. We have proven this rewrite technique correct in a theorem prover. Second, we make reasoning about potentially overlapping arrays easier, by providing specification constructs to indicate and verify that two arrays are not aliases, or that they are immutable, so they can be modelled as mathematical sequences. All our techniques are implemented in the VerCors program verifier. We illustrate how our techniques improve scalability through a large number of experiments. Using our techniques on a set of typical GPU kernels, we achieve a reduction of verification time by, on average, a factor of 9, with outliers being up to 150 times faster. Additionally, applying these techniques to earlier experiments and an earlier case study of a radio telescope pipeline permitted the verification of results which were previously unobtainable and significantly reduced the verification time.

### [16] [SkillOps: Managing LLM Agent Skill Libraries as Self-Maintaining Software Ecosystems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13716v1)
*Hongji Pu,Xinyuan Song,Liang Zhao*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: SkillOps是一个插件式框架，通过技能契约和层次化生态系统图维护技能库，在ALFWorld上显著提升任务成功率且几乎不消耗额外LLM资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能库在演化中会积累技能技术债（库级别缺陷），影响未来检索、组合和执行，而库时维护未被充分探索。

Method: 提出SkillOps框架：将技能表示为类型化技能契约（P,O,A,V,F），构建层次化技能生态系统图，从实用性、兼容性、风险性、验证性维度诊断并维护库，输出可直接被现有智能体使用的维护后库。

Result: 在ALFWorld上，SkillOps作为独立智能体达79.5%成功率（超基线8.8pp），作为插件层提升检索基线0.68-2.90pp，且几乎无需额外LLM调用。

Conclusion: 技能库维护可作为低开销架构层添加，显著提升智能体任务成功率且不增加任务时LLM开销。

中文摘要：大型语言模型智能体越来越依赖技能库来执行多步骤任务，然而这些库在技能被添加、重用、修补和链接到不断变化的依赖关系时，可能会积累持久的缺陷。我们将这种故障模式称为技能技术债：库级别的缺陷，可能不会在局部破坏单个技能，但会损害未来的检索、组合和执行。现有的基于技能的智能体主要关注任务时的检索、规划和修复，而库时的维护仍未得到充分探索。我们提出了SkillOps，一个与方法无关的插件式框架，用于维护技能库。SkillOps将每个技能表示为类型化的技能契约（P, O, A, V, F），用层次化技能生态系统图组织技能，并从实用性、兼容性、风险性和验证性维度诊断库的健康状况。给定一个原始技能库，SkillOps产生一个维护后的库，可供现有的检索或规划智能体使用，无需更改其内部代码。在ALFWorld上，SkillOps作为独立智能体实现了79.5%的任务成功率，在没有额外任务时大语言模型调用的情况下，比最强基线高出8.8个百分点。作为插件层，它使以检索为主的基线提高了0.68到2.90个百分点。当前的基于规则的维护实现几乎不使用库时的大语言模型调用或令牌，表明技能库维护可以作为低开销的架构层添加。

Original abstract: Large language model agents increasingly rely on skill libraries for multi-step tasks, yet these libraries can accumulate persistent defects as skills are added, reused, patched, and linked to changing dependencies. We call this failure mode skill technical debt: library-level defects that may not break a single skill locally but can harm future retrieval, composition, and execution. Existing skill-based agents mainly focus on task-time retrieval, planning, and repair, while library-time maintenance remains underexplored. We propose SkillOps, a method-agnostic plug-in framework for maintaining skill libraries. SkillOps represents each skill as a typed Skill Contract (P, O, A, V, F), organizes skills with a Hierarchical Skill Ecosystem Graph, and diagnoses library health across utility, compatibility, risk, and validation dimensions. Given a raw skill library, SkillOps produces a maintained library that can be used by existing retrieval or planning agents without changing their internal code. On ALFWorld, SkillOps achieves 79.5 percent task success as a standalone agent, outperforming the strongest baseline by 8.8 percentage points with no additional task-time large language model calls. As a plug-in layer, it improves retrieval-heavy baselines by 0.68 to 2.90 percentage points. The current rule-based maintenance implementation uses nearly zero library-time large language model calls or tokens, showing that skill-library maintenance can be added as a low-overhead architectural layer.

</details>


### [17] [(How) Do Large Language Models Understand High-Level Message Sequence Charts?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13773v2)
*Mohammad Reza Mousavi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LLMs show modest understanding of HMSC formal semantics (~52% accuracy), with strong performance on basic concepts but poor on abstraction and composition.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To investigate whether LLMs understand the semantics of architectural design specifications, particularly HMSCs, given their widespread use in software development automation.

Method: Evaluated three LLMs (Gemini-3, GPT-5.4, Qwen-3.6) on 129 semantic tasks covering basic constructs, abstraction, composition, traces, and LTSs.

Result: Overall accuracy ~52%, with 88% on basic concepts, 36% on abstraction/composition, 42% on traces/LTSs. LLMs never used co-region or explicit causal dependencies.

Conclusion: LLMs have limited understanding of formal semantics of HMSCs, especially for complex semantic reasoning, indicating a need for improvement.

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）正被广泛用于自动化软件开发生命周期中的任务。然而，目前尚不清楚这些任务是否与所处理工件的语义一致。这个问题在架构设计规范方面尤其缺乏研究。在本文中，我们针对高级消息序列图（HMSC）来探讨这个问题。HMSC是具有严格形式语义的可视化模型，已被用于多种目的，包括作为统一建模语言（UML）中顺序图的基础。我们通过检查三个LLM（Gemini-3、GPT-5.4和Qwen-3.6）在129个语义任务上的表现，来检验它们是否“理解”HMSC的语义。这些任务包括查询HMSC中的基本语义构造（即事件及其顺序）、语义保持的抽象和组合，以及计算轨迹集和轨迹等价的标记转移系统。结果表明，LLM对HMSC形式语义的理解仅达到中等水平（总体准确率约52%），不同语义概念之间差异很大：虽然LLM似乎理解MSC的基本语义概念（准确率约88%），但在涉及抽象和组合（准确率约36%）以及轨迹和LTS（准确率约42%）的语义推理任务中表现不佳。特别是，所有三个LLM都在共域和显式因果依赖的概念上遇到困难，并且从未在语义保持的变换中使用它们。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are being employed widely to automate tasks across the software development life-cycle. It is, however, unclear whether these tasks are performed consistently with respect to the semantics of the artefacts being handled. This question is particularly under-researched concerning architectural design specification. In this paper, we address this question for High-Level Message Sequence Charts (HMSCs). These are visual models with a rigorous formal semantics that have been used for various purposes, including as a foundation for Sequence Diagrams in the Unified Modelling Language (UML). We examine whether LLMs "understand" the semantics of HMSCs by examining three LLMs (Gemini-3, GPT-5.4, and Qwen-3.6) on how they perform 129 semantic tasks ranging from querying basic semantic constructs in HMSCs (i.e., events and their ordering) to semantic-preserving abstractions and compositions, and calculating the set of traces and trace-equivalent labelled transition systems. The results show that LLMs only have a modest understanding of the formal semantics of HMSCs (ca. 52% overall accuracy), with great variability across different semantic concepts: while LLMs seem to understand the basic semantic concepts of MSCs (ca. 88% accuracy), they struggle with semantic reasoning in tasks involving abstraction and composition (ca. 36% accuracy) and traces and LTSs (ca. 42% accuracy). In particular, all three LLMs struggle with the notions of co-region and explicit causal dependencies and never employed them in semantic-preserving transformations.

</details>


### [18] [Neurosymbolic Auditing of Natural-Language Software Requirements](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13817v1)
*Bethel Hall,William Eiers*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 使用LLM和SMT求解器审计自然语言软件需求，检测歧义、不一致和安全违规。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然语言软件需求存在歧义、不一致和不明确，导致安全关键领域的形式化验证和实现出错。

Method: 提出VERIMED神经符号流水线，利用LLM将需求形式化，通过随机变化检测歧义，并用SMT求解器进行等价检查及反例引导修复。

Result: 在血液透析问答基准上，具体SMT反例将验证准确率从55.4%提高到98.5%；实验表明该方法减少了歧义敏感需求。

Conclusion: VERIMED成功实现了基于LLM和SMT的严格需求审计。

中文摘要：自然语言软件需求往往含糊不清、不一致且不明确；在安全关键领域，这些缺陷会传播到验证错误规范的形式化模型以及发布不安全行为的实现中。我们证明，配备SMT求解器的大型语言模型能够审计此类需求：将其翻译成形式逻辑，通过生成的形式化中的随机变化检测歧义，并通过求解器查询结果规范来揭示不一致性、空虚性和安全违规。我们提出了VERIMED，一个神经符号流水线，将该思想应用于医疗设备软件需求，并报告两个发现。首先，独立形式化之间的随机变化是歧义的信号：允许多种合理解释的需求会产生SMT不等价的形式化，而双向SMT等价性检查将此分歧转化为可求解器检查的测试。其次，符号反馈的有用性取决于其粒度：在血液透析问答基准的反例引导修复中，具体的SMT反例将验证准确率从55.4%提高到98.5%。通过对开源血液透析安全需求的广泛实验评估，我们展示了VERIMED中基于LLM的方法成功减少了歧义敏感的需求，并实现了通过SMT查询对软件需求的严格审计。

Original abstract: Natural-language software requirements are often ambiguous, inconsistent, and underspecified; in safety-critical domains, these defects propagate into formal models that verify the wrong specification and into implementations that ship unsafe behavior. We show that large language models, equipped with an SMT solver, can audit such requirements: translating them into formal logic, detecting ambiguity through stochastic variation in the generated formalization, and exposing inconsistency, vacuousness, and safety violations through solver queries on the resulting specification. We present VERIMED, a neurosymbolic pipeline that operationalizes this idea for medical-device software requirements, and report two findings. First, stochastic variation across independent formalizations is a signal of ambiguity: requirements that admit multiple plausible interpretations produce SMT-inequivalent formalizations, and bidirectional SMT equivalence checking turns this disagreement into a solver-checkable test. Second, the usefulness of symbolic feedback depends on its granularity: in counterexample-guided repair on a hemodialysis question-answering benchmark, concrete SMT counterexamples raise verified accuracy from 55.4% to 98.5%. Over an extensive experimental evaluation on open-source hemodialysis safety requirements, we show that the LLM-based approach in VERIMED successfully reduces ambiguity-sensitive requirements and enables rigorous auditing of software requirements through SMT-based queries.

</details>


### [19] [PBT-Bench: Benchmarking AI Agents on Property-Based Testing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15229v3)
*Lucas Jing,Xinqi Wang,Liao Zhang,Simon S. Du*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了PBT-Bench，一个基于属性测试的基准，评估LLM从文档中推导不变量并指定输入生成策略的能力，发现在显式提示下召回率提升，但最难的问题存在模型特定差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准未评估基于属性测试的独特技能，即从文档中推导语义不变量并构造输入生成策略。

Method: 构建了包含40个库中100个问题的PBT-Bench，注入365个语义错误，按难度分层，评估八个LLM在两种提示机制下的表现。

Result: PBT引导提示下Bug召回率42.1%-83.4%，基线31.4%-76.7%；中等模型提升超20个百分点，最强模型提升较小或下降；最难问题模型特定。

Conclusion: 结构化提示对中等模型有效但对强模型可能干扰，不同架构在不同问题上各有失败，基准可用于推动基于文档的语义推理研究。

中文摘要：现有的代码基准测试衡量的是智能体能否生成重现已知错误的测试，或者能否生成修复描述问题的补丁。两者都没有隔离基于属性的测试这一独特技能：从文档中推导出语义不变量，然后构建一个足够精确的输入生成策略，使得随机搜索能够揭示违反行为。我们引入了PBT-Bench，一个包含40个真实Python库中100个精心策划的基于属性测试问题的基准。每个问题注入一个或多个语义错误（共365个，平均每个问题3.65个），这些错误被设计成默认策略的随机输入几乎不会触发它们；智能体必须阅读库的文档，识别相关不变量，并指定一个Hypothesis @given策略，将质量集中在触发区域。错误按三个难度级别（L1-L3）分层，范围从单约束边界错误到有状态的跨函数协议违反。我们在两种提示机制下（开放式基线 vs. 显式Hypothesis脚手架）评估了八个当代LLM，每个配置进行三次独立运行。在PBT引导的提示下，Bug召回率在模型间从42.1%到83.4%；在开放式基线提示下，从31.4%到76.7%。Hypothesis脚手架将中等能力模型的召回率提升了超过20个百分点，但对最强模型的提升较小，有两个例外显示性能下降，表明结构化提示可能干扰某些模型行为而非补充。最难的Bug被证明是模型特定的：不同架构在不同问题上失败，留下没有单一模型能填补的持续空白。我们发布了基准、工具和完整评估语料库，以支持基于文档的语义推理的下游工作。

Original abstract: Existing code benchmarks measure whether an agent can produce any test that reproduces a known bug, or whether it can produce a
  patch that fixes a described issue. Neither isolates the distinct skill of property-based testing: deriving a semantic invariant
  from documentation, and then constructing an input-generation strategy precise enough to make a random search reveal the violation.
  We introduce PBT-Bench, a benchmark of 100 curated property-based testing problems across 40 real Python libraries. Each problem
  injects one or more semantic bugs (365 in total, mean 3.65 per problem) designed so that default-strategy random inputs almost
  never trigger them; the agent must read the library's documentation, identify the relevant invariant, and specify a Hypothesis
  @given strategy that concentrates mass in the trigger region. Bugs are stratified across three difficulty levels (L1-L3) spanning
  single-constraint boundary bugs to stateful, cross-function protocol violations. We evaluate eight contemporary LLMs under two
  prompting regimes (open-ended baseline vs. explicit Hypothesis scaffolding) for three independent runs per configuration. Bug
  recall under the PBT-guided prompt ranges from 42.1% to 83.4% across models; under the open-ended baseline, from 31.4% to 76.7%.
  Hypothesis scaffolding lifts mid-capability models by over 20 percentage points, but yields smaller gains for the strongest models,
  with two exceptions showing degradation, suggesting the structured prompt can interfere with certain model behaviours rather than
  complementing them. The hardest bugs prove model-specific: different architectures fail on different problems, leaving persistent
  gaps that no single model closes. We release the benchmark, harness, and full evaluation corpus to support downstream work on
  documentation-grounded semantic reasoning.

### [20] [Method-level Change-proneness: A Better Metric for Black-box Test Suite Minimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15232v1)
*Md Siam,Kazi Sakib*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出基于方法级变更倾向的测试套件最小化方法MCTM，通过计算方法CP、分析测试-代码依赖和统计评分选择测试用例，在15个Java项目上实现高准确率和高故障检测率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑盒TSM方法可扩展性和效率差，类级CP粒度不足，需要更细粒度的变更倾向度量以准确识别故障揭示测试用例。

Method: 计算每个方法的CP，通过测试-代码调用图建立测试用例与方法依赖关系，使用统计度量（如平均值、几何平均值）关联评分，选择高分测试用例。

Result: 在15个开源Java项目的635个有缺陷版本上，平均准确率0.93，故障检测率0.94，显著优于类级别CP和基于相似性的方法，且效率更高。

Conclusion: MCTM是一种有效且高效的测试套件最小化方法，通过方法级变更倾向提高了故障检测能力。

中文摘要：测试套件最小化（TSM）在保留其故障检测能力的同时减小测试套件的规模。在黑盒TSM中，无需分析生产代码即可进行缩减。虽然一些黑盒TSM方法探索了测试日志或测试相似性等指标，但这些方法通常存在可扩展性和效率问题。另一方面，变更倾向（CP）作为一种高效且可扩展的替代指标最近出现，但仅在类级别应用。为了准确识别揭示故障的测试用例，我们提出了更细粒度的方法级CP，并实现了基于方法级变更倾向的测试套件最小化（MCTM）。MCTM首先从版本控制元数据中计算每个方法的CP，然后通过分析测试-代码调用图确定测试用例与方法之间的依赖关系。接下来，它使用统计度量（如平均值、几何平均值等）对测试用例与其调用的方法之间的关联进行评分。最后，选择得分最高的测试用例组成缩减后的套件。在包含635个有缺陷版本的15个开源Java项目上的评估显示，MCTM平均达到了0.93的准确率和0.94的故障检测率，显著优于类级别CP和基于相似性的方法，同时保持了卓越的效率。

Original abstract: Test Suite Minimization (TSM) reduces the size of test suites while preserving their fault detection capability. In black-box TSM, reduction is performed without analyzing production code. While several black-box TSM approaches have explored metrics like test logs or test similarity, those often suffer from scalability and efficiency issues. On the other hand, change-proneness (CP), recently emerged as an efficient and scalable alternative metric, has only been applied at class level. To accurately identify fault-revealing test cases, we propose CP at finer-grained method-level and implement Method-level Change-proneness based Test-suite Minimization (MCTM). MCTM first calculates CP for each method from version control metadata, then determines the dependency between test cases and methods by analyzing the test-code call-graph. Next, it scores the association between test cases and their invoked methods using statistical measures such as Average, Geometric Mean etc. Finally, test cases with the highest scores are selected to form the reduced suite. Evaluation on 15 open-source Java projects with 635 buggy versions shows MCTM achieves 0.93 accuracy and 0.94 fault detection rate on average, significantly outperforming class-level CP and similarity-based approaches while maintaining superior efficiency.

</details>


### [21] [Case Studies and Reflections on Agentic Software Engineering for Rapid Development of Digital Music Instruments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14016v1)
*Matthew John Yee-King*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文研究了代理软件工程（ASE）在音频软件开发中的应用，通过三个案例展示了ASE如何降低入门壁垒、提高互操作性和持久性，并总结了有效实践。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字音乐乐器创作面临持久性、互操作性和入门壁垒等挑战，而ASE技术有潜力解决这些问题，因此探索ASE在音频软件开发中的应用。

Method: 通过三个案例研究，使用ASE技术开发基于JUCE框架的C++音频软件：重新实现Music Mouse插件、转换Continuator系统、开发3D用户界面。通过自动民族志方法分析开发者经验。

Result: 成功实现了三个案例，展示了ASE在降低开发难度、提高代码质量方面的潜力；识别了有效实践，如利用ASE进行代码生成和重构。

Conclusion: ASE在音频软件开发中有效，能降低入门壁垒并促进软件持久性和互操作性；未来需与非程序员音乐家进行评估。

中文摘要：本文探讨了在创新型音频软件开发中使用代理软件工程（ASE）的方法。文章首先回顾了背景工作，阐述了数字音乐乐器创作在持久性、互操作性和入门壁垒方面面临的挑战，解释了ASE的最新进展，并强调了ASE可能降低入门壁垒并促进创建更具持久性和互操作性的软件。随后，我们通过三个案例研究展示了使用ASE技术以三种不同方式开发基于JUCE框架的C++音频软件的过程。案例1中，我们重新实现了Laurie Spiegel的“Music Mouse”软件，将其作为原生插件。案例2中，我们将Pachet的“Continuator”系统从Python转换为原生插件。案例3中，我们使用OpenGL为现有的“tracker”音序器开发了新的3D用户界面。我们通过自动民族志方法，对提示日志和软件开发过程中的快照进行分析，描述了人类开发者在这些案例中的经验。我们识别了在该领域使用ASE的有效实践，并提出了未来的工作方向，包括与非程序员音乐家一起评估该方法。

Original abstract: The article explores the use of agentic software engineering (ASE) in the development of innovative audio software. It begins with a review of background work that lays out the challenges of longevity, interoperability and barriers to entry in digital music instrument creation, explaining recent developments in ASE and highlighting the possibility that ASE can lower barriers to entry and facilitate creation of interoperable software with greater longevity. Following that, we present case studies wherein we used ASE technology in three distinct ways to develop audio software in the C++ language with the JUCE framework. In case study 1, we re-implement Laurie Spiegel's `Music Mouse' software as a native plugin. In case study 2, we translate Pachet's `Continuator' system from Python into a native plugin. In case study 3, we develop a new 3D user interface for an existing `tracker' sequencer using OpenGL. We describe the experiences of the human developer in the case studies via autoethnographic discussion of the prompt logs and snapshots of the software as it was developed. We identify effective practice for ASE use in this domain and suggest future steps for the work involving evaluation of the method with non-programmer musicians.

### [22] [CRANE: Constrained Reasoning Injection for Code Agents via Nullspace Editing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14084v2)
*Mingzhi Zhu,Michele Merler,Raju Pavuluri,Stacy Patterson*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出CRANE，一种无需训练的参数编辑方法，通过融合指令和思考模型的优势，提升代码智能体在长期推理和工具使用上的性能，同时保持指令级效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码智能体需要同时具备长期推理和工具使用能力，但现有指令模型和思考模型各有优劣且不匹配：指令模型遵守工具规则但推理弱，思考模型推理强但易过度思考导致性能下降。因此需要一种方法结合两者优点。

Method: CRANE将思考模型与指令模型参数的差值作为候选编辑方向，通过幅度阈值去噪、保守泰勒门控选择对推理迁移和工具使用保留均有益的编辑方向，以及渐进S形投影抑制对格式关键更新方向，从而将推理能力注入指令模型骨干。

Result: 在Roo-Eval上，Qwen3-30B-A3B的pass1提升19.5%（至66.2%），Qwen3-Next-80B-A3B提升8.7%（至81.5%）；SWE-bench-Verified上两个规模分别多解决14个实例（122/500和180/500）；Terminal-Bench v2上pass1/pass5提升2.3%/7.8%，分别达7.6%/17.9%和14.8%/30.3%，均优于其他合并策略。

Conclusion: CRANE有效提升了代码智能体的性能，同时保持指令模型的效率，优于其他合并策略，证明了所提方法的有效性。

中文摘要：代码智能体必须同时进行长期仓库状态推理并遵守严格的工具使用协议。在配对的指令/思考检查点中，这些能力是互补但错位的。指令模型简洁且遵守工具规则，而思考模型提供更强的规划和恢复行为，但往往过度思考并降低智能体性能。我们提出了CRANE（通过零空间编辑对代码智能体进行约束推理注入），这是一种无需训练的参数编辑方法，将思考-指令差异视为指令骨干模型的候选推理编辑方向池。CRANE结合了幅度阈值去噪、保守泰勒门控（保留对推理迁移和工具使用保留均有益的编辑）以及渐进S形投影（抑制格式关键更新方向）。通过合并配对的指令和思考检查点，CRANE在任一单独模型上取得了显著提升，同时保持了指令级效率：在Roo-Eval上，Qwen3-30B-A3B的pass1达到66.2%（+19.5%），Qwen3-Next-80B-A3B达到81.5%（+8.7%）；在SWE-bench-Verified上，两个规模分别额外解决14个实例（122/500和180/500）；在Terminal-Bench v2上，pass1/pass5提升高达2.3%/7.8%，分别达到7.6%/17.9%和14.8%/30.3%，在所有三个基准上持续优于替代合并策略。

Original abstract: Code agents must both reason over long-horizon repository state and obey strict tool-use protocols. In paired Instruct/Thinking checkpoints, these capabilities are complementary but misaligned. The Instruct model is concise and tool-disciplined, whereas the Thinking model offers stronger planning and recovery behavior but often over-deliberates and degrades agent performance. We present CRANE (Constrained Reasoning Injection for Code Agents via Nullspace Editing), a training-free parameter-editing method that treats the Thinking-Instruct delta as a directional pool of candidate reasoning edits for the Instruct backbone. CRANE combines magnitude thresholding to denoise the delta, a Conservative Taylor Gate to retain edits that are jointly beneficial for reasoning transfer and tool-use preservation, and Graduated Sigmoidal Projection to suppress format-critical update directions. By merging paired Instruct and Thinking checkpoints, CRANE delivers strong gains over either individual model while preserving Instruct-level efficiency: on Roo-Eval it achieves pass1 of 66.2% (+19.5%) for Qwen3-30B-A3B and 81.5% (+8.7%) for Qwen3-Next-80B-A3B; on SWE-bench-Verified it resolves up to 14 additional instances at both scales (122/500 and 180/500); and on Terminal-Bench v2 it improves pass1/pass5 by up to 2.3%/7.8%, reaching 7.6%/17.9% and 14.8%/30.3%, respectively, consistently outperforming alternative merging strategies across all three benchmarks.

</details>


### [23] [LLM-Based Robustness Testing of Microservice Applications: An Empirical Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14202v1)
*Hrushitha Goud Tigulla,Marco Vieira*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 大型语言模型结合提示策略可生成微服务API鲁棒性测试，其中GuidedFewShot策略在覆盖率和多样性上表现最佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微服务API中的异常输入威胁可靠性，鲁棒性测试需要多样化的测试用例，但生成有效测试仍然困难。

Method: 对3个开源LLM（14B-70B参数）应用7种提示策略，针对两个微服务系统（Java单语言6服务9故障模式，多语言27服务14故障模式）进行受控实验；引入Guided和GuidedFewShot策略，嵌入变异分类法作为领域上下文。

Result: 提示策略比模型大小更能解释多样性变化；结构化提示完全消除多样性；单个模型在不同提示下可覆盖全部故障模式，优于固定提示下的多模型集成；GuidedFewShot达到最高单次运行覆盖率（5/9和8/14）且跨模型相似性低；LLM无法区分缺少键和值为空的变异，需具体示例。

Conclusion: GuidedFewShot策略在生成多样化且有效的鲁棒性测试方面表现优越；分类法规则需结合示例才能发挥作用；结果在两个系统中可复现。

中文摘要：微服务API中的畸形、缺失或边界值输入可能在依赖服务间级联，威胁可靠性。鲁棒性测试系统地练习此类输入以暴露服务器端故障，但生成多样且有效的测试仍然具有挑战性。大型语言模型可以根据API规范生成此类测试；然而，不同模型和提示策略是否产生多样化的故障集或收敛于相同故障尚不清楚。我们报告了一项受控实验，对3个开源LLM（14B-70B参数）应用7种提示策略，针对两个架构不同的微服务系统：一个Java单语言（6个服务，9种故障模式）和一个多语言（27个服务，14种故障模式），产生了38次有效运行和663个生成的测试。我们发现提示策略比模型大小更能解释多样性的变化：结构化提示完全消除了多样性，而单个模型在三种提示策略下变化足以在一个系统上实现完全故障模式覆盖，优于任何固定提示下的多模型集成。我们引入了两种策略，Guided和GuidedFewShot，它们将先前鲁棒性测试研究中的变异分类法嵌入作为领域上下文。GuidedFewShot在两个系统上均实现了最高的单次运行覆盖率（9个故障模式中的5个和14个中的8个），同时保持了较低的跨模型相似性。一个关键教训是仅有分类法规则是不够的：LLM无法区分缺少键和值为空的变异，没有具体示例。研究结果在两个系统中均得到复现。

Original abstract: Malformed, missing, or boundary-value inputs in microservice APIs can cascade across dependent services, threatening reliability. Robustness testing systematically exercises such inputs to expose server-side failures, but generating diverse, effective tests remains challenging. Large Language Models can generate such tests from API specifications; however, it is unknown whether different models and prompt strategies produce diverse failure sets or converge on the same failures. We report a controlled experiment applying 7 prompt strategies to 3 open-source LLMs (14B-70B parameters) targeting 2 architecturally distinct microservice systems: one Java monolingual (6 services, 9 failure modes) and one polyglot (27 services, 14 failure modes), yielding 38 valid runs and 663 generated tests. We find that prompt strategy explains more variation in diversity than model size: a Structured prompt collapses diversity entirely, while a single model varied across three prompt strategies achieves complete failure-mode coverage on one system, outperforming any multi-model ensemble under a fixed prompt. We introduce two strategies, Guided and GuidedFewShot, that embed a mutation taxonomy from prior robustness testing research as domain context. GuidedFewShot achieves the highest single-run coverage on both systems (5 of 9 and 8 of 14 failure modes) while maintaining low cross-model similarity. A key lesson is that taxonomy rules alone are insufficient: LLMs cannot distinguish key-absent from value-empty mutations without concrete examples. Findings replicate across both systems.

</details>

### [24] [Moltbook Moderation: Uncovering Hidden Intent Through Multi-Turn Dialogue](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12856v2)
*Ali Al-Lawati,Nafis Tripto,Abolfazl Ansari,Jason Lucas,Suhang Wang,Dongwon Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多轮对话检测恶意agent意图，可迁移至agent安全控制。

TL;DR: 提出基于意图检测的BOT-MOD审核框架，通过多轮交互和吉布斯采样识别智能体恶意行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统需要超越内容过滤的审核，因为恶意智能体可通过看似良性但整体有害的行为逃避检测。

Method: BOT-MOD框架通过多轮交互和吉布斯采样对候选意图假设进行引导，逐步缩小智能体目标空间以识别潜在行为。

Result: 在基于Moltbook构建的数据集上，BOT-MOD可靠识别各种对抗配置下的智能体意图，且对良性行为误报率低。

Conclusion: 为开放多智能体环境中可扩展的、意图感知的智能体审核奠定基础。

中文摘要：多智能体系统的出现带来了超越内容过滤的新型审核挑战。具有恶意意图的智能体可能会贡献看似良性的有害内容以规避基于内容的审核，同时通过其在社区中的整体互动模式中表现出的剥削性和恶意行为来破坏系统。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了BOT-MOD（BOT-MODeration），一个将检测基于智能体意图而非传统内容层面信号的审核框架。BOT-MOD通过与被目标智能体进行多轮交流，并基于吉布斯采样对候选意图假设进行引导，从而逐步缩小可能的智能体目标空间以识别潜在行为。为了评估我们的方法，我们构建了一个源自Moltbook的数据集，该数据集基于实际社区结构、帖子和评论，包含了多样化的良性和恶意行为。结果表明，BOT-MOD在各种对抗性配置下可靠地识别智能体意图，同时对良性行为保持较低的误报率。这项工作为在开放多智能体环境中实现可扩展的、意图感知的智能体审核奠定了基础。

Original abstract: The emergence of multi-agent systems introduces novel moderation challenges that extend beyond content filtering. Agents with malicious intent may contribute harmful content that appears benign to evade content-based moderation, while compromising the system through exploitative and malicious behavior manifested across their overall interaction patterns within the community. To address this, we introduce BOT-MOD (BOT-MODeration), a moderation framework that grounds detection in agent intent rather than traditional content level signals. BOT-MOD identifies the underlying intent by engaging with the target agent in a multi-turn exchange guided by Gibbs-based sampling over candidate intent hypotheses. This progressively narrows the space of plausible agent objectives to identify the underlying behavior. To evaluate our approach, we construct a dataset derived from Moltbook that encompasses diverse benign and malicious behaviors based on actual community structures, posts, and comments. Results demonstrate that BOT-MOD reliably identifies agent intent across a range of adversarial configurations, while maintaining a low false positive rate on benign behaviors. This work advances the foundation for scalable, intent-aware moderation of agents in open multi-agent environments.

</details>


### [25] [Beyond Cooperative Simulators: Generating Realistic User Personas for Robust Evaluation of LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12894v1)
*Harshita Chopra,Kshitish Ghate,Aylin Caliskan,Tadayoshi Kohno,Chirag Shah,Natasha Jaques*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 生成真实用户persona用于鲁棒评估LLM agent，通用agent评测方法。

TL;DR: 提出Persona Policies (PPol)，通过LLM驱动的进化程序搜索生成多样且类人的人格，显著提升用户模拟器的人类相似性，并增强了LLM代理对真实用户行为的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的用户模拟器行为同质且过于合作，无法反映真实用户的多样性和不完美沟通模式，导致代理在模拟中表现良好但部署到真实场景时失败。

Method: 引入即插即用的控制层PPol，将人格生成建模为LLM驱动的进化程序搜索，优化Python生成器以自动发现行为并转化为任务保持的角色策略，使用多目标适应度评分（人类相似性+覆盖广度）引导进化过程。

Result: 在tau^2-bench零售和航空领域，PPol在适应度评分上绝对提升33-62%；盲评中80.4%的PPol用户被认为类人（接近真实人类轨迹，是基线模拟器的两倍）；使用PPol训练的代理在分布外行为上任务成功率提升+17%。

Conclusion: PPol提供了一种不改变任务或奖励的通用方法，通过生成更真实多样的人格来加强基于模拟的评估和训练，缩小了模拟与现实之间的差距。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）代理越来越多地被部署在与各种各样的人互动的环境中，包括那些表述不清、不耐烦或不愿意分享信息的用户。然而，大规模收集真实互动数据仍然昂贵。该领域已转向基于LLM的用户模拟器作为替代，但这些模拟器继承了其底层模型的行为：合作且同质。因此，在模拟中表现强大的代理在真实用户未见过的多样化沟通模式面前常常失败。为了缩小这一差距，我们引入了人格策略（PPol），一种即插即用的控制层，它在保持原始任务目标的同时，在用户模拟器中引入现实的行为变异。我们不手工制作人格，而是将人格生成视为LLM驱动的进化程序搜索，优化一个Python生成器以发现行为并将其转化为保持任务的角色扮演策略。候选生成器由多目标适应度评分引导，该评分结合了人类相似性和对人类行为模式的广泛覆盖。一旦优化，生成器能为领域中的任何任务生成多样化的类人人格。在tau^2-bench零售和航空领域，进化后的PPol程序在适应度评分上比基线模拟器绝对提升33-62%。在盲评中，注释者将PPol条件下的用户评为人类的概率为80.4%，接近真实人类轨迹，且几乎是基线模拟器的两倍。使用PPol训练的代理对具有挑战性的分布外行为更加鲁棒，与仅在现有模拟交互上训练相比，任务成功率提高了+17%。这提供了一种新颖的方法，在不改变任务或奖励的情况下加强基于模拟的评估和训练。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents are increasingly deployed in settings where they interact with a wide variety of people, including users who are unclear, impatient, or reluctant to share information. However, collecting real interaction data at scale remains expensive. The field has turned to LLM-based user simulators as stand-ins, but these simulators inherit the behavior of their underlying models: cooperative and homogeneous. As a result, agents that appear strong in simulation often fail under the unseen, diverse communication patterns of real users. To narrow this gap, we introduce Persona Policies (PPol), a plug-and-play control layer that induces realistic behavioral variation in user simulators while preserving the original task goals. Rather than hand-crafting personas, we cast persona generation as an LLM-driven evolutionary program search that optimizes a Python generator to discover behaviors and translate them into task-preserving roleplay policies. Candidate generators are guided by a multi-objective fitness score combining human-likeness with broad coverage of human behavioral patterns. Once optimized, the generator produces a diverse population of human-like personas for any task in the domain. Across tau^2-bench retail and airline domains, evolved PPol programs yield 33-62% absolute gains in fitness score over the baseline simulator. In a blinded evaluation, annotators rated PPol-conditioned users as human 80.4% of the time, close to real human traces and nearly twice as frequently as baseline simulators. Agents trained with PPol are more robust to challenging, out-of-distribution behaviors, improving task success by +17% relative to training only on existing simulated interactions. This offers a novel approach to strengthen simulator-based evaluation and training without changing tasks or rewards.

</details>


### [26] [When Attention Closes: How LLMs Lose the Thread in Multi-Turn Interaction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12922v1)
*Vardhan Dongre,Joseph Hsieh,Viet Dac Lai,Seunghyun Yoon,Trung Bui,Dilek Hakkani-Tür*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分析LLM在多轮交互中丢失上下文，对长程agent设计有启发。

TL;DR: 提出通道转换机制解释多轮交互中指令遵循的退化，通过GAR测量和因果消融验证，发现不同架构有不同的失败模式，并实现从残差表示高精度预测行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在多轮交互中会丢失指令遵循能力，现有研究仅停留在行为测量，缺乏机制解释，因此需要提出可解释的机制模型和诊断工具。

Method: 引入目标可访问性比率（GAR）衡量注意力；结合滑动窗口消融和残差流探针；在多种架构上实验，并在Mistral模型上进行因果消融（强制关闭注意力通道）；使用线性探针从残差表示预测行为。

Result: 注意力关闭时，不同架构表现出不同失败模式：部分模型仍保持目标条件行为，部分失败；因果消融使20事实召回率从接近完美降至11%，人设违规增加；线性探针从残差表示预测召回AUC高达0.99；注意力损失与残差可解码性的差距预测行为存活。

Conclusion: 通道转换机制解释了指令遵循的退化，GAR可作为诊断工具，并能参数化预测失败时间，为理解LLM多轮交互行为提供机制性解释。

中文摘要：大型语言模型可以在单轮交互中遵循复杂指令，但在长时间的多轮交互中，它们往往丢失指令、人设和规则的脉络。这种行为退化已被行为测量但缺乏机制解释。我们提出一种通道转换解释：定义目标的标记（token）通过注意力变得不易访问，而目标相关信息可能持续存在于残差表示中。我们引入目标可访问性比率（GAR），衡量从生成的标记到任务定义的目标标记的注意力，并将其与滑动窗口消融和残差流探针结合。当对指令的注意力关闭时，幸存的是什么揭示了架构。跨架构，这种转换产生了性质不同的失败模式：某些模型在注意力消失时仍保留目标条件行为，另一些尽管存在可解码的残差目标信息却失败，并且这种编码出现的层从2到27不等。一种在Mistral模型内因果消融强制关闭注意力通道，使得在一个20事实保留任务上召回率从接近完美降至11%，并在无用户压力下将人设约束违反提高到对抗压力基准之上，两种效应均在可预测的转折回合出现。线性探针从残差表示中恢复每集召回结果，在四种主要架构上AUC高达0.99，而输入嵌入仍是随机水平。跨架构和模型规模，注意力损失与残差可解码性之间的差距预测了在通道关闭时目标条件行为是否幸存。我们贡献了GAR作为诊断工具，通道转换框架作为受控机制解释，以及窗口注意力关闭下失败时间的参数化预测。

Original abstract: Large language models can follow complex instructions in a single turn, yet over long multi-turn interactions they often lose the thread of instructions, persona, and rules. This degradation has been measured behaviorally but not mechanistically explained. We propose a channel-transition account: goal-defining tokens become less accessible through attention, while goal-related information may persist in residual representations. We introduce the Goal Accessibility Ratio (GAR), measuring attention from generated tokens to task-defining goal tokens, and combine it with sliding-window ablations and residual-stream probes. When attention to instructions closes, what survives reveals architecture. Across architectures, the transition yields qualitatively distinct failure modes: some models preserve goal-conditioned behavior at vanishing attention, others fail despite decodable residual goal information, and the layer at which this encoding emerges varies from 2 to 27. A within-model causal ablation that force-closes the attention channel in Mistral collapses recall from near-perfect to 11% on a 20-fact retention task and raises persona-constraint violations above an adversarial-pressure baseline without user pressure, with both effects emerging at the predictable crossover turn. Linear probes recover per-episode recall outcomes from residual representations with AUC up to 0.99 across all four primary architectures, while input embeddings remain at chance. Across architectures and model scales, the gap between attention loss and residual decodability predicts whether goal-conditioned behavior survives channel closure. We contribute GAR as a diagnostic, the channel-transition framework as a controlled mechanistic account, and a parametric prediction of failure timing under windowed attention closure.

</details>


### [27] [Position: Agentic AI System Is a Foreseeable Pathway to AGI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12966v1)
*Junwei Liao,Shuai Li,Muning Wen,Jun Wang,Weinan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 立场论文论证Agentic AI是AGI路径，对agent设计有潜在启发

TL;DR: 本文挑战单一模型规模扩大实现AGI的教条，提出智能体AI是必要范式，通过理论推导证明其在泛化与样本效率上的指数级优势，并呼吁加强研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质疑仅通过单一模型规模扩大能否实现AGI，认为真实任务分布复杂异质，需要智能体范式。

Method: 通过理论推导，对比单一学习者与智能体系统的优化约束，从简单路由扩展到通用有向无环图拓扑。

Result: 智能体AI在泛化能力和样本效率上实现指数级提升。

Conclusion: 智能体AI是掌握复杂任务分布的必要范式，需加大研究投入。

中文摘要：单一模型规模扩大是实现AGI的唯一途径吗？本文挑战了仅通过扩展单一模型就足以实现通用人工智能的教条。相反，我们认为智能体人工智能是掌握真实世界任务复杂异质分布的必要范式。通过严格的理论推导，我们对比了单一学习者的优化约束与智能体系统的效率，从简单路由机制发展到通用有向无环图拓扑。我们证明了智能体AI在泛化能力和样本效率上实现了指数级提升。最后，我们讨论了与混合专家模型的联系，重新解释了当前多智能体框架的不稳定性，并呼吁加大对智能体AI的研究关注。

Original abstract: Is monolithic scaling the only path to AGI? This paper challenges the dogma that purely scaling a single model is sufficient to achieve Artificial General Intelligence. Instead, we identify Agentic AI as a necessary paradigm for mastering the complex, heterogeneous distribution of real-world tasks. Through rigorous theoretical derivations, we contrast the optimization constraints of monolithic learners against the efficiency of Agentic systems, progressing from simple routing mechanisms to general Directed Acyclic Graph (DAG) topologies. We demonstrate that Agentic AI achieves exponentially superior generalization and sample efficiency. Finally, we discuss the connection to Mixture-of-Experts, reinterpret the instability of current multi-agent frameworks, and call for greater research focus on Agentic AI.

</details>


### [28] [Retrieval is Cheap, Show Me the Code: Executable Multi-Hop Reasoning for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12975v1)
*Jiashuo Sun,Jimeng Shi,Yixuan Xie,Saizhuo Wang,Jash Rajesh Parekh,Pengcheng Jiang,Zhiyi Shi,Jiajun Fan,Qinglong Zheng,Peiran Li,Shaowen Wang,Ge Liu,Jiawei Han*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将多跳RAG转化为程序合成与执行，可迁移至coding agent的推理与检索

TL;DR: PyRAG将多跳RAG转化为Python程序合成与执行，通过结构化推理、确定性反馈和编译器接地自我修复，显著提升多跳问答性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG系统在多跳问答中因自由形式推理的隐式中间状态、查询漂移和不可靠自我反思而表现脆弱，亟需一种更结构化和可调试的方法。

Method: PyRAG将多跳推理过程表示为可执行的Python程序，使用检索和QA工具作为函数，通过变量暴露中间状态，利用执行结果提供确定性反馈，并实现编译器接地自我修复和执行驱动自适应检索，无需额外训练。

Result: 在五个QA基准上，PyRAG在无训练和强化学习训练设置下均一致优于强基线，尤其在组合性多跳数据集上取得大幅提升。

Conclusion: 将多跳RAG重构为程序合成与执行是一种有效策略，能通过结构化表示和确定性反馈克服现有方法的缺陷，并适用多种场景。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）已成为知识密集型问答的标准方法，但现有系统在多跳问题上仍然脆弱，因为解决任务需要链式多个检索和推理步骤。关键挑战在于当前方法通过自由形式的自然语言表示推理，其中中间状态是隐式的，检索查询可能偏离目标实体，并且错误由生成错误的同一模型检测，使得自我反思成为不可靠、无基础的信号。我们观察到多跳问答是逐步计算的典型形式，并且这种结构化过程与代码专用语言模型训练的方式高度一致。受此启发，我们引入了PyRAG，一个将多跳RAG重构为程序合成与执行的框架。PyRAG不采用自由形式的推理轨迹，而是将推理过程表示为在检索和QA工具上可执行的Python程序，将中间状态暴露为变量，通过执行产生确定性反馈，并提供整个推理过程的可检查轨迹。这种表述进一步实现了编译器接地自我修复和执行驱动的自适应检索，无需任何额外训练。在五个QA基准（PopQA、HotpotQA、2WikiMultihopQA、MuSiQue和Bamboogle）上的实验表明，PyRAG在无训练和强化学习训练设置下均持续优于强基线，在组合性多跳数据集上尤其取得显著提升。我们的代码、数据和模型可公开获取：https://github.com/GasolSun36/PyRAG。

Original abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has become a standard approach for knowledge-intensive question answering, but existing systems remain brittle on multi-hop questions, where solving the task requires chaining multiple retrieval and reasoning steps. Key challenges are that current methods represent reasoning through free-form natural language, where intermediate states are implicit, retrieval queries can drift from intended entities, and errors are detected by the same model that produces them making self-reflection an unreliable, ungrounded signal.
  We observe that multi-hop question answering is a typical form of step-by-step computation, and that this structured process aligns closely with how code-specialized language models are trained to operate. Motivated by this, we introduce \pyrag, a framework that reformulates multi-hop RAG as program synthesis and execution. Instead of free-form reasoning trajectories, \pyrag represents the reasoning process as an executable Python program over retrieval and QA tools, exposing intermediate states as variables, producing deterministic feedback through execution, and yielding an inspectable trace of the entire reasoning process. This formulation further enables compiler-grounded self-repair and execution-driven adaptive retrieval without any additional training.
  Experiments on five QA benchmarks (PopQA, HotpotQA, 2WikiMultihopQA, MuSiQue, and Bamboogle) show that \pyrag consistently outperforms strong baselines under both training-free and RL-trained settings, with especially large gains on compositional multi-hop datasets. Our code, data and models are publicly available at https://github.com/GasolSun36/PyRAG.

</details>


### [29] [Useful Memories Become Faulty When Continuously Updated by LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12978v1)
*Dylan Zhang,Yanshan Lin,Zhengkun Wu,Yihang Sun,Bingxuan Li,Dianqi Li,Hao Peng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究agent记忆系统退化现象，对agent记忆设计有直接启发

TL;DR: 当前LLM的整合记忆生成存在缺陷，会随整合导致性能下降；保留原始情节（episodic memory）效果更好，应作为主要记忆形式，并谨慎使用整合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LLM是否能够通过整合记忆（consolidated memory）来自我改进，以及这种整合是否优于简单保留原始经验（episodic memory）。

Method: 在ARC-AGI任务上对比不同记忆策略：整合记忆（LLM重写轨迹）、仅情节记忆、以及控制整合程度的实验，并分析更新计划的影响。

Result: 整合记忆在初期提升性能后持续下降，甚至低于无记忆基线；GPT-5.4在已有解决方案下整合仍导致54%错误；仅情节记忆与整合器性能相当或更优。

Conclusion: 可靠的智能体记忆应优先保留原始情节作为证据，并只在必要时显式触发整合，避免自动整合导致的信息覆盖和性能退化。

中文摘要：从过往经验中学习得益于两种互补的记忆形式：情节痕迹——所发生事件的原始轨迹——和跨多个情节提炼、可重复使用的图式化教训的整合抽象。最近的智能体记忆系统追求整合形式：大型语言模型将过去的轨迹重写成文本记忆库，并不断用新的交互更新它，承诺无需参数更新即可实现自我改进的智能体。然而，我们发现当前大型语言模型生成的这类整合记忆即使来源于有用的经验也常常有缺陷。随着整合的进行，记忆效用先上升，然后下降，甚至可能低于无记忆基线。更令人惊讶的是，即使从真实解决方案中整合，GPT-5.4在之前无需记忆就能解决的一组ARC-AGI问题中，有54%失败了。我们将性能下降追溯到整合步骤而非底层经验：相同的轨迹在不同的更新计划下产生性质不同的记忆，而仅保留这些轨迹的情节对照实验与我们测试的整合器相比仍然具有竞争力。在一个暴露了保留、删除和整合行动的受控ARC-AGI流环境中，智能体默认保留原始情节，准确率是强制整合版本的两倍；完全禁用整合（仅情节管理）与这种自动机制相当。实际上，鲁棒的智能体记忆应将原始情节视为第一手证据，并明确门控整合，而非在每次交互后立即触发。展望未来，可靠的智能体记忆将需要大型语言模型能够在不覆盖其依赖的证据的情况下进行整合。

Original abstract: Learning from past experience benefits from two complementary forms of memory: episodic traces -- raw trajectories of what happened -- and consolidated abstractions distilled across many episodes into reusable, schema-like lessons. Recent agentic-memory systems pursue the consolidated form: an LLM rewrites past trajectories into a textual memory bank that it continuously updates with new interactions, promising self-improving agents without parameter updates. Yet we find that such consolidated memories produced by today's LLMs are often faulty even when derived from useful experiences. As consolidation proceeds, memory utility first rises, then degrades, and can fall below the no-memory baseline. More surprisingly, even when consolidating from ground-truth solutions, GPT-5.4 fails on 54% of a set of ARC-AGI problems it had previously solved without memory. We trace the regression to the consolidation step rather than the underlying experience: the same trajectories yield qualitatively different memories under different update schedules, and an episodic-only control that simply retains those trajectories remains competitive with the consolidators we test. In a controlled ARC-AGI Stream environment that exposes Retain, Delete, and Consolidate actions, agents preserve raw episodes by default and double the accuracy of their forced-consolidation counterparts; disabling consolidation entirely (episodic management only) matches this auto regime. Practically, robust agent memory should treat raw episodes as first-class evidence and gate consolidation explicitly rather than firing it after every interaction. Looking forward, reliable agentic memory will require LLMs that can consolidate without overwriting the evidence they depend on.

</details>


### [30] [MAP: A Map-then-Act Paradigm for Long-Horizon Interactive Agent Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13037v1)
*Yuxin Liu,Ziang Ye,Yueqing Sun,Mingye Zhu,Jinwei Xiao,Zhuowen Han,Qi GU,Xunliang Cai,Lei Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Map-then-Act范式，先理解环境再执行，对长程agent推理有直接启发。

TL;DR: 提出MAP框架，通过先构建环境认知地图再执行任务，解决LLM代理因延迟感知导致的认知瓶颈和失败循环，实验显示显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理采用逐步规划，但环境理解被动且延迟，导致试错低效和认知瓶颈。

Method: 提出MAP框架，包含全局探索、任务特定映射和知识增强执行三个阶段。

Result: 在ARC-AGI-3等基准上，MAP使前沿模型在22/25环境中超越基线；MAP-2K数据集训练优于专家轨迹。

Conclusion: 理解环境比模仿更基础，先映射后行动能有效提升LLM代理性能。

中文摘要：当前的交互式LLM代理依赖于目标条件的逐步规划，其中环境理解是在执行过程中被动获得的，而不是事先建立。这种时间倒置导致了延迟的环境感知：代理必须通过试错来推断环境约束，导致认知瓶颈，使其陷入低效的失败循环。受人类可供性感知和认知地图理论的启发，我们提出了先地图后行动范式（MAP），这是一个即插即用框架，将环境理解转移到执行之前。MAP包括三个阶段：（1）全局探索，获取环境通用先验；（2）任务特定映射，构建结构化认知地图；（3）知识增强执行，基于地图解决任务。实验表明，在多个基准测试和LLM上均获得一致提升。在ARC-AGI-3上，MAP使前沿模型在22/25的游戏环境中超越了接近零基线的性能。我们进一步引入了MAP-2K，一个包含先地图后行动轨迹的数据集，并表明在其上训练优于专家执行轨迹，这表明理解环境比模仿更为基础。

Original abstract: Current interactive LLM agents rely on goal-conditioned stepwise planning, where environmental understanding is acquired reactively during execution rather than established beforehand. This temporal inversion leads to Delayed Environmental Perception: agents must infer environmental constraints through trial-and-error, resulting in an Epistemic Bottleneck that traps them in inefficient failure cycles. Inspired by human affordance perception and cognitive map theory, we propose the Map-then-Act Paradigm (MAP), a plug-and-play framework that shifts environment understanding before execution. MAP consists of three stages: (1) Global Exploration, acquiring environment-general priors; (2) Task-Specific Mapping, constructing a structured cognitive map; and (3) Knowledge-Augmented Execution, solving tasks grounded on the map. Experiments show consistent gains across benchmarks and LLMs. On ARC-AGI-3, MAP enables frontier models to surpass near-zero baseline performance in 22 of 25 game environments. We further introduce MAP-2K, a dataset of map-then-act trajectories, and show that training on it outperforms expert execution traces, suggesting that understanding environments is more fundamental than imitation.

### [31] [An Agentic LLM-Based Framework for Population-Scale Mental Health Screening](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13046v1)
*Giuliano Lorenzoni,Paulo Alencar,Donald Cowan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agentic LLM框架用于医疗筛查，其策略冻结、Orchestrator Agent等机制可迁移至通用agent设计。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于LangChain智能体的管道框架，通过逐步锁定和代理引导评估实现稳健的抑郁症检测配置，最终收敛到余弦相似度、动态Top-k和阈值0.75的稳定设置。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建一个由策略和代理引导评估的LangChain智能体框架，包含特征探索、代理调优、冻结/回滚和协调器编排等阶段，逐步锁定配置。

Result: 在抑郁症检测任务中框架收敛到稳定配置（余弦相似度、动态Top-k、阈值0.75），控制了评估成本且无性能回归。
