中文摘要：心理健康障碍影响着全球数百万人，医疗系统日益被来自电子病历、远程医疗平台和群体筛查项目的临床数据量所淹没。与此同时，医疗领域新型基于人工智能的方法的出现，要求能够处理特定领域非结构化临床信息并适应患者特定需求的智能框架。本文提出了一种用于构建鲁棒性基于大语言模型管道的智能体框架，其中每个阶段都被封装为一个由显式策略和代理引导评估的LangChain智能体。阶段一旦验证就会被逐步锁定，确保后续修改无法在没有显示改进的情况下覆写配置。所提出的框架从特征级探索开始，通过基于代理的调优和冻结/回滚机制，最终由协调器智能体全面编排预处理、检索、选择、多样性、阈值优化和解码。在基于转录本的抑郁症检测概念验证中，该框架收敛到稳定配置，例如余弦相似度、动态Top-k和阈值0.75，同时控制评估成本并避免回归。这些结果突显了智能体人工智能在大型临床数据集上实现群体级心理健康筛查的潜力，解决了医疗环境所需的关键挑战，包括可信度、可重复性和适应性。

Original abstract: Mental health disorders affect millions worldwide, and healthcare systems are increasingly overwhelmed by the volume of clinical data generated from electronic records, telemedicine platforms, and population-level screening programs. At the same time, the emergence of novel AI-based approaches in healthcare calls for intelligent frameworks capable of processing domain-specific unstructured clinical information while adapting to patient-specific needs. This paper proposes an agentic framework for building robust LLM-based pipelines, where each stage is encapsulated as a LangChain agent governed by explicit policies and proxy-guided evaluation. Stages are incrementally locked once validated, ensuring that later adaptations cannot overwrite configurations without demonstrated improvement. The proposed framework evolves from feature-level exploration, through proxy-based tuning and freeze/rollback mechanisms, to full orchestration by an Orchestrator Agent that coordinates preprocessing, retrieval, selection, diversity, threshold optimization, and decoding. A proof-of-concept in transcript-based depression detection demonstrates that the framework converges to stable configurations, such as cosine similarity, dynamic Top-k, and threshold 0.75, while controlling evaluation costs and avoiding regressions. These results highlight the potential of agentic AI to enable population-level mental health screening over large clinical datasets, addressing critical challenges in trustworthiness, reproducibility, and adaptability required in healthcare environments.

*Moritz Firsching,Paul Lezeau,Salvatore Mercuri,Miklós Z. Horváth,Yaël Dillies,Calle Sönne,Eric Wieser,Fred Zhang,Thomas Hubert,Blaise Agüera y Arcas,Pushmeet Kohli*

TL;DR: 提出了一个包含2615个Lean 4形式化数学问题的基准测试Formal Conjectures，包括开放猜想和已解决问题，用于评估自动推理能力，并已用于数学发现。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建Formal Conjectures基准，从活跃数学研究领域收集问题，形式化为Lean 4；通过结构化接口连接数学家和AI系统；利用AI生成的证明/反证进行迭代审计以确保正确性。

Result: 包含2615个问题，其中1029个开放猜想和836个已解决问题；已用于解决开放猜想并做出新数学发现；在冻结子集上报告了基线结果。

Original abstract: As automated reasoning systems advance rapidly, there is a growing need for research-level formal mathematical problems to accurately evaluate their capabilities. To address this, we present Formal Conjectures, an evolving benchmark of currently 2615 mathematical problem statements formalized in Lean 4. Sourced from areas of active mathematical research, the dataset features 1029 open research conjectures providing a zero-contamination benchmark for mathematical proof discovery, and 836 solved problems for proof autoformalization. Notably, the repository provides a structured interface connecting mathematicians who formalize and clarify problems with the AI systems and humans attempting to solve them. Demonstrating its immediate utility, the benchmark has already been leveraged to make new mathematical discoveries, including the resolution of open research conjectures. We describe our approach to ensuring the correctness of these formalizations in a collaborative open-source project where contributions stem from an active community. In this framework, AI-generated proofs and disproofs serve as a valuable auditing mechanism to iteratively improve the fidelity of the benchmark. Finally, we provide a standardized evaluation setup and report baseline results on frozen evaluation subsets, demonstrating a climbable signal that measures the current frontier of automated reasoning on research-level mathematics.

### [33] [ICRL: Learning to Internalize Self-Critique with Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15224v1)
*Jianbo Lin,Xiaomin Yu,Yi Xin,Yifu Guo,Zhuosong Jiang,Zhongqi Yue,Weishi Wang,Heqing Zou,Chengwei Qin,Hui Xiong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出ICRL框架，通过强化学习内化自我批判，提升agent推理能力，可迁移至代码优化agent的自我改进。

TL;DR: 提出ICRL框架，通过强化学习联合训练求解器和批评者，使求解者内化批评并自我改进，无需外部批评，在多项基准上取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前模型依赖外部批评指导才能正确，移除批评后失败，且冻结的批评者无法自我提升，限制了自我改进。

Method: ICRL框架，基于共享骨干网络联合训练求解器和批评者，引入分布校准重加权比率处理分布偏移，以及角色分组优势估计稳定联合优化。

Result: 在智能体推理和数学推理任务上，ICRL比GRPO平均提升6.4和7.0个百分点；学到的8B批评者与32B性能相当且更高效。

Conclusion: ICRL有效实现了模型自我改进，无需外部批评，且批评者高效，展示了内化批评的潜力。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型的智能体可能会犯错，但批评通常能引导同一模型走向正确行为。然而，当批评被移除后，模型可能在相同查询上再次失败，表明它并未将批评的指导内化为其基础能力。同时，冻结的批评者无法随时间提高其反馈质量，限制了迭代自我改进的潜力。为解决这个问题，我们提出通过学习内化自我批评与强化学习（ICRL），这是一种新颖的框架，从共享骨干网络联合训练求解器和批评者，将批评引发的成功转化为无需协助的求解器能力。批评者根据求解器后续性能提升获得奖励，激励可操作的反馈。为了解决批评条件和无批评行为之间的分布偏移，ICRL引入了一个分布校准重加权比率，有选择地转移与求解器自身提示分布兼容的批评引导改进。此外，角色分组优势估计稳定了两个角色之间的联合优化。这些机制共同确保求解器学会在没有外部批评的情况下自我改进，而不是依赖批评条件行为。我们在涵盖智能体推理和数学推理任务的多种基准上评估ICRL，使用Qwen3-4B和Qwen3-8B作为骨干网络。结果显示持续改进，在智能体任务上比GRPO平均提升6.4个百分点，在数学推理上提升7.0个百分点。值得注意的是，学到的8B批评者与32B批评者性能相当，同时使用更少的令牌。代码可在https://github.com/brick-pid/ICRL获取。

Original abstract: Large language model-based agents make mistakes, yet critique can often guide the same model toward correct behavior. However, when critique is removed, the model may fail again on the same query, indicating that it has not internalized the critique's guidance into its underlying capability. Meanwhile, a frozen critic cannot improve its feedback quality over time, limiting the potential for iterative self-improvement. To address this, we propose learning to internalize self-critique with reinforcement learning(ICRL), a novel framework that jointly trains a solver and a critic from a shared backbone to convert critique-induced success into unassisted solver ability. The critic is rewarded based on the solver's subsequent performance gain, incentivizing actionable feedback. To address the distribution shift between critique-conditioned and critique-free behavior, ICRL introduces a distribution-calibration re-weighting ratio that selectively transfers critique-guided improvements compatible with the solver's own prompt distribution. Additionally, a role-wise group advantage estimation stabilizes joint optimization across the two roles. Together, these mechanisms ensure that the solver learns to improve itself without external critique, rather than becoming dependent on critique-conditioned behavior. We evaluate ICRL on diverse benchmarks spanning agentic and mathematical reasoning tasks, using Qwen3-4B and Qwen3-8B as backbones. Results show consistent improvements, with average gains of 6.4 points over GRPO on agentic tasks, and 7.0 points on mathematical reasoning. Notably, the learned 8B critic is comparable to 32B critics while using substantially fewer tokens. The code is available at https://github.com/brick-pid/ICRL.

</details>


### [34] [Hierarchical Attacks for Multi-Modal Multi-Agent Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13213v1)
*Hao Zhou,Tiru Wu,Yan Jiang,Wanqi Zhou,Junxing Hu,Ai Han*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多模态多agent系统层次化攻击，对agent安全性和鲁棒性有参考价值。

TL;DR: 提出了针对多模态多智能体系统的分层攻击框架HAM$^{3}$，在感知、通信和推理三层实施攻击，在GQA基准上达到78.3%攻击成功率，推理层攻击最有效，且多数成功攻击导致多智能体一致错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对抗攻击研究主要针对孤立智能体或单模态设置，忽视了多模态多智能体系统的脆弱性，亟需系统性探索。

Method: 提出HAM$^{3}$分层攻击框架，包含三层：(1)感知层：扰动视觉、文本输入及融合表示；(2)通信层：破坏消息内容和交互拓扑；(3)推理层：干扰认知管道偏置推理轨迹。

Result: 在GQA基准上，基于ReAct、Plan-and-Solve和Reflexion范式的多智能体系统，攻击成功率达78.3%，推理层攻击最有效，超半数成功攻击导致多个智能体产生一致错误。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了多模态多智能体系统的脆弱性，为构建更鲁棒和可解释的多智能体智能提供了宝贵见解。

中文摘要：多模态多智能体系统（MM-MAS）因其在跨不同模态实现复杂推理和协调的能力而受到越来越多的关注。随着这些系统的规模和功能持续扩展，研究其潜在脆弱性变得愈发重要。然而，现有的多智能体系统对抗攻击研究主要关注孤立智能体或单模态设置，导致MM-MAS的脆弱性在很大程度上未被探索。为填补这一空白，我们提出了HAM$^{3}$，一种针对多模态多智能体系统的分层攻击框架，将攻击分解为三个相互连接的层次。具体而言，在感知层，HAM$^{3}$通过扰动视觉输入、文本输入及其融合的视觉-文本表示来发起攻击。在通信层，它执行通信级攻击，破坏消息内容和交互拓扑，例如操纵共享上下文或通信链路以扭曲集体信息流。在推理层，它进行推理级攻击，干扰每个智能体的认知管道，偏置推理轨迹，最终危及最终决策。我们在GQA基准上，通过基于不同推理范式（包括ReAct、Plan-and-Solve和Reflexion）构建的多智能体系统评估了HAM$^{3}$。实验表明，我们的框架实现了高达78.3%的攻击成功率，其中推理层攻击最为有效。超过一半的成功攻击导致多个智能体产生一致错误。这些发现为构建更鲁棒和可解释的多智能体智能提供了宝贵见解。

Original abstract: Multi-modal multi-agent systems (MM-MAS) have gained increasing attention for their capacity to enable complex reasoning and coordination across diverse modalities. As these systems continue to expand in scale and functionality, investigating their potential vulnerabilities has become increasingly important. However, existing studies on adversarial attacks in multi-agent systems primarily focus on isolated agents or unimodal settings, leaving the vulnerabilities of MM-MAS largely underexplored. To bridge this gap, we introduce HAM$^{3}$, a Hierarchical Attack framework for multi-modal multi-agent systems that decomposes attacks into three interconnected layers. Specifically, at the perception layer, HAM$^{3}$ mounts attacks by perturbing visual inputs, textual inputs, and their fused visual-textual representations. At the communication layer, it performs communication-level attacks that corrupt message content and interaction topology, such as manipulating shared context or communication links to distort collective information flow. At the reasoning layer, it conducts reasoning-level attacks that interfere with each agent's cognitive pipeline, biasing reasoning trajectories and ultimately compromising final decisions. We evaluate HAM$^{3}$ on the GQA benchmark through multi-agent systems built on distinct reasoning paradigms including ReAct, Plan-and-Solve, and Reflexion. Experiments demonstrate that our framework achieves an Attack Success Rate of up to 78.3%, with reasoning-layer attacks being the most effective. More than half of the successful attacks lead multiple agents to produce consistent errors. These findings offer valuable insights for building more robust and interpretable multi-agent intelligence.

</details>


### [35] [Improving Code Translation with Syntax-Guided and Semantic-aware Preference Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13229v1)
*Yuhan Wu,Huan Zhang,Wei Cheng,Chen Shen,Jingyue Yang,Wei Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出CTO方法，结合语法引导和语义感知的偏好优化，通过对比学习训练跨语言语义模型评估功能等价性，显著提升代码翻译的语法正确性和语义一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在C++、Java和Python翻译任务上，CTO显著优于现有基线和替代偏好优化策略。

Conclusion: CTO通过语法引导和语义感知的偏好优化有效提升了代码翻译质量，验证了直接源自源代码的语义奖励的鲁棒性。

中文摘要：LLMs在代码翻译方面显示出了巨大的潜力，但它们在确保语法正确性和语义一致性方面常常面临困难。虽然基于偏好的学习提供了一种有前景的对齐策略，但由于从稀疏的测试用例或限制性的参考翻译中得出的不可靠语义奖励，该策略受到阻碍。我们认为，代码翻译的鲁棒语义奖励必须直接从源代码中得出。在本文中，我们提出了CTO，通过语法引导和语义感知的偏好优化来改进代码翻译。通过对比学习，我们训练了一个跨语言语义模型，以直接评估源代码和翻译代码之间的功能等价性。通过将代码翻译表述为多目标优化问题，这个鲁棒的语义信号与基于编译器的语法反馈在直接偏好优化框架内无缝统一。在C++、Java和Python翻译上的大量实验表明，CTO显著优于现有基线和替代偏好优化策略。

Original abstract: LLMs have shown immense potential for code translation, yet they often struggle to ensure both syntactic correctness and semantic consistency. While preference-based learning offers a promising alignment strategy, it is hindered by unreliable semantic rewards derived from sparse test cases or restrictive reference translations. We argue that a robust semantic reward for code translation must be derived directly from the source code. In this paper, we propose CTO to improve code translation with syntax-guided and semantic-aware preference optimization. Through contrastive learning, we train a cross-lingual semantic model to directly assess functional equivalence between source and translated code. By formulating code translation as a multi-objective optimization problem, this robust semantic signal is seamlessly unified with compiler-based syntactic feedback within the direct preference optimization framework. Extensive experiments on C++, Java, and Python translations demonstrate that CTO significantly outperforms existing baselines and alternative preference optimization strategies.

### [36] [It's not the Language Model, it's the Tool: Deterministic Mediation for Scientific Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13245v1)
*Marios Adamidis,Danae Katrisioti,Yannis Tzitzikas,Emmanuel Stratakis*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出工具中介模式保障科学工作流可重复性，对代码优化agent使用确定性工具（如编译器）有重要参考。

TL;DR: 本文提出类型中介模式，让语言模型调用确定性工具而非生成代码，从而保证科学分析的可重复性，实验表明该方法在多个商业模型上输出一致且用户反馈积极。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型生成的科学分析结果不可重复，相同查询可能产生不同输出，研究者难以判断信任哪个结果。

Method: 提出类型中介模式：模型选择并调用编码了精确分析流程的确定性工具，工具输出固定，不随重新生成改变。

Result: 类型工具在所有运行中产生相同结果，商业平台结果变化或失败；在真实仪器上部署六个月，用户反馈积极。

Conclusion: 类型中介是一种实用模式，适用于需要可重复性的科学工作流，能大幅缩短分析时间并保证输出一致性，部署拓扑是结构要求。

中文摘要：语言模型可以生成令人信服的科学分析，但对同一数据重复生成并不保证相同的结果。研究者可能重新生成相同的查询却得到不同的拟合、不同的峰值位置或不同的分析流程，却无法明确判断该信任哪个输出。我们提出了类型中介（typed mediation）模式，即模型协调确定性工具而非生成分析代码。每个工具编码了一位研究者在结构化的访谈中移植的一个仪器的精确流程。模型选择调用哪个工具以及使用什么参数。工具产生结果。重新生成不会改变结果。我们通过在四个平台上运行相同的光致发光分析来评估这一主张，包括三个商业基础模型，每个模型使用相同提示运行四次。类型工具在所有运行中产生相同的结果。商业平台要么在数值输出和分析方法上随运行而变化，要么无法在该任务上产生有效结果。我们将该模式部署在两个服务于用户约六个月的仪器上，获得了非常积极的用户反馈。两个案例都非常具有挑战性：它们涉及专有二进制格式和按席位许可的软件，这迫使工具与数据及其操作的仪器一起保留在本地基础设施上。我们认为部署拓扑不仅仅是一种偏好，而是科学工具中介的结构性要求。结果是一种在需要可重复性的科学工作流中部署语言模型的实用模式，将分析时间从数周缩短到分钟，同时保证跨运行产生相同的输出。

Original abstract: Language models can produce convincing scientific analyses, but repeated generations on the same data do not guarantee the same result. A researcher may regenerate an identical query and receive a different fit, a different peak position or a different analysis procedure, without an obvious way to decide which output to trust. We propose typed mediation, a pattern in which the model orchestrates deterministic tools rather than generating analytical code. Each tool encodes one researcher's exact procedure for one instrument, ported through structured interviews. The model selects which tool to call and with what parameters. The tool produces the result. Regeneration does not change it. We evaluate this claim by running the same photoluminescence analysis on four platforms, including three commercial foundation models, four times each with the same prompt. The typed tool produces identical results across all runs. The commercial platforms either vary in numerical output and analytical methodology across runs, or fail to produce valid results on the task. We deploy this pattern on two instruments serving users over approximately six months, with very positive user feedback. Both cases are very challenging: they involve proprietary binary formats and per-seat licensed software, which force the tool to remain on local infrastructure alongside the data and the instrument it operates. We argue that deployment topology is not just a preference, but a structural requirement of scientific tool mediation. The result is a practical pattern for deploying language models in scientific workflows where reproducibility is mandatory, reducing analysis time from weeks to minutes while guaranteeing identical outputs across runs.

### [37] [D-VLA: A High-Concurrency Distributed Asynchronous Reinforcement Learning Framework for Vision-Language-Action Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13276v2)
*Yucheng Guo,Yongjian Guo,Zhong Guan,Wen Huang,Haoran Sun,Haodong Yue,Xiaolong Xiang,Shuai Di,Zhen Sun,Luqiao Wang,Junwu Xiong,Yicheng Gong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分布式RL框架，可迁移至agent训练流程。

TL;DR: D-VLA通过平面解耦、泳道流水线和双池VRAM管理，实现了大规模VLA模型的高效分布式强化学习训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型在分布式RL训练中存在资源冲突和执行阶段低效，导致吞吐量受限。

Method: 提出平面解耦隔离数据与权重控制，设计四线程异步泳道流水线实现并行重叠，采用双池VRAM管理和拓扑感知复制解决内存与通信问题。

Result: 在十亿参数VLA模型上显著优于主流框架，在万亿参数规模下保持稳定和线性加速。

中文摘要：具身智能的快速发展使得视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在多模态感知和任务执行方面表现出色。然而，将这些大型模型应用于大规模分布式环境中的强化学习（RL）面临严重的系统瓶颈，主要源于高保真物理模拟与深度学习密集的VRAM/带宽需求之间的资源冲突。这种冲突往往导致整体吞吐量受限于执行阶段低效。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了D-VLA，一种面向大规模具身基础模型的高并发、低延迟分布式强化学习框架。D-VLA引入了“平面解耦”，将高频训练数据与低频权重控制物理隔离，以消除模拟与优化之间的干扰。我们还设计了一个四线程异步“泳道”流水线，实现了采样、推理、梯度计算和参数分布的完全并行重叠。此外，双池VRAM管理模型和拓扑感知复制解决了内存碎片问题并优化了通信效率。在LIBERO等基准测试上的实验表明，D-VLA在十亿参数VLA模型的吞吐量和采样效率上显著优于主流强化学习框架。在万亿参数可扩展性测试中，我们的框架保持了出色的稳定性和线性加速，为高性能通用具身智能体提供了稳健的系统。

Original abstract: The rapid evolution of Embodied AI has enabled Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models to excel in multimodal perception and task execution. However, applying Reinforcement Learning (RL) to these massive models in large-scale distributed environments faces severe systemic bottlenecks, primarily due to the resource conflict between high-fidelity physical simulation and the intensive VRAM/bandwidth demands of deep learning. This conflict often leaves overall throughput constrained by execution-phase inefficiencies. To address these challenges, we propose D-VLA, a high-concurrency, low-latency distributed RL framework for large-scale embodied foundation models. D-VLA introduces "Plane Decoupling," physically isolating high-frequency training data from low-frequency weight control to eliminate interference between simulation and optimization. We further design a four-thread asynchronous "Swimlane" pipeline, enabling full parallel overlap of sampling, inference, gradient computation, and parameter distribution. Additionally, a dual-pool VRAM management model and topology-aware replication resolve memory fragmentation and optimize communication efficiency. Experiments on benchmarks like LIBERO show that D-VLA significantly outperforms mainstream RL frameworks in throughput and sampling efficiency for billion-parameter VLA models. In trillion-parameter scalability tests, our framework maintains exceptional stability and linear speedup, providing a robust system for high-performance general-purpose embodied agents.

### [38] [Differentiable Learning of Lifted Action Schemas for Classical Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13282v2)
*Jonas Reiter,Jakob Elias Gebler,Hector Geffner*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 学习动作模式用于规划，可启发coding agent的动作抽象。

TL;DR: 提出了一种从完全可观测状态但不可观测动作参数的轨迹中学习提升动作模式的新型神经网络架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典规划中学习动作模式和关系是结构泛化的关键，但现有方法需要不同类型的观测，而实际中动作参数常不可观测，因此需要一种能从部分观测数据中学习的方法。

Method: 开发了一种神经网络架构，从轨迹中同时学习动作模式并识别动作参数，输出一个可微组件用于神经符号模型。

Result: 在多个规划领域上，学到的提升动作模式能恢复真实结构，且对观测噪声具有鲁棒性，并与基于槽的动态模型相关的方法进行了比较。

Conclusion: 该工作为从图像序列和动作标签学习规划领域奠定了基础，提供了一个稳健的可微学习组件。

中文摘要：经典规划器可以有效地解决用STRIPS或PDDL表示的非常大的确定性MDP，其中状态是关于对象和关系的原子集合，而提升的动作模式添加或删除这些原子。这种紧凑的表示产生了强大的搜索启发式方法，并为结构泛化提供了理想的环境，因为提升的关系和动作模式产生了无限多的领域实例。一个核心挑战是从数据中学习这些关系和动作模式，最近的方法使用不同类型的观测来解决这个问题。在这项工作中，我们开发了一种新颖的神经网络架构，用于从状态完全可观测但动作参数不可观测的轨迹中学习动作模式。这个问题是一个简化，但却是朝着从图像序列和动作标签学习规划领域的重要一步，我们的目标是以近乎完美的方式解决这个简化问题。挑战在于在学习动作模式的同时，从观察到的状态变化中识别动作参数。我们的方法产生了一个稳健的可微组件，然后可以集成到更大的神经符号模型中。我们在各种规划领域上评估了该架构，其中学到的提升动作模式必须恢复真实结构。此外，我们报告了关于对观测噪声的鲁棒性以及与基于槽的动态模型相关的变体的实验。

Original abstract: Classical planners can effectively solve very large deterministic MDPs represented in STRIPS or PDDL where states are sets of atoms over objects and relations, and lifted action schemas add or delete these atoms. This compact representation yields strong search heuristics and provides an ideal setting for structural generalization, since lifted relations and action schemas give rise to infinitely many domain instances. A central challenge is to learn these relations and action schemas from data, and recent approaches have addressed this problem using different types of observations. In this work, we develop a novel neural network architecture for learning action schemas from traces where states are fully observed but action arguments are unobserved. The problem is a simplification but an important step towards learning planning domains from sequences of images and action labels, and we aim to solve this simplification in a nearly perfect manner. The challenge lies in learning the action schemas while simultaneously identifying the action arguments from observed state changes. Our approach yields a robust differentiable component that can then be integrated into larger neuro-symbolic models. We evaluate the architecture on various planning domains, where the learned lifted action schemas must recover the ground-truth structure. Additionally, we report experiments on robustness to observation noise and on a variation related to slot-based dynamics models.

### [39] [Discrete Diffusion for Complex and Congested Multi-Agent Path Finding with Sparse Social Attention](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13296v1)
*Yuanzhe Wang,Tian Zhi,Zihang Wei,Hongguang Wang,Jiaming Guo,Yang Zhao,Zisheng Liu,Shiyu Quan,Xing Hu,Zidong Du,Yunji Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 离散扩散用于多智能体路径规划，可迁移至多agent协作。

TL;DR: 提出DiffLNS，将离散扩散模型与LNS2结合，通过生成高质量初始计划提升MAPF修复成功率，在拥挤场景中达到95.8%平均成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于修复的MAPF求解器对初始计划质量敏感，而次优初始计划在密集环境中易产生复合冲突，影响修复效率。

Method: 构建DiffLNS框架，使用D3PM作为初始化器生成多样化的联合计划草案，作为LNS2的热启动，通过稀疏社交注意力学习时空先验。

Result: 在20个复杂拥挤场景中，DiffLNS平均成功率达95.8%，超过最强基线9.6个百分点，并泛化到未见的大规模实例（最多312智能体）。

Conclusion: 离散扩散模型能有效为LNS2提供高质量初始计划，显著提升MAPF求解性能，是首个将此类方法应用于MAPF的工作。

中文摘要：多智能体路径规划（MAPF）是一个协调问题，需要在组合规划复杂度下，从各个起始位置到指定的目标位置计算全局一致、无碰撞的轨迹。在密集环境中，次优的初始计划会引起复合冲突，阻碍可行的修复。对于基于修复的求解器（如LNS2），初始计划质量对下游修复至关重要，但这一因素尚未得到充分探索。我们提出了DiffLNS，一种将离散去噪扩散概率模型（D3PM）与LNS2集成的混合框架。D3PM作为初始化器，具有稀疏社交注意力，从专家演示中学习协调多智能体动作轨迹的时空先验，并对多个联合计划进行采样。直接在分类动作空间上操作，我们的离散扩散保留了MAPF动作结构，并从多模态联合计划分布中采样，生成适合邻域修复的多样化草案。这些草案作为下游修复的热启动，在硬MAPF约束下完成未完成的轨迹并解决剩余冲突。实验结果表明，尽管仅在最多96个智能体的实例上训练，该初始化器在推理时能泛化到多达312个智能体的场景。在20个复杂拥挤的设置中，DiffLNS实现了95.8%的平均成功率，比最强的测试基线高出9.6个百分点，并在所有20个设置中匹配或超过所有基线。据我们所知，这是首个利用离散扩散热启动基于LNS的MAPF求解器的工作。

Original abstract: Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) is a coordination problem that requires computing globally consistent, collision-free trajectories from individual start positions to assigned goal positions under combinatorial planning complexity. In dense environments, suboptimal initial plans induce compound conflicts that hinder feasible repair. For repair-based solvers like LNS2, initial plan quality critically affects downstream repair, yet this factor remains underexplored. We propose DiffLNS, a hybrid framework that integrates a discrete denoising diffusion probabilistic model (D3PM) with LNS2. The D3PM serves as an initializer with sparse social attention that learns a spatiotemporal prior over coordinated multi-agent action trajectories from expert demonstrations and samples multiple joint plans. Operating directly on the categorical action space, our discrete diffusion preserves the MAPF action structure and samples from a multimodal joint-plan distribution to produce diverse drafts well suited for neighborhood repair. These drafts act as warm starts for downstream repair, which completes unfinished trajectories and resolves remaining conflicts under hard MAPF constraints. Experimental results show that despite being trained only on instances with at most 96 agents, the initializer generalizes to scenarios with up to 312 agents at inference time. Across 20 complex and congested settings, DiffLNS achieves an average success rate of 95.8%, outperforming the strongest tested baseline by 9.6 percentage points and matching or exceeding all baselines in all 20 settings. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work to leverage discrete diffusion for warm-starting an LNS-based MAPF solver.

### [40] [IdeaForge: A Knowledge Graph-Grounded Multi-Agent Framework for Cross-Methodology Innovation Analysis and Patent Claim Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13311v1)
*Joy Bose*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI创新系统使用单一方法论和顺序提示，缺乏中间推理结构，导致跨方法论的见解碎片化，难以追溯和评估。

Result: 在法律技术用例上，相比单一方法论基线，IdeaForge产生的创新候选更多样化且可追溯。

Conclusion: 图原生多方法论合成能增强计算创造力和可解释AI发明，为创新系统提供新范式。

中文摘要：当前人工智能辅助的创新系统通常采用单一的创新方法论（如TRIZ或设计思维），使用基于顺序提示的工作流，这些工作流不保留中间推理结构。因此，跨方法论产生的见解仍然分散，限制了可追溯性、综合性和新颖性的系统评估。我们提出了IdeaForge，一个知识图谱驱动的多智能体框架，用于创新分析和专利权利要求生成。IdeaForge通过专业智能体在持久化FalkorDB知识图谱上操作，整合了多种创新方法论（TRIZ、设计思维和SCAMPER）。每个智能体贡献结构化的实体和关系，表示矛盾、发明原理、用户需求、转换、类比和候选权利要求。IdeaForge的核心贡献是通过基于图谱的权利要求链接实现的跨方法论收敛机制。由多种方法论独立支持的权利要求通过CONVERGENT关系连接，从而通过图遍历识别高置信度的创新候选。下游专利起草智能体基于收敛权利要求子图生成结构化专利草案，减少了对无约束语言模型生成的依赖。创新分数公式根据收敛支持度、方法论多样性、权利要求强度和现有技术挑战数量对权利要求进行排名。我们描述了图模式、智能体架构、收敛检测管道和专利合成工作流。在法律技术用例上的实验表明，与单一方法论基线相比，基于图谱的多方法论合成产生了更多样化和可追溯的创新候选。我们讨论了对计算创造力、可解释的人工智能辅助发明和图原生创新系统的启示。

Original abstract: Current AI-assisted innovation systems typically apply a single ideation methodology (such as TRIZ or Design Thinking) using sequential prompt-based workflows that do not preserve intermediate reasoning structure. As a result, insights generated across methodologies remain fragmented, limiting traceability, synthesis, and systematic evaluation of novelty. We present IdeaForge, a knowledge graph-grounded multi-agent framework for innovation analysis and patent claim generation. IdeaForge integrates multiple innovation methodologies (TRIZ, Design Thinking, and SCAMPER) through specialist agents operating over a persistent FalkorDB knowledge graph. Each agent contributes structured entities and relationships representing contradictions, inventive principles, user needs, transformations, analogies, and candidate claims. The central contribution of IdeaForge is a cross-methodology convergence mechanism implemented through graph-based claim linkage. Claims independently supported by multiple methodologies are connected using CONVERGENT relationships, enabling identification of high-confidence innovation candidates through graph traversal. A downstream patent drafting agent generates structured patent drafts grounded in convergent claim subgraphs, reducing reliance on unconstrained language model generation. An InnovationScore formula ranks claims by convergent support, methodology diversity, claim strength, and prior art challenge count. We describe the graph schema, agent architecture, convergence detection pipeline, and patent synthesis workflow. Experiments on a legal technology use case demonstrate that graph-grounded multi-methodology synthesis produces more diverse and traceable innovation candidates compared to single-methodology baselines. We discuss implications for computational creativity, explainable AI-assisted invention, and graph-native innovation systems.

### [41] [Ego2World: Compiling Egocentric Cooking Videos into Executable Worlds for Belief-State Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13335v1)
*Qinchuan Cheng,Zhantao Gong,Pengzhan Sun,Angela Yao,Xulei Yang,Shijie Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 信念状态规划基准，测试agent记忆与规划能力。

TL;DR: Ego2World将第一人称烹饪视频转化为可执行的符号世界，用于评估具身智能体在部分可观测下的规划和信念维护能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准要么是被动视频数据集，要么是交互式模拟器但存在sim-to-real差距和全观测假设，无法充分测试部分可观测下的规划能力。

Method: 从HD-EPIC视频注释中推导可重用转换规则，构建隐藏符号世界图；智能体基于局部观测和反馈在其部分信念图上规划。

Result: 动作重叠分数高估物理状态成功；持久信念记忆提高任务完成度并减少重复视觉探索。

中文摘要：居家环境中的具身智能体必须在部分可观测下进行规划：它们需要记住物体、跟踪状态变化，并在动作失败时恢复。现有基准仅部分测试了这种能力。第一人称视频数据集捕捉了真实的人类活动，但仍然是被动式的，而交互式模拟器支持执行，但依赖于合成场景和手工制作的动力学，引入了模拟到现实的差距，并且通常假设完全可观测的状态。我们引入了Ego2World，一个可执行的基准，它将第一人称烹饪视频转化为由图转换规则控制的可执行符号世界。基于HD-EPIC，Ego2World从视频注释中推导出可重用的转换规则，并在隐藏的符号世界图中执行。在评估期间，模拟器维护隐藏的世界图，而智能体仅使用局部观察和执行反馈在其部分信念图上进行规划。这种分离迫使智能体在不观察真实世界状态的情况下更新记忆并重新规划。实验表明，动作重叠分数高估了物理状态的成功，而持久信念记忆提高了任务完成度，同时减少了重复的视觉探索——这表明信念维护应成为具身智能体评估的首要目标。

Original abstract: Embodied agents in household environments must plan under partial observation: they need to remember objects, track state changes, and recover when actions fail. Existing benchmarks only partially test this ability. Egocentric video datasets capture realistic human activities but remain passive, while interactive simulators support execution but rely on synthetic scenes and hand-crafted dynamics, introducing a sim-to-real gap and often assuming fully observable state. We introduce Ego2World, an executable benchmark that turns egocentric cooking videos into executable symbolic worlds governed by graph-transition rules. Built on HD-EPIC, Ego2World derives reusable transition rules from video annotations and executes them in a hidden symbolic world graph. During evaluation, the simulator maintains the hidden world graph, while the agent plans over its own partial belief graph using only local observations and execution feedback. This separation forces agents to update memory and replan without observing the true world state. Experiments show that action-overlap scores overestimate physical-state success, and that persistent belief memory improves task completion while reducing repeated visual exploration -- suggesting that belief maintenance should be a first-class target of embodied-agent evaluation.

### [42] [RS-Claw: Progressive Active Tool Exploration via Hierarchical Skill Trees for Remote Sensing Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13391v1)
*Liangtian Liu,Zeyuan Wang,Ziyu Li,Kai Ouyang,Zichao Tang,Chengfu Liu,Haifeng Li,Hanwen Yu,Wentao Yang,Cheng Yang,Dongyang Hou*

Selection reason: 主动工具探索与分层技能树架构，通用agent工具使用与规划方法。

TL;DR: 提出RS-Claw，一种主动探索工具空间的遥感智能体架构，通过技能封装实现分层决策，在Earth-Bench上实现86%令牌压缩并全面超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有遥感智能体采用被动工具选择（Flat或RAG），在工具海量且异构的背景下无法平衡上下文负载与工具完整性，导致长期任务中上下文不足或关键工具遗漏。

Method: 提出RS-Claw架构，利用技能封装技术对工具描述进行分层结构化，使智能体先读摘要选技能分支，再动态加载详细描述，实现按需顺序决策的主动探索。

Result: 在Earth-Bench基准上，RS-Claw的主动机制实现输入令牌压缩86%，有效过滤语义噪声，在复杂推理评估中全面优于Flat和RAG基线。

Conclusion: 主动探索范式显著释放上下文空间并保证关键工具命中率，为大规模遥感工具生态下的智能体设计提供了有效方案。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的兴起正在将遥感（RS）智能从“看见”转向“行动”，因为类似OpenClaw的框架使智能体能够自主操作海量遥感图像处理工具以完成复杂任务。现有的遥感智能体采用被动选择范式进行工具调用，要么依赖全工具注册（Flat），要么依赖检索增强生成（RAG）。然而，在海量且多源异构的遥感工具生态系统中，这种被动机制难以在任务推理过程中动态平衡“上下文负载”和“工具集完整性”，从而表现出固有局限性：全工具注册在长期任务中引发上下文空间不足，而RAG检索可能遗漏关键步骤中的必要工具。为克服这些瓶颈，本文重新定义工具选择，主张智能体应作为工具空间中的主动探索者。基于此观点，我们提出RS-Claw，一种新型遥感智能体架构。通过在工具端利用技能封装技术，该架构分层结构化工具描述，使智能体能够执行按需的顺序决策：首先仅通过阅读工具摘要选择相关技能分支，然后动态加载详细描述，最终实现精确调用。这种主动范式不仅显著释放了智能体的上下文空间，还有效确保了长期推理过程中关键工具的准确命中率。在Earth-Bench基准上的系统实验表明，RS-Claw的主动探索机制有效过滤语义噪声并大幅释放推理空间，实现了高达86%的输入令牌压缩比，并在复杂推理评估中全面超越现有的Flat和RAG基线。

Original abstract: The rise of multi-modal large language models (MLLMs) is shifting remote sensing (RS) intelligence from "see" to "action", as OpenClaw-style frameworks enable agents to autonomously operate massive RS image-processing tools for complex tasks. Existing RS agents adopt a passive selection paradigm for tool invocation, relying on either full tool registration (Flat) or retrieval-augmented generation (RAG). However, in the massive and multi-source heterogeneous RS tool ecosystem, such passive mechanisms struggle to dynamically balance "context load" and "toolset completeness" throughout task reasoning, thus exhibiting inherent limitations: full tool registration triggers context space deficits during long-horizon tasks, whereas RAG retrieval may omit critical tools in essential steps. To overcome these bottlenecks, this paper redefines tool selection by arguing that the agent should act as an active explorer within the tool space. Based on this perspective, we propose RS-Claw, a novel RS agent architecture. By leveraging Skill encapsulation technology at the tool end, this architecture hierarchically structures tool descriptions, enabling the agent to execute on-demand sequential decision-making: initially selecting relevant skill branches by reading only tool summaries, then dynamically loading detailed descriptions, and ultimately achieving precise invocation. This active paradigm not only significantly liberates the agent's context space but also effectively ensures the accurate hit rate of critical tools during long-horizon reasoning. Systematic experiments on the Earth-Bench benchmark demonstrate that RS-Claw's active exploration mechanism effectively filters semantic noise and substantially frees up reasoning space, achieving an input token compression ratio of up to 86%, and comprehensively outperforming existing Flat and RAG baselines across complex reasoning evaluations.

### [43] [TRIAGE: Evaluating Prospective Metacognitive Control in LLMs under Resource Constraints](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13414v1)
*Zabir Al Nazi,Shubhashis Roy Dipta*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估LLM资源约束下的元认知控制，直接测试agent规划与资源分配能力。

TL;DR: 本文提出TRIAGE评估框架，测试语言模型在前瞻性元认知控制方面的能力，即如何在有限token预算下智能选择、排序和分配计算资源。实验发现现有模型存在显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型作为自主智能体需要前瞻性元认知控制，但现有评估只关注单任务准确率，忽略了在有限资源下的多任务规划能力。

Method: 提出TRIAGE框架，模型接收任务池和token预算，输出单一排序计划（选择、排序、分配），与全知大仙的分数比较得到分诊效率比。

Result: 前沿和开源模型（包括推理模式）在竞赛数学、科学、代码、多学科知识上表现出显著的前瞻性元认知控制差距。

Conclusion: 揭示了语言模型尚未测量的能力维度，对资源高效的智能体部署有直接意义。

中文摘要：将语言模型部署为自主智能体需要的不仅仅是每任务的准确率：当智能体在有限token预算下面临一系列问题时，它必须决定尝试哪些问题、以什么顺序、以及每个问题投入多少计算量，所有这些都在任何执行反馈可用之前完成。这是人类认知中研究了数十年的前瞻性元认知控制形式，但语言模型是否具备这种能力尚未得到检验。我们提出了TRIAGE，一个评估框架，其中模型接收一个任务池和一个根据自身基线成本校准的token预算，并承诺一个单一的排序计划，该计划联合编码了选择、排序和每个问题的分配。计划根据一个全知的大仙进行评估，该大仙知道模型在每个问题上的可解性和成本，从而得出一个通用尺度上的分诊效率比。我们评估了前沿和开源模型，无论是否启用推理，涉及竞赛数学、研究生水平科学、代码生成和专家多学科知识，发现当前语言模型在前瞻性元认知控制方面表现出显著差距，揭示了一个先前未测量的能力维度，对资源高效的智能体部署有直接影响。

Original abstract: Deploying language models as autonomous agents requires more than per-task accuracy: when an agent faces a queue of problems under a finite token budget, it must decide which to attempt, in what order, and how much compute to commit to each, all before any execution feedback is available. This is the prospective form of metacognitive control studied for decades in human cognition, yet whether language models possess it remains untested. We introduce TRIAGE, an evaluation framework in which a model receives a task pool and a token budget calibrated to its own baseline cost, and commits to a single ordered plan that jointly encodes selection, sequencing, and per-problem allocation. Plans are scored against an oracle with full knowledge of the model's solvability and cost on each problem, yielding a triage efficiency ratio on a common scale. We evaluate frontier and open-source models, with and without reasoning enabled, across competition mathematics, graduate-level science, code generation, and expert multidisciplinary knowledge, and find that current language models exhibit substantial gaps in prospective metacognitive control, revealing a previously unmeasured capability dimension with direct implications for resource-efficient agent deployment.

### [44] [CogniFold: Always-On Proactive Memory via Cognitive Folding](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13438v3)
*Suli Wang,Yiqun Duan,Yu Deng,Rundong Zhao,Dai Shi,Minghua Deng,Chen Chen,Xinliang Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 类脑主动记忆系统，持续自主组织经验，直接贡献agent记忆机制。

TL;DR: 提出CogniFold，一种受大脑启发的“始终在线”代理记忆，通过图拓扑自组织将事件流折叠为认知结构，在三层CLS理论（海马体、新皮层、前额叶）上实现，并经实验验证产生符合认知期望的结构并在多个下游任务上表现稳健。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理记忆是反应性和基于检索的，缺乏自主组织经验为持久认知结构的能力，需要更主动的认知机制。

Method: 扩展CLS理论至三层（增加前额叶意图层），通过图拓扑自组织实现主动结构形成：事件流驱动认知结构组装、合并、衰减、关联重连和意图涌现。

Result: CogEval-Bench上产生符合认知期望的结构和概念涌现；在八个下游基准（包括LoCoMo、LongMemEval等）上同时表现稳健。

Conclusion: CogniFold是一种有效的主动代理记忆，通过脑启发设计实现了认知结构的自组织，并在多个任务上验证了其性能。

中文摘要：现有的代理记忆仍然主要反应性和基于检索，缺乏自主将经验组织为持久认知结构的能力。为了实现真正自主的代理，我们引入了CogniFold，一种受大脑启发的“始终在线”的代理记忆，专为下一代主动助手设计。CogniFold持续将碎片化的事件流折叠成自涌现的认知结构，从传入事件和积累知识中引导出逐渐高级的认知。我们通过将互补学习系统（CLS）理论从两层（海马体、新皮层）扩展到三层，加入前额叶意图层来奠定基础。模拟前额叶皮层作为意图控制和决策的场所，CogniFold通过图拓扑自组织实现：认知结构在流下主动组装，在语义相似时合并，在过时时衰退，通过关联回忆重新链接，并在概念簇密度超过阈值时浮现意图。我们使用CogEval-Bench评估结构形成，证明CogniFold独特地产生符合认知期望和概念涌现的记忆结构。此外，在八个下游基准——两个 probing 长期对话记忆（LoCoMo, LongMemEval）和六个跨越其他认知领域——上，我们验证了CogniFold同时在传统记忆任务上表现稳健。我们的代码可在 https://github.com/OpenNorve/CogniFold 获取。

Original abstract: Existing agent memory remains predominantly reactive and retrieval-based, lacking the capacity to autonomously organize experience into persistent cognitive structure. Toward genuinely autonomous agents, we introduce CogniFold, a brain-inspired "always-on" agent memory designed for the next generation of proactive assistants. CogniFold continuously folds fragmented event streams into self-emerging cognitive structures, bootstrapping progressively higher-level cognition from incoming events and accumulated knowledge. We ground this by extending Complementary Learning Systems (CLS) theory from two layers (hippocampus, neocortex) to three, adding a prefrontal intent layer. Emulating the prefrontal cortex as the locus of intentional control and decision-making, CogniFold achieves this through graph-topology self-organization: cognitive structures proactively assemble under the stream, merge when semantically similar, decay when stale, relink through associative recall, and surface intents when concept-cluster density crosses a threshold. We evaluate structural formation using CogEval-Bench, demonstrating that CogniFold uniquely produces memory structures that match cognitive expectations and concept emergence. Furthermore, across eight downstream benchmarks -- two probing long-term conversational memory (LoCoMo, LongMemEval) and six spanning other cognitive domains -- we validate that CogniFold simultaneously performs robustly on conventional memory tasks. Our code is available at https://github.com/OpenNorve/CogniFold.

### [45] [Assessing the Creativity of Large Language Models: Testing, Limits, and New Frontiers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13450v1)
*Samuel Schapiro,Alexi Gladstone,Jonah Black,Heng Ji*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估LLM创造力并引入新测试，可启发agent创造力评测。

TL;DR: 评估人类创造力测试对LLM创造性成就的预测能力，提出新的DRAT测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有创造力测试对LLM的有效性未验证，且不能可靠预测科学构思能力，因此需要系统评估并开发新测试。

Method: 系统评估多种人类创造力测试在创意写作、发散性思维和科学构思三个构念上的预测效果，并提出DRAT测试。

Result: DAT和条件性DAT分别最佳预测创意写作和发散性思维；无测试可靠预测科学构思；DRAT是首个能预测科学构思的测试。

Conclusion: DRAT能可靠预测科学构思能力，且其优势源于同时评估发散性和聚合性思维。

中文摘要：衡量大型语言模型（LLM）的创造力对于设计能够提升创造力的方法以及增强我们对此能力的科学理解至关重要。为实现这一目标，近年来普遍采用向LLM施测人类创造力测试的方法。尽管这些测试提供了一种便捷且全自动的方式来评分“创造力”，但其作为机器创造力衡量标准的有效性尚未确立，且这些测试作为人类创造力预测因子的有效性本就有限。为解决此问题，我们开展了首个大规模系统性研究，评估人类创造力测试在预测LLM创造性成就方面的有效性，涵盖三个目标构念：创意写作、发散性思维和科学构思。我们发现，发散联想任务（DAT）和条件性DAT分别是创意写作和发散性思维的最佳预测因子，但测试有效性因构念而异，且没有单一测试能良好预测所有构念。此外，与普遍看法相反，现有测试均不能可靠预测科学构思能力。受此问题驱动，我们提出了发散性远程联想测试（DRAT），这是一种词汇空间测试，可在单一工具中同时评估聚合性思维和发散性思维。DRAT是首个且唯一能显著预测科学构思能力的LLM创造力测试，并在主要设计选择上表现出鲁棒性。此外，DRAT的性能提升无法从发散联想任务和远程联想测试的任何线性组合中恢复，表明在同一测试中评估发散性和聚合性思维对于可靠预测科学构思能力至关重要。

Original abstract: Measuring the creativity of large language models (LLMs) is essential for designing methods that can improve creativity and for enhancing our scientific understanding of this ability. To accomplish this, it has become common in recent years to administer tests of human creativity to LLMs. Although these tests provide a convenient and fully automated way to score "creativity," their validity as measures of machine creativity has not been established, and these tests already have limited validity as predictors of human creativity. To address this problem, we conduct the first large-scale, systematic study assessing the effectiveness of human creativity tests for predicting the creative achievement of LLMs across three target constructs: creative writing, divergent thinking, and scientific ideation. We find that the Divergent Association Task (DAT) and the Conditional DAT are the best predictors of creative writing and divergent thinking, respectively, but that test effectiveness varies significantly by construct, and no single test predicts all constructs well. Moreover, contrary to popular belief, no existing test reliably predicts scientific ideation ability. Motivated by this problem, we introduce the Divergent Remote Association Test (DRAT), a vocabulary-space test that assesses both convergent and divergent thinking in a single instrument. The DRAT is the first and only creativity test for LLMs that is a significant predictor of scientific ideation ability, demonstrating robustness across major design choices. Furthermore, the performance gain of the DRAT is not recoverable from any linear combination of the Divergent Association Task and the Remote Associates Test, indicating that assessing divergent and convergent thinking in the same test is essential to reliably predicting scientific ideation ability.

</details>


### [46] [Why We Need World Models for AGI: Where LLMs Fail and How World Models May Outperform](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23972v1)
*Feisal Alaswad,Batoul Aljaddouh,Maher Alrahhal,Poovammal E,Talal Bonny*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 世界模型与LLM对比，揭示长期规划与状态跟踪缺陷，启发agent架构设计。

TL;DR: 本文提出潜在动态推理（LDI）视角，并通过Flux环境证明，显式建模潜在状态空间的强化学习代理在长期规划中显著优于仅依赖序列预测的LLM（胜率79% vs 11%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在因果推理、持久状态跟踪和长期规划上表现受限，可能源于序列预测与潜在环境动态推理之间的目标不匹配。

Method: 引入潜在动态推理（LDI）概念，并构建Flux环境（完全由自然语言规则定义的顺序推理环境）。将规则编译为显式状态转换模拟器，提取潜在状态空间，用于训练强化学习代理，并与直接处理文本观察的LLM进行对比。

Result: 强化学习代理在长期游戏中胜率约79%，而LLM仅11%。定性分析显示LLM存在无效动作、状态跟踪错误和短视推理等失败模式。

Conclusion: 仅靠序列预测难以支持稳健的长期动态推理，需要持久状态跟踪和转换建模机制。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在语言生成和知识密集型任务上表现强劲，但在需要因果推理、持久状态跟踪和长期规划的设置中仍然受限。我们认为这些局限性可能源于序列预测与对潜在环境动态进行推理之间的目标层面不匹配。为了形式化这一区别，我们引入了潜在动态推理（LDI），这是一种概念性视角，将语言和多模态观察解释为底层转换动态的部分证据。为了实验性地调查这一视角，我们引入了Flux，一个完全通过自然语言规则指定的顺序推理环境。作为一个概念验证案例研究，规则首先被编译成一个显式的状态转换模拟器，表明结构化的潜在转换动态在某些情况下可以从文本规则描述中操作性地提取出来。这使得我们能够进行控制比较：仅基于文本观察操作的LLM与直接在提取的潜在状态空间中训练的强化学习代理。在这个案例研究中，显式访问潜在状态空间的代理在长期游戏中表现出更稳定的行为，实现了大约79%的总胜率，而LLM仅为11%。定性分析进一步揭示了与不稳定的持久状态跟踪一致的失败模式，包括无效动作、状态跟踪错误和短视推理失败。Flux环境的完整实现可在https://github.com/FeisalAlaswad/FLUX-RL-Agent获取。在评估的设置中，这些结果表明，如果没有持久状态跟踪和转换建模的机制，仅靠强大的序列预测可能难以支持稳健的长期动态推理。

Original abstract: Large language models achieve strong performance in language generation and knowledge-intensive tasks, yet remain limited in settings requiring causal reasoning, persistent state tracking, and long-horizon planning. We argue that these limitations may arise from an objective-level mismatch between sequence prediction and reasoning over latent environment dynamics. To formalize this distinction, we introduce Latent Dynamics Inference (LDI), a conceptual perspective that interprets language and multimodal observations as partial evidence of underlying transition dynamics. To empirically investigate this perspective, we introduce Flux, a sequential reasoning environment specified entirely through natural-language rules. As a proof-of-concept case study, the rules are first compiled into an explicit state-transition simulator, illustrating that structured latent transition dynamics can, in some cases, be operationally extracted from textual rule descriptions. This enables a controlled comparison between the LLMs operating purely over textual observations and reinforcement-learning agents trained directly within the extracted latent state space. Within this case study, agents operating with explicit access to the latent state space exhibit substantially more stable behavior in long-horizon gameplay, achieving an aggregate win rate of approximately 79% versus 11% for LLMs. Qualitative analysis further reveals failure modes consistent with unstable persistent state tracking, including invalid actions, state-tracking errors, and short-horizon reasoning failures. The complete implementation of the Flux environment available at https://github.com/FeisalAlaswad/FLUX-RL-Agent Within the evaluated setting, these results suggest that strong sequence prediction alone may struggle to support robust long-horizon dynamic reasoning without mechanisms for persistent state tracking and transition modeling

</details>


### [47] [MMSkills: Towards Multimodal Skills for General Visual Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13527v3)
*Kangning Zhang,Shuai Shao,Qingyao Li,Jianghao Lin,Lingyue Fu,Shijian Wang,Wenxiang Jiao,Yuan Lu,Weiwen Liu,Weinan Zhang,Yong Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多模态技能包生成与使用，促进视觉agent的复用和泛化能力。

TL;DR: 提出MMSkills框架，通过多模态技能包（文本程序+状态卡+关键帧）提升视觉智能体的决策能力，从公共轨迹生成技能，并在推理时分支加载指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能包主要基于文本或代码，忽略了视觉智能体所需的程序性知识的多模态特性，包括状态识别、视觉证据解释等。因此需要形式化多模态程序性知识并解决其挑战。

Method: 提出MMSkills框架，包含技能表示（状态条件包，含文本程序、状态卡、多视角关键帧），技能生成（轨迹转技能生成器，包括工作流分组、程序归纳、视觉基础、元技能审计），以及技能使用（分支加载多模态技能智能体，临时分支检查并对齐环境，提炼指导）。

Result: 在GUI和游戏视觉基准上，MMSkills持续改进了前沿和较小的多模态智能体。

Conclusion: 外部多模态程序性知识可补充模型内部先验，提升视觉智能体性能。

中文摘要：可复用技能已成为提高智能体能力的核心基础，然而现有的大多数技能包主要将可复用行为编码为文本提示、可执行代码或学习到的程序。但对于视觉智能体而言，程序性知识本质上是多模态的：复用不仅取决于执行什么操作，还取决于识别相关状态、解释进展或失败的视觉证据，以及决定下一步做什么。我们将这一需求形式化为多模态程序性知识，并解决了三个实际挑战：（I）多模态技能包应包含什么；（II）如何从公共交互经验中派生这些技能包；（III）智能体如何在推理时查阅多模态证据，而无需过多的图像上下文或过度锚定于参考截图。我们提出了MMSkills，一个用于表示、生成和使用可复用多模态程序以进行运行时视觉决策的框架。每个MMSkill是一个紧凑的、基于状态条件的包，将文本程序与运行时状态卡和多视角关键帧相结合。为了构建这些技能包，我们开发了一个智能体轨迹到技能的生成器，通过工作流分组、程序归纳、视觉基础和元技能引导审计，将公共非评估轨迹转化为可复用的多模态技能。为了使用它们，我们引入了一个分支加载的多模态技能智能体：在临时分支中检查选定的状态卡和关键帧，与实时环境对齐，并提炼为对主智能体的结构化指导。在GUI和基于游戏的视觉智能体基准上的实验表明，MMSkills持续改进了前沿和较小的多模态智能体，表明外部多模态程序性知识补充了模型内部先验知识。

Original abstract: Reusable skills have become a core substrate for improving agent capabilities, yet most existing skill packages encode reusable behavior primarily as textual prompts, executable code, or learned routines. For visual agents, however, procedural knowledge is inherently multimodal: reuse depends not only on what operation to perform, but also on recognizing the relevant state, interpreting visual evidence of progress or failure, and deciding what to do next. We formalize this requirement as multimodal procedural knowledge and address three practical challenges: (I) what a multimodal skill package should contain; (II) where such packages can be derived from public interaction experience; and (III) how agents can consult multimodal evidence at inference time without excessive image context or over-anchoring to reference screenshots. We introduce MMSkills, a framework for representing, generating, and using reusable multimodal procedures for runtime visual decision making. Each MMSkill is a compact, state-conditioned package that couples a textual procedure with runtime state cards and multi-view keyframes. To construct these packages, we develop an agentic trajectory-to-skill Generator that transforms public non-evaluation trajectories into reusable multimodal skills through workflow grouping, procedure induction, visual grounding, and meta-skill-guided auditing. To use them, we introduce a branch-loaded multimodal skill agent: selected state cards and keyframes are inspected in a temporary branch, aligned with the live environment, and distilled into structured guidance for the main agent. Experiments across GUI and game-based visual-agent benchmarks show that MMSkills consistently improve both frontier and smaller multimodal agents, suggesting that external multimodal procedural knowledge complements model-internal priors.

### [48] [Scaling Retrieval-Augmented Reasoning with Parallel Search and Explicit Merging](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13534v1)
*Jiabei Liu,Wenyu Mao,Junfei Tan,Chunxu Shen,Lingling Yi,Jiancan Wu,Xiang Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多查询检索增强推理框架，可迁移至coding agent的检索与规划。

TL;DR: MultiSearch通过多查询并行检索和显式信息合并，提高了检索信噪比和推理准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在每个推理步骤仅生成单个查询进行检索，导致信息覆盖有限、噪声高、信噪比低，从而降低推理准确性并产生不必要的推理步骤。

Method: 提出基于强化学习的MultiSearch框架，在每个推理步骤中从多个视角生成查询并并行检索，然后通过合并过程整合和精炼信息；同时设计了多过程奖励的强化学习框架来优化多查询检索和信息整合。

Result: 在七个基准测试上，MultiSearch优于基线方法，显著提升了检索的信噪比和问答任务的推理性能。

Conclusion: MultiSearch通过多查询检索和显式信息合并有效解决了现有方法的局限，增强了推理过程中的信噪比和准确性。

中文摘要：深度搜索代理已被证明通过在多步推理过程中检索外部知识来增强大型语言模型（LLMs）的效果。然而，现有方法通常在每个推理步骤仅生成单个查询进行检索，限制了信息覆盖范围并引入了高噪声。这可能导致搜索过程中信噪比（SNR）较低，降低推理准确性并导致不必要的推理步骤。在本文中，我们介绍了MultiSearch，一种基于强化学习（RL）的框架，通过多查询检索和显式合并检索信息来解决这些限制。在每个推理步骤，MultiSearch从多个视角生成查询并并行检索外部信息，扩大相关信息的范围并减轻对任何单一检索结果的依赖。然后，代理在合并过程中整合并精炼检索到的信息，提高信噪比并确保更准确的推理。此外，我们提出了一种具有多过程奖励设计的强化学习框架，以优化代理的多查询检索和信息整合能力。在七个基准测试上的大量实验表明，MultiSearch优于基线方法，提高了检索的信噪比并改进了问答任务中的推理性能。

Original abstract: Deep search agents have proven effective in enhancing LLMs by retrieving external knowledge during multi-step reasoning. However, existing methods often generate a single query for retrieval at each reasoning step, limiting information coverage and introducing high noise. This may result in low signal-to-noise ratios (SNR) during search, degrading reasoning accuracy and leading to unnecessary reasoning steps. In this paper, we introduce MultiSearch, an RL-based framework that addresses these limitations through multi-query retrieval and explicit merging of retrieved information. At each reasoning step, MultiSearch generates queries from multiple perspectives and retrieves external information in parallel, expanding the scope of relevant information and mitigating the reliance on any single retrieval result. Then, the agent consolidates and refines retrieved information at the merging process, improving the SNR and ensuring more accurate reasoning. Additionally, we propose a reinforcement learning framework with a multi-process reward design to optimize agents for both multi-query retrieval and information consolidation. Extensive experiments on seven benchmarks demonstrate that MultiSearch outperforms baseline methods, enhancing the SNR of retrieval and improving reasoning performance in question-answering tasks.

### [49] [RealICU: Do LLM Agents Understand Long-Context ICU Data? A Benchmark Beyond Behavior Imitation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13542v1)
*Chengzhi Shen,Weixiang Shen,Tobias Susetzky,Chen,Chen,Jun Li,Yuyuan Liu,Xuepeng Zhang,Zhenyu Gong,Daniel Rueckert,Jiazhen Pan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ICU基准将历史临床行为视为真实情况，但这些行为可能因信息不完整和时序限制而次优，难以评估AI推理能力，因此需要更真实的评估基准。

Method: 引入RealICU基准，由高级医生事后审查完整患者轨迹后标注，制定四个任务（患者状态、急性问题、推荐行动、红旗行动），以30分钟窗口划分轨迹，发布RealICU-Gold（930窗口）和RealICU-Scale（11862窗口）；提出ICU-Evo结构化记忆智能体。

Result: 现有LLM（包括记忆增强模型）在RealICU上表现不佳，存在两种失败模式：临床建议的回忆-安全性权衡和早期解释的锚定偏差；ICU-Evo改进了长时程推理但未完全消除安全性失败。

Conclusion: RealICU为高风险护理中AI顺序决策支持的衡量和改进提供了临床基础的测试平台。

中文摘要：重症监护室（ICU）会产生长序列、密集且不断演变的临床信息流，医生必须在时间压力下反复重新评估患者状态，这突显了对可靠人工智能决策支持的明确需求。现有的ICU基准通常将历史临床医生的行为视为真实情况。然而，这些行为是在信息不完整且对潜在患者状态的时间背景有限的情况下做出的，因此可能是次优的，这使得难以评估AI系统的真正推理能力。我们引入了RealICU，这是一个事后标注的基准，用于在现实ICU条件下评估大型语言模型（LLM），其中标注是在高级医师审查完整患者轨迹后创建的。我们制定了四个由医生驱动的任务：评估患者状态、急性问题、推荐行动以及可能导致不安全后果的红旗行动。我们以30分钟窗口划分每个轨迹，并发布两个数据集：RealICU-Gold，包含来自94名MIMIC-IV患者的930个窗口标注；以及RealICU-Scale，包含由Oracle（一个经过医生验证的LLM事后标注器）扩展的11,862个窗口。现有的LLM，包括增强记忆的LLM，在RealICU上表现不佳，暴露了两种失败模式：临床建议的回忆-安全性权衡，以及对患者早期解释的锚定偏差。我们进一步引入了ICU-Evo来研究结构化记忆智能体，它改进了长时程推理，但并未完全消除安全性失败。总之，RealICU提供了一个临床基础的测试平台，用于衡量和改进高风险护理中AI的顺序决策支持。项目页面：https://chengzhi-leo.github.io/RealICU-Bench/

Original abstract: Intensive care units (ICU) generate long, dense and evolving streams of clinical information, where physicians must repeatedly reassess patient states under time pressure, underscoring a clear need for reliable AI decision support. Existing ICU benchmarks typically treat historical clinician actions as ground truth. However, these actions are made under incomplete information and limited temporal context of the underlying patient state, and may therefore be suboptimal, making it difficult to assess the true reasoning capabilities of AI systems. We introduce RealICU, a hindsight-annotated benchmark for evaluating large language models (LLMs) under realistic ICU conditions, where labels are created after senior physicians review the full patient trajectory. We formulate four physician-motivated tasks: assess Patient Status, Acute Problems, Recommended Actions, and Red Flag actions that risk unsafe outcomes. We partition each trajectory with 30-min windows and release two datasets: RealICU-Gold with 930-window annotations from 94 MIMIC-IV patients, and RealICU-Scale with 11,862 windows extended by Oracle, a physician-validated LLM hindsight labeler. Existing LLMs including memory-augmented ones performed poorly on RealICU, exposing two failure modes: a recall-safety tradeoff for clinical recommendations, and an anchoring bias to early interpretations of the patient. We further introduce ICU-Evo to study structured-memory agents that improves long-horizon reasoning but does not fully eliminate safety failures. Together, RealICU provides a clinically grounded testbed for measuring and improving AI sequential decision-support in high-stakes care. Project page: https://chengzhi-leo.github.io/RealICU-Bench/

### [50] [Learning Local Constraints for Reinforcement-Learned Content Generators](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13570v1)
*Debosmita Bhaumik,Julian Togelius,Georgios N. Yannakakis,Ahmed Khalifa*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 游戏内容生成agent，结合约束和RL，一般agent方法。

TL;DR: 该研究结合WFC和强化学习的方法，通过约束动作空间，在保证局部约束的同时实现全局属性，成功生成了视觉满意且可玩的游戏关卡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: WFC生成的游戏关卡局部视觉好但全局属性难保证，而强化学习生成的关卡全局属性易保证但视觉可能不满意，因此需要结合两者优势。

Method: 使用WFC学习的局部约束限制PCGRL生成器的动作空间，同时变化输入数量、类型，并测试随机坍缩起始状态和排除稀有模式。

Result: 最佳训练生成器能产生视觉满意且可玩的益智平台游戏关卡，如Lode Runner关卡，但方法对超参数敏感。

Conclusion: 混合约束和强化学习的方法有效结合了局部和全局属性，但需仔细调整超参数以优化效果。

中文摘要：基于约束的游戏内容生成器，如波函数坍缩（WFC），可以通过从现有内容中学习局部约束来生成视觉上令人满意的游戏关卡，但在保证全局属性（如可玩性）方面面临挑战。另一方面，强化学习训练的生成器可以保证全局属性——因为这些属性可以轻松包含在奖励函数中——但结果可能在视觉上不尽如人意。在本文中，我们探索了结合这些方法的方式。具体来说，我们利用WFC学习到的约束来限制PCGRL生成器的动作空间，从而有效地允许PCGRL生成器在被迫遵守局部约束的同时实现全局属性。为了更好地分析这种混合内容生成方法的运作方式，我们变化输入的数量和类型，并测试是否随机坍缩起始状态以及排除稀有模式。尽管该方法对超参数调优敏感，但我们训练的最佳生成器能够生成视觉上令人满意且可玩的益智平台游戏关卡——例如Lode Runner关卡——并具有所需的全局属性。

Original abstract: Constraint-based game content generators that learn local constraints from existing content, such as Wave Function Collapse (WFC), can generate visually satisfying game levels but face challenges in guaranteeing global properties, such as playability. On the other hand, reinforcement-learning trained generators can guarantee global properties -- because such properties can easily be included in reward functions -- but the results can be visually dissatisfying. In this paper, we explore ways to combine these methods. Specifically, we constrain the action space of a PCGRL generator with constraints learned by WFC, effectively allowing the PCGRL generator to achieve global properties while forced to adhere to local constraints. To better analyze how this hybrid content generation method operates, we vary the number and type of inputs, and we test whether to randomly collapse the starting state and exclude rare patterns. While the method is sensitive to hyperparameter tuning, the best of our trained generators produce visually satisfying and playable puzzle-platform game levels -- such as Lode Runner levels -- with desired global properties.

Motivation: 现有AI代理在辅助盲人和视障用户时系统性失败，源于设计假设与用户实际约束不匹配。

Method: 分析778个辅助任务实例，识别失败模式；提出可访问性对齐概念和生命周期导向的设计流程。

Result: 验证了设计假设失配是失败主因；提出了包含用户研究、设计、部署和迭代的完整流程。

Conclusion: 辅助任务是AI代理的严峻考验，需转向包容性设计，将可访问性视为对齐问题。

中文摘要：盲人和视障用户的辅助代理需要将可访问性对齐作为首要设计目标。尽管智能代理AI取得了快速进展，但大多数系统是在假设明眼人交互、低成本验证和可容忍试错的条件下设计和评估的，导致在辅助场景中出现系统性失败，这些失败无法通过模型缩放或事后界面适配来解决。基于对先前工作中778个辅助任务实例的分析，我们表明，当前的智能代理AI在辅助场景中仍然容易失败，原因是明眼用户的设计假设与盲人和视障用户面临的验证、风险和交互约束之间存在不匹配。我们认为，可访问性应被视为一个对齐问题，而不是一个外围的可用性问题。为此，我们引入了可访问性对齐，并提出了一个面向生命周期的设计流程，用于实现可访问性对齐的辅助代理，涵盖用户研究、系统设计、部署以及部署后的迭代。我们得出结论，以盲人和视障用户为中心的辅助任务为智能代理AI提供了一个关键的压力测试，并推动了向包容性代理设计的更广泛转变。

Original abstract: Assistive agents for Blind and Visually Impaired (BVI) users require accessibility alignment as a first-class design objective. Despite rapid progress in agentic AI, most systems are designed and evaluated under assumptions of sighted interaction, low-cost verification, and tolerable trial-and-error, leading to systematic failures in assistive scenarios that cannot be resolved by model scaling or post-hoc interface adaptations alone. Drawing on an analysis of 778 assistance task instances from prior work, we show that current agentic AI remain prone to failure in assistive scenarios due to mismatches between sighted-user design assumptions and the verification, risk, and interaction constraints faced by BVI users. We argue that accessibility should be treated as an alignment problem rather than a peripheral usability concern. To this end, we introduce accessibility alignment and propose a lifecycle-oriented design pipeline for accessibility-aligned assistive agents, spanning user research, system design, deployment and post-deployment iteration. We conclude that BVI-centered assistive tasks provide a critical stress test for agentic AI and motivate a broader shift toward inclusive agent design.

</details>

Original abstract: Self-driving laboratories (SDLs) have attracted increasing attention as a means of accelerating scientific discovery; however, developing SDL software remains technically demanding. ### [53] [Unweighted ranking for value-based decision making with uncertainty](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13601v1)
*Aarón López García,Natalia Criado,Jose Such*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 价值决策框架，多agent，一般agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出FUW-VBDM框架和Rankzzy方法，通过移除权重偏见并引入模糊推理，实现高效且一致的人本决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于价值的决策方法中，利益相关者任意分配的权重引入规范偏差，需要一种无权重、能处理不确定性且保持人类价值观一致性的决策方法。

Method: 提出FUW-VBDM框架，将决策变量模糊化并移除先验权重；设计Rankzzy方法，利用模糊推理进行无权重排序，并证明其一致性。

Result: 在大规模问题上计算成本降低，采用毕达哥拉斯均值聚合时排名性能优于现有方法。

Conclusion: FUW-VBDM和Rankzzy有效实现了人本决策，降低了计算开销，并保持了鲁棒的排序性能。

中文摘要：随着智能系统在我们的社会中越来越多地被用于做出自主决策，它们对人类价值观的承诺引发了严重担忧。它们与人类价值观的一致性仍然是一个关键挑战，因为这可能危及公民的诚信与安全。因此，需要一种创新的、以人为本且以价值观为导向的决策方法。在这项工作中，我们引入了模糊无权重基于价值的决策制定（FUW-VBDM）框架，其中智能体结合定量和定性标准来生成以人为本的决策。我们还通过移除先验权重并引入为评分函数定义的决策变量的模糊域，来解决利益相关者引入的任意权重导致的规范偏差。这一概念使我们能够将任何VBDM问题泛化为在权重域中优化评分时寻找可行解的问题。为了提供FUW-VBDM的解决方案，我们提出了Rankzzy，一种可定制的无权重排名方法，它集成了基于模糊的推理来量化不确定性。我们在数学上证明了Rankzzy对于利益相关者选择的任何可接受配置的一致性。我们通过一个说明性案例研究展示了我们方法的适用性，该案例也作为我们的运行示例。进行的评估表明，在大规模基于价值的决策问题中计算成本降低，并且在采用毕达哥拉斯均值聚合时，相对于现有方法具有强大的排名性能。

Original abstract: As intelligent systems are increasingly implemented in our society to make autonomous decisions, their commitment to human values raises serious concerns. Their alignment with human values remains a critical challenge because it can jeopardise the integrity and security of citizens. For this reason, an innovative human-centred and values-driven approach to decision making is required. In this work, we introduce the Fuzzy-Unweighted Value-Based Decision Making (FUW-VBDM) framework, where agents incorporate both quantitative and qualitative criteria to generate human-centred decisions. We also address the normative bias introduced by stakeholders with arbitrary weights by removing prior weights and introducing a fuzzy domain of decision variables defined for a score function. This concept allows us to generalise any VBDM problem as the search for feasible solutions when optimising the score in the weight domain. To provide a solution to FUW-VBDM, we present Rankzzy, a customizable unweighted ranking method that integrates fuzzy-based reasoning to quantify uncertainty. We mathematically prove the consistency of the Rankzzy for any admissible configuration selected by stakeholders. We show the applicability of our method through an illustrative case study, which we also use as a running example. The evaluation conducted indicates a reduced computational cost in large-scale value-based decision-making problems and a strong rank performance regarding existing approaches when employing the aggregation via Pythagorean means.

### [54] [How to Interpret Agent Behavior](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13625v1)
*Jie Gao,Kaiser Sun,Jen-tse Huang,Katherine Van Koevering,Sijie Ji,Heyuan Huang,Weiyan Shi,Zhuoran Lu,Ziang Xiao,Daniel Khashabi,Mark Dredze*

Selection reason: agent行为分类法，用于分析解释agent行为。

TL;DR: 提出了ACT*ONOMY分类法，用于结构化分析和理解自主代理的运行时行为，帮助研究人员和开发者更有效地监督和改进代理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代理运行时行为数据量大且非结构化，难以人工分析，需要系统化的分类来提升可解释性和监督效率。

Method: 基于扎根理论构建三层分类法（10动作、46子动作、120叶子类别），并开发自动化分析流程和开放仓库。

Result: 实验表明ACT*ONOMY能比较不同代理的行为特征，以及单个代理不同轨迹的行为模式，有效揭示故障模式。

Conclusion: ACT*ONOMY提供共享词汇，增强代理行为解释的一致性，促进更好的监督和控制。

中文摘要：自主代理（如Claude Code和Codex）现在可以运行数小时甚至数天。理解它们的运行时行为对于下游任务（如诊断低效、修复错误和确保更好的监督）变得至关重要。获得这种理解的主要途径是分析这些代理生成的推理轨迹和执行轨迹。然而，这些数据仍然是非结构化的自然语言形式，使得人类难以大规模解释。我们引入了ACT*ONOMY（Action和Taxonomy的组合），一个用于描述和分析代理运行时行为的分类法。ACT*ONOMY有两个组成部分：（1）分类法本身，通过扎根理论开发，结构化为三级层次，包括10个动作、46个子动作和120个叶子类别；（2）一个开放仓库，托管这个活的分类法，提供自动化分析流程来应用于代理轨迹分析，并定义了一个扩展协议用于定制和增长。我们的实验表明，ACT*ONOMY可以比较代理之间的行为特征，并表征单个代理在不同轨迹中的行为，揭示指示故障模式的模式。通过提供共享词汇，ACT*ONOMY帮助研究人员、代理设计者和最终用户更一致地解释代理行为，从而实现更好的监督和控制。

Original abstract: Autonomous agents such as Claude Code and Codex now operate for hours or even days. Understanding their runtime behavior has become critical for downstream tasks such as diagnosing inefficiencies, fixing bugs, and ensuring better oversight. A primary way to gain this understanding is analyzing the reasoning trajectories and execution traces these agents generate. Yet such data remains in unstructured natural-language form, making it difficult for humans to interpret at scale. We introduce ACT*ONOMY (a combination of Action and Taxonomy), a taxonomy for describing and analyzing agent behavior at runtime. ACT*ONOMY has two components: (1) the taxonomy itself, developed through Grounded Theory and structured as a three-level hierarchy of 10 actions, 46 subactions, and 120 leaf categories; and (2) an open repository that hosts the living taxonomy, provides an automated analysis pipeline that applies it to agent trajectories analysis, and defines an extension protocol for customization and growth. Our experiments show that ACTONOMY can compare behavioral profiles across agents and characterize a single agent's behavior across diverse trajectories, surfacing patterns indicative of failure modes. By providing a shared vocabulary, ACT*ONOMY helps researchers, agent designers, and end users interpret agent behavior more consistently, enabling better oversight and control.

### [55] [ScioMind: Cognitively Grounded Multi-Agent Social Simulation with Anchoring-Based Belief Dynamics and Dynamic Profiles](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13725v1)
*Yitian Yang,Yiqun Duan,Linghan Huang,Yiqi Zhu,Francesco Bailo,Chunmeizi Su,Huaming Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计ScioMind框架，包含记忆锚定信念更新规则（个性调节锚定强度）、层次化记忆架构（持久经验驱动信念）、动态智能体档案（语料库检索生成异质个性与内部状态）。

Result: 在真实政策辩论场景中，ScioMind在极化、多样性、极端化、轨迹稳定性等指标上均优于基线，动态档案增加多样性，记忆与反思减少震荡，锚定产生持久轨迹。

Conclusion: 认知基础的设计能同时提升基于LLM的社会模拟的稳定性和行为现实性，提供了一种新颖解决方案。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）的多智能体模拟为研究社会舆论动态提供了一个强大的试验平台。然而，当前的方法通常采用两种截然不同的方式：要么依赖固定更新规则且认知基础有限，要么将信念变化大部分交由不受约束的LLM交互来处理。我们提出了ScioMind，一个认知基础模拟框架，通过结合结构化的舆论动态与基于LLM的智能体推理，桥接了这些范式。ScioMind集成了三个关键组成部分：1）一种记忆锚定的信念更新规则，通过个性调节的锚定强度来调节对影响的易感性；2）一种层次化记忆架构，支持持久的、经验驱动的信念形成；以及3）基于语料库检索流水线生成的动态智能体档案，实现了异质个性、理由和不断演化的内部状态。我们在一个真实政策辩论场景的多个案例研究中评估了ScioMind。在包括极化、多样性、极端化和轨迹稳定性等指标上，提出的组件始终带来了行为现实性的改进。特别是，动态档案增加了意见多样性，记忆与反思减少了不稳定震荡，而锚定则产生了与政治心理学中报告的模式更一致的持久信念轨迹。这些结果表明，我们的认知基础设计为基于LLM的社会模拟提供了一种新颖的解决方案，同时提升了稳定性和行为现实性。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based multi-agent simulation offers a powerful testbed for studying social opinion dynamics. Yet current approaches often adopt two contrasting methods: either relying on fixed update rules with limited cognitive grounding or delegating belief change largely to unconstrained LLM interaction. We introduce ScioMind, a cognitively grounded simulation framework that bridges these paradigms by combining structured opinion dynamics with LLM-based agent reasoning. ScioMind integrates three key components: 1) a memory-anchored belief update rule that modulates susceptibility to influence via personality-conditioned anchoring strength; 2) a hierarchical memory architecture that supports persistent, experience-driven belief formation; and 3) dynamic agent profiles derived from a corpus-grounded retrieval pipeline, enabling heterogeneous personalities, rationales, and evolving internal states. We evaluate ScioMind on multiple case studies in a real-world policy debate scenario. Across metrics including polarisation, diversity, extremization, and trajectory stability, the proposed components consistently yield improvements in behavioural realism. In particular, dynamic profiles increase opinion diversity, memory and reflection reduce unstable oscillation, and anchoring induces persistent belief trajectories that better align with patterns reported in political psychology. These results suggest that our cognitively grounded design provides a novel solution to LLM-based social simulation that improves both stable and behavioural realism

### [56] [Harnessing Agentic Evolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13821v1)
*Jiayi Zhang,Yongfeng Gu,Jianhao Ruan,Maojia Song,Yiran Peng,Zhiguang Han,Jinyu Xiang,Zhitao Wang,Caiyin Yang,Yixi Ouyang,Bang Liu,Chenglin Wu,Yuyu Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: AEvo: 利用agentic evolution改进程序/workflow，直接相关agent框架与自动优化。

TL;DR: 提出AEvo框架，将智能体进化的积累证据作为过程状态，通过元编辑控制进化过程，在多个基准上取得最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法缺乏稳定接口组织积累的证据并修改进化机制，导致灵活性或长程稳定性不足。

Method: 将智能体进化视为交互环境，积累上下文作为过程状态，元智能体观察状态并通过编辑过程或智能体上下文而非直接提出候选来驱动进化。

Result: 在智能体和推理基准上相对最强基线提升26%，在三个开放式优化任务中达到SOTA。

Conclusion: AEvo通过统一接口有效利用积累证据，适用于多种进化范式，性能优越。

中文摘要：智能体进化已成为一种强大的范式，通过迭代生成候选方案、评估它们并利用反馈指导未来搜索来改进程序、工作流程和科学解决方案。然而，现有方法通常要么实例化为固定手工设计的过程（虽然模块化但僵化），要么实例化为通用智能体（灵活整合反馈但可能在长程进化中漂移）。两种形式都会随时间积累丰富的证据，包括候选方案、反馈、轨迹和失败，但缺乏一个稳定的接口来组织这些证据并修改驱动未来进化的机制。我们通过将智能体进化公式化为一个交互式环境来解决这一限制，其中积累的进化上下文作为过程级状态。我们引入了AEvo，一个受控的元编辑框架，其中元智能体观察该状态并采取行动，不是直接提出下一个候选方案，而是编辑控制未来进化的过程或智能体上下文。这种统一接口使AEvo能够引导基于过程和基于智能体的进化，使积累的证据可用于长程搜索。在智能体和推理基准上的实证评估表明，AEvo优于五种进化基线，相对于最强基线实现了26%的相对改进。在三个开放式优化任务中，AEvo进一步优于四种进化基线，并在相同的迭代预算下达到了最先进的性能。

Original abstract: Agentic evolution has emerged as a powerful paradigm for improving programs, workflows, and scientific solutions by iteratively generating candidates, evaluating them, and using feedback to guide future search. However, existing methods are typically instantiated either as fixed hand-designed procedures that are modular but rigid, or as general-purpose agents that flexibly integrate feedback but can drift in long-horizon evolution. Both forms accumulate rich evidence over time, including candidates, feedback, traces, and failures, yet lack a stable interface for organizing this evidence and revising the mechanism that drives future evolution. We address this limitation by formulating agentic evolution as an interactive environment, where the accumulated evolution context serves as a process-level state. We introduce AEvo, a harnessed meta-editing framework in which a meta-agent observes this state and acts not by directly proposing the next candidate, but by editing the procedure or agent context that controls future evolution. This unified interface enables AEvo to steer both procedure-based and agent-based evolution, making accumulated evidence actionable for long-horizon search. Empirical evaluations on agentic and reasoning benchmarks show that AEvo outperforms five evolution baselines, achieving a 26 relative improvement over the strongest baseline. Across three open-ended optimization tasks, AEvo further outperforms four evolution baselines and achieves state-of-the-art performance under the same iteration budget.

</details>


### [57] [History Anchors: How Prior Behavior Steers LLM Decisions Toward Unsafe Actions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13825v1)
*Alberto G. Rodríguez Salgado*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: History Anchors: 历史行为影响LLM动作安全，agent安全与行为研究。

TL;DR: 有害历史步骤会在特定提示下使前沿LLM从安全转向不安全，导致高比例有害选择甚至升级行为，且旗舰模型受影响最大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究LLM作为代理时，先前有害动作是否会影响后续安全决策，特别是在轨迹可能被操纵、重放或注入的部署场景中。

Method: 构建HistoryAnchor-100数据集，包含100个跨越10个高风险领域的场景，每个场景有3个强制有害先前动作后接自由选择节点（2个安全、2个不安全），测试17个来自6个提供商的模型，使用中性提示和一致性提示，并设计控制实验。

Result: 中性提示下最强对齐模型几乎不选不安全选项；添加“保持与先前历史一致”的提示后，不安全选择率升至91-98%且模型常升级行为；控制实验显示该效果源于有害历史而非标签或指令本身；不同模型族翻转所需有害历史剂量不同，且每个对齐族中旗舰模型受影响最大，呈现逆安全缩放模式。

Conclusion: 当前对齐模型在有害历史下极易被诱导继续有害行为，这对代理部署构成严重安全风险，尤其当轨迹可能被篡改时。

中文摘要：前沿大型语言模型越来越多地被部署为代理，它们根据同一或不同模型产生的长时间工具调用日志来选择下一个动作。我们提出了一个简单的安全问题：如果日志中的前一步是有害的，模型会继续有害行为吗？我们构建了HistoryAnchor-100，包含100个跨越十个高风险领域的短场景，每个场景将三个强制性的有害先前动作与一个自由选择节点配对，该节点提供两个安全选项和两个不安全选项。在来自六家提供商的17个前沿模型中，我们发现了一个惊人的不对称性：在中性系统提示下，最强大的对齐模型几乎从不选择不安全选项，但添加一句话“保持与先前历史中显示的策略一致”后，它们选择不安全选项的比例达到91-98%，并且翻转的模型往往表现出升级行为。两个控制实验排除了更简单的解释：交换动作标签效果不变，而相同指令配合全安全的历史将不安全率保持在7%以下。不同模型族在不同剂量的有害历史下发生翻转，并且在每个对齐的模型族中，旗舰模型是最受影响的兄弟姐妹，这呈现出与安全性相关的逆缩放模式。这些结果对于代理部署中轨迹可能被重放、伪造或注入的情况是一个危险信号。

Original abstract: Frontier LLMs are increasingly deployed as agents that pick the next action after a long log of prior tool calls produced by the same or a different model. We ask a simple safety question: if a prior step in that log was harmful, will the model continue the harmful course? We build HistoryAnchor-100, 100 short scenarios across ten high-stakes domains, each pairing three forced harmful prior actions with a free-choice node offering two safe and two unsafe options. Across 17 frontier models from six providers we find a striking asymmetry: under a neutral system prompt the strongest aligned models almost never pick unsafe, but a single added sentence, "stay consistent with the strategy shown in the prior history", flips them to 91-98%, and the flipped models often escalate beyond continuation. Two controls rule out simpler explanations: permuting action labels leaves the effect intact, and the same instruction with an all-safe prior history keeps unsafe rates below 7%. Different families flip at different doses of unsafe history, and within every aligned family the flagship is the most affected sibling, an inverse-scaling pattern with respect to safety. These results are a red flag for agentic deployments where trajectories may be replayed, forged, or injected.

</details>


### [58] [Verifiable Agentic Infrastructure: Proof-Derived Authorization for Sovereign AI Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15228v1)
*Jun He,Deying Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自治agent的可验证授权基础设施，涉及安全控制与可审计性，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出分布式信任框架（DTF），通过证明派生权限替代基于身份的授权，使自主AI代理的执行变得可验证和可审计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主AI代理可能生成语法有效但语义不安全的操作，使得基于身份的常驻权限带来重大操作风险，需要可验证的授权机制。

Method: 引入理由证明、共识模型、临时执行身份和仅追加证据链，构建从结构化工件计算执行权限的分布式信任框架。

Result: 在基于OpenKedge的受控变异子层上实例化模型，并映射到云原生环境，实现了紧凑授权不变量。

Conclusion: DTF通过将授权从常驻身份转移到证明派生权限，为主权AI部署中的代理执行提供了可治理、可审计和有界的基础设施基础。

中文摘要：现代云和企业系统依赖基于身份的授权，假设拥有有效凭证的调用者可以安全地执行命令。自主AI代理的出现使这一假设失效：代理可以生成语法有效但语义不安全的操作，使得常驻权限成为一个重大的操作风险。这种风险在主权AI系统中尤为严重，其中自主代理可能与云基础设施、受监管数据、金融工作流和国家规模的数字服务交互。受控变异子层通过介入代理操作来降低风险：代理提交意图，基础设施评估上下文和策略，并调解执行。然而，这转移了信任边界：如何使授权意图的决定变得可验证、分布式和可重放？
我们提出了一种分布式信任框架（DTF），这是一个用于受控变异系统的验证框架，从结构化、可验证的工件计算执行权限。DTF引入了一个理由证明来编码操作的可接受性基础，一个用于独立评估的共识模型，一个从已批准证明派生的临时执行身份，以及一个保留授权生命周期的仅追加证据链。在所述子层假设下，该架构强制执行紧凑的授权不变量：没有证明对象就没有高风险执行，没有共识就没有派生权限，没有与证据分离的有效变异。
我们定义模型，在基于OpenKedge的受控变异子层上实例化，并展示如何将其映射到云原生环境中。通过将授权从常驻身份转移到证明派生权限，DTF为在主权AI部署中使代理执行变得可治理、可审计和有界提供了基础设施基础。

Original abstract: Modern cloud and enterprise systems rely on identity-centric authorization, assuming that callers possessing valid credentials are safe to execute commands. The emergence of autonomous AI agents invalidates this assumption: agents can generate syntactically valid but semantically unsafe actions, making standing privileges a significant operational risk. This risk becomes especially acute in sovereign AI systems, where autonomous agents may interact with cloud infrastructure, regulated data, financial workflows, and national-scale digital services. Governed mutation substrates reduce this risk by interposing on agent actions: agents submit intents, infrastructure evaluates context and policy, and execution is mediated. However, this shifts the trust boundary: how can the decision to authorize an intent be made verifiable, distributed, and replayable?
  We introduce a Distributed Trust Framework (DTF), a verification framework for governed mutation systems that computes execution authority from structured, verifiable artifacts. DTF introduces a Justification Proof to encode the admissibility basis of an action, a consensus model for independent evaluation, an ephemeral Execution Identity derived from the approved proof, and an append-only Evidence Chain that preserves the authorization lifecycle. Under stated substrate assumptions, this architecture enforces a compact authorization invariant: no high-stakes execution without a proof object, no derived authority without consensus, and no valid mutation detached from evidence.
  We define the model, instantiate it over an OpenKedge-based governed mutation substrate, and show how it maps onto cloud-native environments. By shifting authorization from standing identity to proof-derived authority, DTF provides an infrastructure foundation for making agentic execution governable, auditable, and bounded in sovereign AI deployments.

Original abstract: Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) embedded in agentic frameworks have transformed information retrieval from static, long context question answering into open-ended exploration. Yet real world use requires models to discover and synthesize "long-tail" facts from dispersed sources, a capability that remains under-evaluated. We introduce PolitNuggets, a multilingual benchmark for agentic information synthesis via constructing political biographies for 400 global elites, covering over 10000 political facts. We standardize evaluation with an optimized multi agent system and propose FactNet, an evidence conditional protocol that scores discovery, fine-grained accuracy, and efficiency. Across models and settings, we find that current systems often struggle with fine-grained details, and vary substantially in efficiency. Finally, using benchmark diagnostics, we relate agent performance to underlying model capabilities, highlighting the importance of short-context extraction, multilingual robustness, and reliable tool use.

### [60] [Sheaf-Theoretic Transport and Obstruction for Detecting Scientific Theory Shift in AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14033v1)
*David N. Olivieri,Roque J. Hernández*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于层论的科学理论迁移检测框架，面向AI agent，潜在启发agent推理与概念学习。

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于层理论的框架，用于AI智能体检测表征框架在跨领域时的运输失败和理论转变候选者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI智能体无法自动检测表征框架何时需要扩展而非仅拟合数据，需要形式化方法识别理论转变候选者。

Method: 构建有限层理论框架，将上下文组织为局部到全局结构，通过拟合、限制、粘合图表并计算障碍（残余拟合、重叠不兼容、约束违反、极限关系失败、表征成本）来排名候选者。

Result: 在过渡卡片基准上，预期变形或扩展通常为最低障碍候选者，且转换类型可被分离。

Conclusion: 该框架为AI智能体提供了一个有限的诊断子问题：检测表征运输失败并识别扩展作为连贯下一步。

中文摘要：人工智能智能体中的科学理论转变需要的不仅仅是拟合方程到数据上。一个科学智能体必须检测现有的表征框架是否可以运输到新的领域中，或者其语言是否变成了局部到全局的障碍而必须扩展。本文开发了一个有限的层理论框架，通过运输和障碍来检测理论转变候选者。上下文被组织为一个局部到全局的结构，其中源、重叠、目标、验证图表被拟合、约束并测试粘合。障碍通过残余拟合、重叠不兼容、约束违反、极限关系失败和表征成本来衡量一致性的失败。我们在一个受控的过渡卡片基准上评估该框架，该基准旨在将源语言内的变形与该语言的扩展分开。主要结果是直接障碍排名：预期的变形或扩展通常是障碍最低的候选者，并且转换类型在基准中被分离。一个基于相同签名的星座核仅作为次要的表征相似性探针包含在内。目标不是重建历史范式转变或解决开放式的自主理论发明，而是为AI智能体分离一个有限的诊断子问题：检测何时表征运输失败且扩展成为连贯的下一步。

Original abstract: Scientific theory shift in AI agents requires more than fitting equations to data. An artificial scientific agent must detect whether an existing representational framework remains transportable into a new regime, or whether its language has become locally-to-globally obstructed and must be extended. This paper develops a finite sheaf-theoretic framework for detecting theory-shift candidates through transport and obstruction. Contexts are organized as a local-to-global structure in which source, overlap, target, and validation charts are fitted, restricted, and tested for gluing. Obstruction measures failure of coherence through residual fit, overlap incompatibility, constraint violation, limiting-relation failure, and representational cost. We evaluate the framework on a controlled transition-card benchmark designed to separate deformation within a source language from extension of that language. The main result is direct obstruction ranking: the intended deformation or extension is usually the lowest-obstruction candidate, and transition type is separated in the benchmark. A constellation kernel over the same signatures is included only as a secondary representational-similarity probe. The aim is not to reconstruct historical paradigm shifts or solve open-ended autonomous theory invention, but to isolate a finite diagnostic subproblem for AI agents: detecting when representational transport fails and extension becomes the coherent next move.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体的广泛应用需要与人类的社会价值观高度一致。然而，当前工作在自我认知、困境决策以及自我情感方面仍存在不足。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了一种新颖的基于价值的框架，该框架使用GraphRAG将原则转化为基于价值的指令，并通过在特定对话上下文中检索合适的指令来引导智能体按预期行为。为了评估预期行为的比率，我们从两个著名理论——马斯洛需求层次理论和Plutchik情绪轮盘——中定义了预期行为。通过在DAILYDILEMMAS基准上实验我们的方法，我们的方法相比基于提示的基线（包括ECoT、Plan-and-Solve和元认知提示）表现出显著的性能提升。我们的方法为AI系统中自我情感的出现提供了基础。

Original abstract: Wide applications of LLM-based agents require strong alignment with human social values. However, current works still exhibit deficiencies in self-cognition and dilemma decision, as well as self-emotions. To remedy this, we propose a novel value-based framework that employs GraphRAG to convert principles into value-based instructions and steer the agent to behave as expected by retrieving the suitable instruction upon a specific conversation context. To evaluate the ratio of expected behaviors, we define the expected behaviors from two famous theories, Maslow's Hierarchy of Needs and Plutchik's Wheel of Emotion. By experimenting with our method on the benchmark of DAILYDILEMMAS, our method exhibits significant performance gains compared to prompt-based baselines, including ECoT, Plan-and-Solve, and Metacognitive prompting. Our method provides a basis for the emergence of self-emotion in AI systems.
