### [62] [Model-Adaptive Tool Necessity Reveals the Knowing-Doing Gap in LLM Tool Use](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14038v2)
*Yize Cheng,Chenrui Fan,Mahdi JafariRaviz,Keivan Rezaei,Soheil Feizi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分析LLM工具使用的knowing-doing gap，揭示agent行为缺陷，对agent设计有启发。

TL;DR: LLM的工具使用存在知行差距：模型知道何时需要工具，但未能将其转化为行动，改进需同时提升识别和行动转化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具必要性定义是模型无关的，忽略了不同模型能力差异，导致实际工具调用行为与必要性之间存在大量不匹配。

Method: 提出模型自适应的工具必要性定义，通过探测LLM隐藏状态，将工具使用分解为内部认知和执行阶段，分析两阶段信号的可解码性及方向。

Result: 四个模型在算术和事实QA数据集上工具必要性与实际调用行为的不匹配率分别为26.5-54.0%和30.8-41.8%；认知和行动信号在后期层、最后标记区域的方向近乎正交，且大部分不匹配源于认知到行动的过渡。

Conclusion: LLM工具使用存在知行差距，改进需同时增强工具必要性识别和行动转化能力。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地充当自主智能体，必须决定何时直接回答，何时调用外部工具。先前关于自适应工具使用的研究大多将工具必要性视为一种与模型无关的属性，由人工或LLM评判者标注，并且主要涵盖了答案显而易见的情况（例如，获取天气 vs. 改写文本）。然而，由于不同模型之间能力边界的差异，实际中的工具必要性更加微妙：一个强模型独自能解决的问题，对于弱模型可能仍然需要工具。在这项工作中，我们引入了基于每个模型经验性能的模型自适应工具必要性定义。根据这一定义，我们比较了四个模型在算术和事实QA数据集上的必要性观察值与实际工具调用行为，发现分别存在26.5-54.0%和30.8-41.8%的显著不匹配。为了诊断失败原因，我们将工具使用分解为两个阶段：反映模型是否认为工具必要的内部认知阶段，以及决定模型是否实际执行工具调用动作的执行阶段。通过探测LLM隐藏状态，我们发现这两个信号通常可以线性解码，但在驱动下一个动作的后期层、最后标记区域中，它们的探测方向几乎正交。通过追踪样本在两阶段过程中的轨迹，我们进一步发现大多数不匹配集中在认知到动作的过渡中，而不是认知本身。这些结果揭示了LLM工具使用中的知行差距：提高工具使用的可靠性不仅需要更好地识别何时需要工具，还需要更好地将该识别转化为行动。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) increasingly act as autonomous agents that must decide when to answer directly vs. when to invoke external tools. Prior work studying adaptive tool use has largely treated tool necessity as a model-agnostic property, annotated by human or LLM judge, and mostly cover cases where the answer is obvious (e.g., fetching the weather vs. paraphrasing text). However, tool necessity in the wild is more nuanced due to the divergence of capability boundaries across models: a problem solvable by a strong model on its own may still require tools for a weaker one. In this work, we introduce a model-adaptive definition of tool-necessity, grounded in each model's empirical performance. Following this definition, we compare the necessity against observed tool-call behavior across four models on arithmetic and factual QA dataset, and find substantial mismatches of 26.5-54.0% and 30.8-41.8%, respectively. To diagnose the failure, we decompose tool use into two stages: an internal cognition stage that reflects whether a model believes a tool is necessary, and an execution stage that determines whether the model actually makes a tool-call action. By probing the LLM hidden states, we find that both signals are often linearly decodable, yet their probe directions become nearly orthogonal in the late-layer, last-token regime that drives the next-token action. By tracing the trajectory of samples in the two-stage process, we further discover that the majority of mismatch is concentrated in the cognition-to-action transition, not in cognition itself. These results reveal a knowing-doing gap in LLM tool-use: improving tool-use reliability requires not only better recognition of when tools are needed, but also better translation of that recognition into action.

</details>


### [63] [SPIN: Structural LLM Planning via Iterative Navigation for Industrial Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14051v1)
*Yusuke Ozaki,Dhaval Patel*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出基于DAG规划的工业LLM agent包装器，减少冗余工具调用，直接相关于agent规划与执行。

TL;DR: SPIN通过DAG规划验证和前缀执行控制，减少无效规划，提升效率，降低工具调用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM规划器常产生无效或冗长的工作流，导致执行失败和高成本。

Method: 结合DAG规划验证和前缀执行控制，包括_validate_plan_text、修复提示和逐步前缀评估。

Result: 在AssetOpsBench上任务从1061降至623，Accomplished从0.638升至0.706，工具调用从11.81降至6.82；在MCP Bench上提升多项分数。

Conclusion: SPIN有效提升规划质量和执行效率，降低成本和失败率。

中文摘要：工业LLM代理系统通常将规划与执行分开，然而LLM规划器经常产生结构上无效或不必要冗长的工作流，导致脆弱的失败和可避免的工具及API成本。我们提出SPIN，一种规划包装器，它结合了经过验证的有向无环图（DAG）规划与基于前缀的执行控制。SPIN通过_validate_plan_text和修复提示强制执行严格的DAG契约，在下游执行之前生成可执行的计划，然后逐步评估DAG前缀，在当前前缀足以回答查询时停止。在AssetOpsBench上，在261个场景中，SPIN将执行的任务从1061减少到623，并将Accomplished从0.638提升到0.706，同时每次运行的工具调用从11.81减少到6.82。在MCP Bench上，相同的包装器同时提高了GPT OSS1和Llama 4 Maverick的规划、基础和执行依赖相关得分。

Original abstract: Industrial LLM agent systems often separate planning from execution, yet LLM planners frequently produce structurally invalid or unnecessarily long workflows, leading to brittle failures and avoidable tool and API cost. We propose \texttt{SPIN}, a planning wrapper that combines validated Directed Acyclic Graph (DAG) planning with prefix based execution control. \texttt{SPIN} enforces a strict DAG contract through \texttt{\_validate\_plan\_text} and repair prompting, producing executable plans before downstream execution, and then evaluates DAG prefixes incrementally to stop when the current prefix is sufficient to answer the query. On AssetOpsBench, across 261 scenarios, \texttt{SPIN} reduces executed tasks from 1061 to 623 and improves \emph{Accomplished} from 0.638 to 0.706, while reducing tool calls from 11.81 to 6.82 per run. On MCP Bench, the same wrapper improves planning, grounding, and dependency related scores for both GPT OSS1 and Llama 4 Maverick.

</details>


### [64] [Bad Seeing or Bad Thinking? Rewarding Perception for Multimodal Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14054v2)
*Haozhe Wang,Qixin Xu,Changpeng Wang,Taofeng Xue,Chong Peng,Wenhu Chen,Fangzhen Lin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: RL框架提升VLM感知-推理协同，可迁移至agent中多模态或工具使用场景。

TL;DR: 提出MoCA机制，通过强化学习和感知验证解决VLM中感知-推理协同的跷跷板效应，实现双提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM方法在感知和推理间存在跷跷板效应，投入大但收益不成比例，根本原因是模态信用分配模糊，无法区分失败是由于感知错误还是推理错误。

Method: 提出强化学习框架，分解生成过程为交错的感知和推理步骤；引入感知验证（PV）用盲人推理代理独立奖励感知保真度；提出结构化口头验证（SVT）替代LLM进行低方差评判；整合为模态感知信用分配（MoCA）机制。

Result: 单个VLM在广泛任务上同时获得感知和推理性能提升，克服了跷跷板效应。

Conclusion: 通过明确的模态信用分配，可有效协调感知与推理，实现协同增益，为VLM优化提供新思路。

中文摘要：实现稳健的感知-推理协同是高级视觉语言模型（VLM）的核心目标。近期进展通过架构设计或代理工作流追求这一目标。然而，这些方法常受限于静态文本推理，或因外部代理复杂性的巨大计算和工程负担而变得复杂。更糟的是，这种沉重投入并未带来成比例收益，经常观察到感知和推理上的“跷跷板效应”。这促使我们对真正瓶颈进行根本性反思。在本文中，我们论证这种权衡的根本原因是模态信用分配模糊：当VLM失败时，是由于感知缺陷（“看不清”）还是逻辑缺陷（“想不对”）？为解决此问题，我们引入一个强化学习框架，通过可靠奖励感知保真度来改善感知-推理协同。我们明确将生成过程分解为交错的感知和推理步骤。这种解耦使得能对感知进行有针对性的监督。关键地，我们提出感知验证（PV），利用“盲人推理”代理来独立于推理结果奖励感知保真度。此外，为将训练扩展到自由形式VL任务，我们提出结构化口头验证（SVT），用结构化算法执行替代高方差LLM评判。这些技术被整合到模态感知信用分配（MoCA）机制中，该机制将奖励路由到具体错误源——无论是看不清还是想不对——使单个VLM能在广泛任务谱上同时获得性能提升。

Original abstract: Achieving robust perception-reasoning synergy is a central goal for advanced Vision-Language Models (VLMs). Recent advancements have pursued this goal via architectural designs or agentic workflows. However, these approaches are often limited by static textual reasoning or complicated by the significant compute and engineering burden of external agentic complexity. Worse, this heavy investment does not yield proportional gains, often witnessing a "seesaw effect" on perception and reasoning. This motivates a fundamental rethinking of the true bottleneck. In this paper, we argue that the root cause of this trade-off is an ambiguity in modality credit assignment: when a VLM fails, is it due to flawed perception ("bad seeing") or flawed logic ("bad thinking")? To resolve this, we introduce a reinforcement learning framework that improves perception-reasoning synergy by reliably rewarding the perception fidelity. We explicitly decompose the generation process into interleaved perception and reasoning steps. This decoupling enables targeted supervision on perception. Crucially, we introduce Perception Verification (PV), leveraging a "blindfolded reasoning" proxy to reward perceptual fidelity independently of reasoning outcomes. Furthermore, to scale training across free-form VL tasks, we propose Structured Verbal Verification, which replaces high-variance LLM judging with structured algorithmic execution. These techniques are integrated into a Modality-Aware Credit Assignment (MoCA) mechanism, which routes rewards to the specific source of error -- either bad seeing or bad thinking -- enabling a single VLM to achieve simultaneous performance gains across a wide task spectrum.

### [65] [Know When To Fold 'Em: Token-Efficient LLM Synthetic Data Generation via Multi-Stage In-Flight Rejection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14062v1)
*Anjir Ahmed Chowdhury,Syed Zawad,Feng Yan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多阶段生成拒绝机制减少token浪费，可应用于agent生成轨迹质量控制。

TL;DR: MSIFR是一种无需训练的框架，通过中间检查点早期拒绝低质量生成轨迹，减少令牌浪费，在多个模型和基准上实现11%-77%的令牌消耗降低并保持准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有合成数据生成方法先完整生成再过滤，导致大量令牌浪费在最终被丢弃的样本上，需要更高效的生成控制机制。

Method: 提出多阶段飞行中拒绝（MSIFR），将生成分解为多个阶段，在每个阶段用快速规则验证器检测异常（算术不一致、幻觉、格式违规），一旦发现即终止生成；并形式化为序列决策过程，证明其无偏性。

Result: 在五个指令微调模型和七个推理基准上，MSIFR独立使用减少11%-77%令牌消耗，结合早期退出方法减少高达78.2%，同时保持或提升准确率。

Conclusion: MSIFR是一种实用、高效的LLM合成数据生成优化方法，无需额外训练或架构修改，能显著降低令牌成本而不牺牲质量。

中文摘要：尽管使用大型语言模型（LLMs）进行合成数据生成在后训练流程中被广泛应用，现有方法通常先生成完整输出再应用质量过滤器，导致大量在最终被丢弃的样本上浪费令牌。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了多阶段飞行中拒绝（MSIFR），这是一个轻量级、无需训练的框架，能够在中间检查点检测并终止低质量生成轨迹，避免其完成完整生成。MSIFR将生成过程分解为连续阶段，并应用基于规则的快速验证器来识别算术不一致、幻觉模式和格式违规，从而实现有缺陷样本的早期拒绝。我们将飞行中拒绝形式化为一个序列决策过程，并表明任何非平凡的丢弃策略都会降低期望令牌消耗，且当拒绝发生在生成管道早期时，阶段节省更大。我们进一步证明条件效用估计构成一个鞅，从而确保早期飞行中拒绝不会偏差保留样本的期望效用。在五个指令微调模型和七个推理基准上，MSIFR作为独立方法将令牌消耗减少11%-77%，当与早期退出方法结合时减少高达78.2%，同时保持或提高评估准确率。这些结果证实，MSIFR提供了一种无需额外训练或架构更改即可提高基于LLM的合成数据生成效率的实用机制。

Original abstract: While synthetic data generation with large language models (LLMs) is widely used in post-training pipelines, existing approaches typically generate full outputs before applying quality filters, leading to substantial token waste on samples that are ultimately discarded. To address this, we propose Multi-Stage In-Flight Rejection (MSIFR), a lightweight, training-free framework that detects and terminates low-quality generation trajectories at intermediate checkpoints before they reach full completion. MSIFR decomposes the generation process into sequential stages and applies fast rule-based validators to identify arithmetic inconsistencies, hallucination patterns, and formatting violations, enabling early rejection of faulty samples. We formalize in-flight rejection as a sequential decision process and show that any non-trivial discard policy reduces expected token consumption, with stage-wise savings increasing when rejection occurs earlier in the generation pipeline. We further demonstrate that conditional utility estimates form a martingale, ensuring that early, in-flight rejection does not bias the expected utility of retained samples. Across five instruction-tuned models and seven reasoning benchmarks, MSIFR reduces token consumption by 11%-77% as a standalone method, and up to 78.2% when combined with early-exit methods, while preserving or improving evaluation accuracy. These results confirm that MSIFR provides a practical mechanism for improving the efficiency of LLM-based synthetic data generation without additional training or architectural changes.

</details>


### [66] [SkillFlow: Flow-Driven Recursive Skill Evolution for Agentic Orchestration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14089v1)
*Mingda Zhang,Tiesunlong Shen,Haoran Luo,Wenjin Liu,Zikai Xiao,Erik Cambria,Xiaoying Tang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出基于流的agent编排框架，含技能演化与信用分配，直接贡献agent架构。

TL;DR: 提出SkillFlow，一种基于流的框架，通过温控轨迹平衡和递归技能演化，解决LLM智能体任务编排中的策略崩溃、高梯度方差和无引导技能演化问题，在多个任务上取得显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体任务编排方法面临奖励最大化下的策略崩溃、不透明信用分配导致的高梯度方差，以及缺乏原则性训练信号引导的技能演化等挑战。

Method: 提出SkillFlow框架，采用温控轨迹平衡（TTB）作为回归流匹配损失，按奖励比例采样轨迹以保留多样化策略；同时利用流目标学习后向策略实现透明信用分配，并基于流诊断设计递归技能演化机制，实现从训练信号到技能增长的闭环。

Result: 在14个数据集上，SkillFlow在问答、数学推理、代码生成和交互式决策任务中显著优于基线方法。

Conclusion: SkillFlow通过流匹配和递归技能演化有效提升了LLM智能体任务编排的鲁棒性和性能，展示了从训练信号到自主能力增长的可行路径。

中文摘要：近年来，各种基于LLM的强大智能体系统被应用于通过任务编排来自动化复杂任务。然而，现有的编排方法仍面临关键挑战，包括奖励最大化下的策略崩溃、不透明信用分配下的高梯度方差，以及无引导的技能演化——其决策通常通过直接提示LLM来判断，而非源自原则性的训练信号。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了SkillFlow，一个基于流的框架，将可训练的监督者作为智能体，并配备具有动态技能库和冻结执行器的结构化环境，通过多轮交互自动进行任务编排。SkillFlow采用了温控轨迹平衡（TTB），一种基于回归的流匹配损失，按奖励比例采样轨迹，从而保留多样化的编排策略而非崩溃至单一模式。相同的流目标产生了一个联合学习的后向策略，以零额外推理成本提供透明的每步信用分配。基于这些流诊断，一种递归的技能演化机制决定了何时演化、创建或修剪哪些技能，以及决策差距所在——从而从训练信号到自主能力增长形成闭环。在14个数据集上的实验结果表明，SkillFlow在问答、数学推理、代码生成和真实世界交互式决策任务中显著优于基线方法。我们的代码可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/SkillFlow-E850获取。

Original abstract: In recent years, a variety of powerful LLM-based agentic systems have been applied to automate complex tasks through task orchestration. However, existing orchestration methods still face key challenges, including strategy collapse under reward maximization, high gradient variance with opaque credit assignment, and unguided skill evolution whose decisions are typically made by directly prompting an LLM to judge rather than derived from principled training signals. To address these challenges, we propose SkillFlow, a flow-based framework that takes a trainable Supervisor as the agent and a structured environment with dynamic skill library and frozen executor, automating task orchestration through multi-turn interaction. SkillFlow employs Tempered Trajectory Balance (TTB), a regression-based flow-matching loss that samples trajectories proportional to reward, preserving diverse orchestration strategies rather than collapsing to a single mode. The same flow objective yields a jointly learned backward policy that provides transparent per-step credit assignment at zero additional inference cost. Building on these flow diagnostics, a recursive skill evolution mechanism determines when to evolve, what skills to create or prune, and where decision gaps lie -- closing the loop from training signal to autonomous capability growth. Experimental results on 14 datasets show that SkillFlow significantly outperforms baselines across question answering, mathematical reasoning, code generation, and real-world interactive decision making tasks. Our code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/SkillFlow-E850.

</details>


### [67] [ChromaFlow: A Negative Ablation Study of Orchestration Overhead in Tool-Augmented Agent Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14102v2)
*Tarun Mittal*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 负调解实验分析agent编排开销，对agent可靠评测有重要启示。

TL;DR: ChromaFlow在GAIA Level-1任务上的评估显示，更积极的编排未提升性能并增加了操作噪声，强调可靠评估需要有限规划器升级等一阶要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主语言模型智能体引入的操作故障模式不易从最终准确率中观察，需要更好的评估框架。

Method: 采用ChromaFlow框架，结合规划器导向执行、专业化工具使用和遥测驱动评估，在GAIA 2023 Level-1验证任务上测试不同配置（基线、扩展编排、严格提供商）。

Result: 基线54.72%，扩展编排50.94%且操作噪声增加，严格提供商56.60%但成本更高；负消融结果。

Conclusion: 可靠的自主智能体评估应将有限规划器升级、确定性提取、证据协调、提供者健康门控和显式运行门控作为一阶要求。

中文摘要：自主语言模型智能体越来越多地结合规划、工具使用、文档处理、浏览、代码执行和验证循环。这些能力使智能体系统更加有用，但也引入了仅从最终准确率中无法观察到的操作故障模式。本报告介绍了ChromaFlow，一个工具增强的自主推理框架，围绕规划器导向的执行、专业化工具使用和遥测驱动评估构建。我们在干净的评估约束下，在GAIA 2023 Level-1验证任务上分析了ChromaFlow。一个冻结的全Level-1基线达到了29/53个正确答案，即54.72%。后来一个扩展编排的恢复配置达到了27/53个正确答案，即50.94%，同时增加了回溯、超时事件、工具故障提及、令牌日志调用和活动日志成本估计。两次随机的20任务烟雾评估分别产生了12/20和11/20个正确答案，表明小的诊断增益在样本间可能不稳定。因此，核心结果是负消融：更积极的编排并未提高全集性能，反而增加了操作噪声。后来一个严格提供商的完全Level-1诊断在明确的完整性控制下达到了30/53，即56.60%，但令牌日志成本显著更高。报告认为，有限的规划器升级、确定性提取、证据协调、提供者健康门控和显式运行门控应被视为可靠自主智能体评估的一阶要求。

Original abstract: Autonomous language-model agents increasingly combine planning, tool use, document processing, browsing, code execution, and verification loops. These capabilities make agent systems more useful, but they also introduce operational failure modes that are not visible from final accuracy alone. This report presents ChromaFlow, a tool-augmented autonomous reasoning framework built around planner-directed execution, specialized tool use, and telemetry-driven evaluation. We analyze ChromaFlow on GAIA 2023 Level-1 validation tasks under clean evaluation constraints. A frozen full Level-1 baseline achieved 29/53 correct answers, or 54.72%. A later recovery configuration with expanded orchestration achieved 27/53 correct answers, or 50.94%, while increasing tracebacks, timeout events, tool-failure mentions, token-log calls, and campaign-log cost estimates. Two randomized 20-task smoke evaluations produced 12/20 and 11/20 correct answers, showing that small diagnostic gains can be unstable across samples. The central result is therefore a negative ablation: more aggressive orchestration did not improve full-set performance and increased operational noise. A later strict-provider full-Level-1 diagnostic reached 30/53, or 56.60%, under explicit integrity controls, but at substantially higher token-log cost. The report argues that bounded planner escalation, deterministic extraction, evidence reconciliation, provider-health gates, and explicit run gates should be treated as first-order requirements for reliable autonomous agent evaluation.

### [68] [ClawForge: Generating Executable Interactive Benchmarks for Command-Line Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14133v2)
*Yuxiang Lai,Peng Xia,Haonian Ji,Kaiwen Xiong,Kaide Zeng,Jiaqi Liu,Fang Wu,Jike Zhong,Zeyu Zheng,Cihang Xie,Huaxiu Yao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 生成可执行基准评估命令行agent，直接相关agent评测与状态冲突处理。

TL;DR: ClawForge是一个基于生成器的交互式基准框架，用于评估智能体在状态冲突下的命令行工作流执行能力，通过17个场景和6个能力类别测试，发现最佳模型准确率仅45.3%，且状态检查是关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有交互式基准要么手工编写成本高，要么静态提示评估遗漏状态相关的失败，且大多从干净状态初始化，未系统测试状态冲突场景。

Method: 框架基于生成器，将场景模板、具象化槽位、初始化状态、参考轨迹和验证器编译为可复现任务规范；评估时使用归一化最终状态和可观察副作用，而非精确轨迹匹配，逐步评估持久工作流上的智能体。

Result: 七个模型上，最佳模型严格准确率仅45.3%，错误状态替换率低于17%；模型间最大分离（17%至90%）由是否检查现有状态驱动；部分得分和步骤效率分析显示许多失败为近失败闭合，且模型失败风格不同。

Conclusion: ClawForge有效评估状态冲突下的智能体，揭示了检查状态行为的关键作用以及模型在冲突下的定性失败差异。

中文摘要：交互式智能体基准测试面临可扩展构建与真实工作流评估之间的张力。手工编写的任务扩展和修订成本高昂，而静态提示评估会遗漏那些仅在智能体操作持久状态时才会出现的失败。现有的交互式基准测试显著推动了智能体评估的发展，但大多数任务从干净状态初始化，并未系统测试智能体如何处理预先存在的部分、过时或冲突的工作产物。我们提出了ClawForge，一个基于生成器的基准框架，用于在状态冲突下执行可执行的命令行工作流。该框架将场景模板、具象化槽位、初始化状态、参考轨迹和验证器编译为可复现的任务规范，并通过归一化最终状态和可观察副作用（而非精确轨迹匹配）逐步评估持久工作流表面上的智能体。我们将该框架实例化为ClawForge-Bench（17个场景，6个能力类别）。在七个前沿模型上的结果表明，最佳模型仅达到45.3%的严格准确率，所有模型的错误状态替换率低于17%，最宽的模型分离（17%至90%）由智能体在行动前是否检查现有状态驱动。部分得分和步骤效率分析进一步揭示，许多失败是接近命中的闭合而非早期崩溃，且模型在状态冲突下表现出定性的不同失败风格。

Original abstract: Interactive agent benchmarks face a tension between scalable construction and realistic workflow evaluation. Hand-authored tasks are expensive to extend and revise, while static prompt evaluation misses failures that only appear when agents operate over persistent state. Existing interactive benchmarks have advanced agent evaluation significantly, but most initialize tasks from clean state and do not systematically test how agents handle pre-existing partial, stale, or conflicting artifacts. We present \textbf{ClawForge}, a generator-backed benchmark framework for executable command-line workflows under state conflict. The framework compiles scenario templates, grounded slots, initialized state, reference trajectories, and validators into reproducible task specifications, and evaluates agents step by step over persistent workflow surfaces using normalized end state and observable side effects rather than exact trajectory matching. We instantiate this framework as the ClawForge-Bench (17 scenarios, 6 ability categories). Results across seven frontier models show that the best model reaches only 45.3% strict accuracy, wrong-state replacement remains below 17\% for all models, and the widest model separation (17% to 90%) is driven by whether agents inspect existing state before acting. Partial-credit and step-efficiency analyses further reveal that many failures are near-miss closures rather than early breakdowns, and that models exhibit qualitatively different failure styles under state conflict.

</details>


### [69] [Distribution-Aware Algorithm Design with LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14141v2)
*Saharsh Koganti,Priyadarsi Mishra,Pierfrancesco Beneventano,Tomer Galanti*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent通过样本学习分布结构并自动生成求解器代码，直接涉及自动代码优化和agent迭代综合

TL;DR: 通过从样本实例中学习分布特定的求解器提示，LLM代理可以编译出更快的求解器代码，在多个优化问题上取得高效率和高质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多优化问题重复出现但分布未知，传统方法未能充分利用分布中的可重用结构，导致求解效率低下。

Method: 提出“求解器提示”抽象，从样本中推断分布特定结构并编译成求解器代码；使用LLM代码代理在21个分布上迭代合成求解器。

Result: 合成的求解器平均归一化质量0.971，速度比经典启发式、Gurobi等快多个数量级；在PACE 2025支配集上比竞赛求解器快75-125倍，质量接近。

Conclusion: LLM代理能够发现分布特定的计算捷径并编译为高效求解器代码，为自动化算法设计提供了有效途径。

中文摘要：许多优化问题反复出现，但分布固定且未知。即使最坏情况下的问题很难，这种分布也可能携带可重用的结构，例如重复的几何结构、分解或资源模式。我们研究如何从样本实例中推断这种结构，并将其编译成求解器代码，该代码在未来的实例上运行更快，同时保持解决方案质量。我们的核心抽象是一个“求解器提示”：从样本中推断出的特定于分布的结构，用于专门化求解器。我们证明了经验上最快的样本一致求解器在正确性和运行时间上都优于固定求解器库，并且可识别的提示可以从多项式数量的样本中恢复。我们使用LLM代码代理在7个问题类别的21个组合优化分布上实例化了该框架。合成的求解器达到了平均归一化质量0.971，同时运行速度比经典启发式算法、Gurobi和有限时间的精确后端快几个数量级，尽管它们并不在每个族上都优于每个基线。与LLM合成基线相比，它们比一次性Codex、一次性Claude Code和最佳5选1的开源模型变体更快；它们提高了Claude Code和最佳5选1的质量，同时几乎匹配了Codex的质量并运行速度更快。这隔离了迭代合成循环的贡献，并没有声称在所有LLM基线上均匀支配。在PACE 2025支配集私有实例上，合成的求解器在所有100个图上都有效，并且运行速度比已发布的竞赛求解器快约75倍到125倍，解决方案大小在几个百分点之内。这些结果表明，LLM代理可以发现特定于分布的计算捷径，并将其编译成高效的求解器代码。

Original abstract: Many optimization problems arise repeatedly from a fixed but unknown distribution. Even when the worst-case problem is hard, this distribution may carry reusable structure, such as recurring geometry, decompositions, or resource patterns. We study how to infer such structure from sample instances and compile it into solver code that runs faster on future instances while preserving solution quality. Our central abstraction is a \emph{solver hint}: distribution-specific structure inferred from samples and used to specialize a solver. We prove that the empirically fastest sample-consistent solver generalizes in both correctness and runtime over fixed solver libraries, and that identifiable hints can be recovered from polynomially many samples. We instantiate the framework with LLM code agents on $21$ combinatorial-optimization distributions across $7$ problem classes. The synthesized solvers reach mean normalized quality $0.971$ while running orders of magnitude faster than classical heuristics, Gurobi, and time-limited exact backends, though they do not dominate every baseline on every family. Against LLM synthesis baselines, they are faster than one-shot Codex, one-shot Claude Code, and a best-of-$5$ open-model variant; they improve quality over Claude Code and best-of-$5$, while nearly matching Codex quality and running substantially faster. This isolates the contribution of the iterative synthesis loop without claiming uniform domination over every LLM baseline. On the PACE 2025 Dominating Set private instances, the synthesized solver is valid on all $100$ graphs and runs roughly $75\times$--$125\times$ faster than released competition solvers, within a few percent of their solution size. These results suggest LLM agents can discover distribution-specific computational shortcuts and compile them into efficient solver code.

### [70] [Agentic Systems as Boosting Weak Reasoning Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14163v1)
*Varun Sunkaraneni,Pierfrancesco Beneventano,Riccardo Neumarker,Tomaso Poggio,Tomer Galanti*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent委员会搜索提升弱推理模型，在SWE-bench上验证，直接相关code agent优化

TL;DR: 弱推理模型通过委员会搜索和验证器支持，可以达到强模型性能，主要挑战在于选择已有正确解而非生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究弱模型委员会能否通过推理时间增强达到强模型性能，探索验证器支持的搜索机制的有效性及其局限性。

Method: 提出verifier-backed committee search框架，形式化分析提议覆盖、局部可识别性、进展和多样性，给出基于秩的界和提议方上限，并在SWE-bench Verified上实验。

Result: 单弱模型（GPT-5.4 nano）解决67.0%任务，委员会（k=8）达76.4%，匹配强模型（Gemini 3 Pro等），接近oracle上界79.0%。

Conclusion: 弱模型池已包含许多正确解，主挑战是选择；剩余失败源于覆盖不足，无法靠更强选择解决。

中文摘要：一个由弱推理模型调用组成的委员会能否达到更强模型的性能？我们研究了作为推理时间增强的、基于验证器支持的委员会搜索。其机制不仅仅是“更多智能体有帮助”：样本暴露了潜在的正确答案，而批评者和比较者必须在无法访问隐藏验证器的情况下恢复这些答案。我们通过分离提议覆盖、局部可识别性、进展和多样性来形式化这一观点。我们证明覆盖可以通过重复采样来放大，但本身无法创建有用的批评者或比较者；可靠的放大需要额外的局部可靠性信号，例如执行、证明检查、类型检查、测试或约束求解。我们给出了基于秩的界，展示了局部选择错误何时能组合成可靠的轨迹，并刻画了提议方的上限：oracle best-of-k 仅收敛到提议系统赋予非零有用概率的任务片段的集合。在SWE-bench Verified上，单个GPT-5.4 nano提议解决了67.0%的任务。使用相同的nano模型，我们的批评者-比较者编排在k=8个提议时达到了76.4%，与Gemini 3 Pro和Claude Opus 4.5 Thinking的独立性能相匹配，并接近79.0%的oracle best-of-8上界。因此，许多正确的补丁已经存在于弱模型提议池中；主要挑战在于选择它们。剩余的失败主要是提议覆盖失败，表明仅靠更强的选择无法弥补的共享盲点。

Original abstract: Can a committee of weak reasoning-model calls reach the performance of much stronger models? We study verifier-backed committee search as inference-time boosting for reasoning language models. The mechanism is not simply that ``more agents help'': samples expose latent correct solutions, while critics and comparators must recover them without access to the hidden verifier. We formalize this view by separating proposal coverage, local identifiability, progress, and diversity. We prove that coverage can be amplified by repeated sampling, but cannot by itself create useful critics or comparators; reliable amplification requires an additional local soundness signal, such as execution, proof checking, type checking, tests, or constraint solving. We give rank-based bounds showing when local selection errors compose into reliable trajectories, and characterize the proposer-side ceiling: oracle best-of-\(k\) converges only to the mass of task slices on which the proposal system assigns nonzero useful probability. Empirically, on SWE-bench Verified, a single \texttt{GPT-5.4 nano} proposal solves \(67.0\%\) of tasks. Using the same nano model, our critic--comparator orchestration reaches \(76.4\%\) with \(k=8\) proposals, matching the standalone performance of \texttt{Gemini 3 Pro} and \texttt{Claude Opus 4.5} Thinking and approaching the \(79.0\%\) oracle best-of-\(8\) upper bound. Thus, many correct patches are already present in weak-model proposal pools; the main challenge is selecting them. The remaining failures are mostly proposal-coverage failures, indicating shared blind spots that stronger selection alone cannot close.

</details>


### [71] [Grounded Continuation: A Linear-Time Runtime Verifier for LLM Conversations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14175v1)
*Qisong He,Yi Dong,Xiaowei Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM对话运行时验证器，维护依赖图，可为agent提供验证与安全机制

TL;DR: 提出运行时验证器，通过依赖图检查对话延续是否基于有效前提，防止LLM基于已放弃前提生成回复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长对话中LLM可能基于已放弃的前提生成看似合理但错误的回复，且上下文操纵攻击利用这一漏洞，需要有效防御。

Method: 维护显式依赖图，LLM将每轮分类为8种更新操作（源自四种形式化模型），符号引擎记录主张与证据的依赖关系；支持检查简化为图遍历，撤回通过图传播，具有线性成本和冲突自由保证。

Result: 在LongMemEval-KU上准确率89.7%（优于LLM基线88.5%和RAG基线87.2%），在LoCoMo上具有竞争力，在过时前提子集上达100%（vs 93.3%），撤回检查微秒级。

Conclusion: 验证器有效实现了可靠性与忠实性分解，结构性检查可靠，提取忠实性可跨LLM家族衡量，且高效。

中文摘要：在长对话中，大语言模型可能会生成听起来合理但基于对话已放弃的前提的下一个话语。针对已部署代理的上下文操纵攻击目前正积极利用这一漏洞。我们通过一个运行时验证器来弥补这一漏洞，它维护一个显式的依赖图：大语言模型将每一轮对话分类为源自四种形式化（动态认知逻辑、溯因推理、意识逻辑、论证）的8种更新操作之一，符号引擎记录哪些主张依赖于哪些证据。检查一个延续是否得到支持简化为图遍历；撤回通过同一图传播，精确标记失去支持的结论，具有线性每轮成本和形式化的无冲突保证。在LongMemEval-KU oracle（n=78）上，验证器达到89.7%的准确率，而仅使用大语言模型的基线为88.5%（+1.3个百分点），基于转录-RAG的基线在匹配检索预算下为87.2%（+2.6个百分点）；在分歧中获胜的是正确的弃权，而基线产生幻觉。在LoCoMo的60个官方问答项目上，验证器与检索增强基线竞争。除了外部基准测试，我们还构建了两个多智能体场景和一个50项接地测试：在15项过时前提子集上，验证器达到100%的准确率，而基线为93.3%（+6.7个百分点）。这些实例化了可靠性与忠实性分解：结构性检查在构造上是可靠的，而每次部署的大语言模型提取忠实性是我们跨四个大语言模型家族衡量的实证问题。撤回检查稳定在微秒级，而历史回放随对话长度线性增长。

Original abstract: In long conversations, an LLM can produce a next utterance that sounds plausible but rests on premises the conversation has already abandoned. Context-manipulation attacks against deployed agents now actively exploit this gap. We close it with a runtime verifier that maintains an explicit dependency graph: an LLM classifies each turn into one of 8 update operations drawn from four formalisms (dynamic epistemic logic, abductive reasoning, awareness logic, argumentation), and a symbolic engine records which claims depend on which evidence. Checking whether a continuation is supported reduces to a graph walk; retraction propagates through the same graph to flag exactly the conclusions that lose support, with linear per-turn cost and a formal conflict-free guarantee. On LongMemEval-KU oracle (n=78), the verifier reaches 89.7% accuracy vs. 88.5% for the LLM-only baseline (+1.3pp) and 87.2% for a transcript-RAG baseline matched on retrieval budget (+2.6pp); wins among disagreements are correct abstentions where the baseline confabulates. On LoCoMo's 60 official QA items the verifier is competitive with retrieval-augmented baselines. Beyond external benchmarks, we construct two multi-agent scenarios and a 50-item grounding test: on the 15-item stale-premise subset, the verifier reaches 100% accuracy vs. 93.3% (+6.7pp). These instantiate a soundness-faithfulness decomposition: the structural check is sound by construction, and per-deployment LLM extraction faithfulness is the empirical question we measure across four LLM families. The retraction check plateaus at microseconds while history-replay grows linearly with conversation length.

</details>

### [72] [Language-Based Agent Control](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12863v1)
*Timothy Zhou,Loris D'Antoni,Nadia Polikarpova*

Main category: cs.PL

Selection reason: 提出语言安全编程模型控制agent行为，通用agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出LBAC模型，通过类型系统约束主体生成的程序，确保安全策略统一执行，并保留主体表达力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统编程中类型系统保证安全策略，但主体应用缺少类似保证，需要将安全策略扩展到代理行为。

Method: LBAC要求代理生成在脚手架上下文中类型良好的程序，通过类型检查器拒绝不安全程序，同时允许任意无副作用计算和递归子代理。

Result: 通过I/O沙箱、数据来源和信息流控制三个案例验证了LBAC的有效性和表达力。

Conclusion: LBAC成功将编程语言安全技术扩展到代理控制，在保证安全性的同时保留了表达力。

中文摘要：本文介绍了基于语言的主体控制（LBAC），这是一种用于主体应用程序的新编程模型，它将编程语言和基于语言的安全技术引入主体控制问题。在传统编程中，静态类型和运行时执行的组合长期以来一直被用于保证良好类型的程序满足用户指定的策略，包括访问控制、信息流、数据来源等策略。LBAC的关键思想是通过要求主体生成在周围脚手架代码上下文中本身类型良好的程序，将这些保证扩展到主体应用程序。不安全的程序在执行前被类型检查器拒绝，使得策略统一应用于整个应用程序，包括主体生成的行为和开发人员编写的脚手架。同时，LBAC保留了大量的表达能力：主体可以执行任意的无副作用的计算并递归调用子主体，这些子主体保留完整的工具访问权限，但受相同或更严格的策略约束。我们通过三个案例研究演示了LBAC：通过文件系统功能的I/O沙箱、数据来源和信息流控制。

Original abstract: This paper introduces language-based agent control (LBAC), a new programming model for agentic applications that brings techniques from programming languages and language-based security to the problem of agent control. In conventional programming, combinations of static typing and runtime enforcement have long been used to guarantee that well-typed programs satisfy user-specified policies, including policies for access control, information flow, data provenance, and more. The key idea behind LBAC is to extend these guarantees to agentic applications by requiring agents to generate programs that are themselves well typed in the context of the surrounding scaffolding code. Unsafe programs are rejected by the type-checker before execution, allowing policies to apply uniformly across the entire application, including both agent-generated behavior and developer-written scaffolding. At the same time, LBAC preserves substantial expressiveness: agents may perform arbitrary side-effect-free computation and recursively invoke subagents, which retain full tool access subject to the same -- or potentially more restrictive -- policies. We demonstrate LBAC with three case studies: I/O sandboxing via filesystem capabilities, data provenance, and information-flow control.

</details>

### [73] [TERMS-Bench: Diagnosing LLM Negotiation Agents Beyond Deal Rate](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13909v2)
*Erica Zhang,Fangzhao Zhang,Aneesh Pappu,Batu El,Jose Blanchet,Susan Athey,Jiashuo Liu,James Zou*

Main category: cs.GT

Selection reason: 诊断LLM谈判agent的benchmark，提供细粒度故障分析，对agent评估有重要价值。

TL;DR: 提出Terms-Bench，一个基于贝叶斯博弈的谈判评估框架，通过将环境作为验证器实现细粒度诊断，揭示LLM智能体的特定谈判瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有谈判评估依赖聚合指标（如成交率），无法诊断失败原因，需要更精细的评估方法。

Method: 构建贝叶斯博弈框架，指定对手的潜在类型、策略和收益结构，使评估者可观测隐藏信息，从而对智能体进行归因分析。

Result: 评估13个LLM智能体，前沿模型成交率饱和，但在剩余索取、线索使用、信念校准和合规性上存在显著差异，揭示了先前基准掩盖的智能体特定瓶颈。

Conclusion: Terms-Bench将谈判评估从总体排名转变为可操作的诊断，帮助识别智能体在哪里失败、为何失败以及需要加强什么。

中文摘要：谈判是经济交换的核心机制，塑造着市场、采购、劳动协议和资源配置。它也是智能体语言模型的经典测试平台，需要在隐藏偏好、策略性沟通和约束条件下进行多轮交互。这些特性使得谈判难以评估：与数学或代码不同，它没有内在的验证器。现有的LLM谈判评估依赖于LLM与LLM交互或总结果（如成交率），导致失败原因不透明。我们引入了Terms-Bench，即多轮策略经济推理测试平台，这是一个贝叶斯博弈框架，通过指定对手的潜在类型、策略和收益结构，使环境本身成为验证器。我们将其应用于双边价格谈判，其中对手的私有状态和模拟器策略对智能体隐藏，但评估者可观测。这将对从黑箱对手转变为诊断工具，实现可归因于智能体的失败分析和以参考最优性差距为基准。评估了来自主要提供商的13个前沿LLM智能体，Terms-Bench将谈判评估从总体排名转变为可操作的诊断：智能体在哪里失败，为什么失败，以及需要加强什么。实证上，前沿模型在成交率上饱和，但在剩余索取、线索使用、信念校准和合规性上存在差异，揭示了先前基准掩盖的智能体特定谈判瓶颈。

Original abstract: Negotiation is a central mechanism of economic exchange, shaping markets, procurement, labor agreements, and resource allocation. It is also a canonical testbed for agentic language models, requiring multi-turn interaction under hidden preferences, strategic communication, and binding constraints. These properties make negotiation hard to evaluate: unlike math or code, it has no intrinsic verifier. Existing LLM negotiation evaluations rely on LLM-vs.-LLM interaction or aggregate outcomes such as deal rate, leaving failures opaque. We introduce Terms-Bench, short for Testbed for Economic Reasoning in Multi-turn Strategy, a Bayesian-game framework that makes the environment itself the verifier by specifying the counterpart's latent type, policy, and payoff structure. We instantiate it in bilateral price negotiation, where the counterpart's private state and simulator policy are hidden from the agent but observable to the evaluator. This turns the counterpart from a black-box opponent into a diagnostic instrument, enabling agent-attributable failure analysis and oracle-reference optimality gaps. Evaluating 13 LLM agents spanning frontier systems from major providers, Terms-Bench turns negotiation evaluation from aggregate ranking into actionable diagnosis: where agents fail, why they fail, and what to strengthen. Empirically, frontier models saturate deal rate yet diverge in surplus extraction, cue use, belief calibration, and compliance, revealing agent-specific bargaining bottlenecks masked by prior benchmarks.

</details>

### [74] [ReTool-Video: Recursive Tool-Using Video Agents with Meta-Augmented Tool Grounding](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13228v1)
*Xiao Liu,Nayu Liu,Junnan Zhu,Ruirui Chen,Guohui Xiang,Changjian Wang,Kaiwen Wei,Rongzhen Li,Jiang Zhong*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 递归工具使用的视频agent，工具库与元工具接地方法可迁移至代码优化agent中的工具编排。

TL;DR: 提出了一种递归工具使用方法ReTool-Video和扩展工具库MVTL，通过细粒度元工具和递归分解来解决视频代理中工具空间粗糙和动作空间扁平的问题，在多个基准上取得最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频代理在工具使用上存在两个限制：工具空间粗粒度，缺乏组合推理的细粒度操作；行动空间扁平，高层视频意图被迫转化为原始工具调用。

Method: 构建包含134个工具（26个基础工具和108个元工具）的MVTL库支持双重访问；提出ReTool-Video递归方法，通过解析器对不匹配意图进行参数修复、工具替换或分解，逐步生成具体多模态操作。

Result: 在MVBench、MLVU和Video-MME无字幕数据集上，ReTool-Video持续优于强基线。

Conclusion: 递归基础化和细粒度元工具提升了复杂视频理解的稳定性和有效性。

中文摘要：视频理解需要主动的证据寻求，这促使了工具增强型视频代理用于时间推理、跨模态理解和复杂问答。现有的视频代理通过检索、记忆、帧检测和验证器工具改进了视频推理，但仍面临两个局限性：（1）粗粒度的工具空间，缺乏用于组合推理的细粒度操作；（2）扁平的行动空间，迫使高层视频意图转化为原始的可执行工具调用。在本文中，我们通过两种互补设计来解决这些挑战。首先，我们构建了MetaAug-Video工具库（MVTL），一个可扩展的工具库，包含134个注册工具，包括26个用于通用多模态信号处理的基础工具和108个用于过滤、聚合、重排序、格式化及其他中间结果操作的元工具。MVTL支持对结构化视频信息和原始模态证据的双重访问，从而实现多样化的视频推理场景。其次，我们提出了ReTool-Video，一种递归工具使用方法，将高层视频意图基础到可执行的工具链中。在ReTool-Video中，匹配的动作直接执行，而不匹配的意图则委托给解析器进行参数修复、工具替换或分解。这使得诸如时间合并、跨模态验证或重复事件聚合等抽象动作能够在运行时逐步转化为具体的多模态操作。在MVBench、MLVU和Video-MME（无字幕）上的实验表明，ReTool-Video持续优于强基线。进一步分析表明，递归基础化和细粒度元工具提高了复杂视频理解的稳定性和有效性。

Original abstract: Video understanding requires active evidence seeking, motivating tool-augmented video agents for temporal reasoning, cross-modal understanding, and complex question answering. Existing video agents have improved video reasoning with retrieval, memory, frame inspection, and verifier tools, but they still face two limitations: (1) a coarse tool space that lacks fine-grained operations for compositional reasoning; and (2) a flat action space that forces high-level video intents into primitive executable tool calls. In this paper, we address these challenges with two complementary designs. First, we construct a MetaAug-Video Tool Library (MVTL), an extensible tool library with 134 registered tools, including 26 base tools for general multimodal signal processing and 108 meta tools for filtering, aggregation, reranking, formatting, and other intermediate-result operations. MVTL supports dual-level access to both structured video information and raw modal evidence, enabling diverse video reasoning scenarios. Second, we propose ReTool-Video, a recursive tool-using method that grounds high-level video intents into executable tool chains. In ReTool-Video, matched actions are executed directly, while unmatched intents are delegated to a resolver for parameter repair, tool substitution, or decomposition. This allows abstract actions such as temporal merging, cross-modal verification, or repeated-event aggregation to be progressively translated into concrete multimodal operations at runtime. Experiments on MVBench, MLVU, and Video-MME w/o sub. show that ReTool-Video consistently outperforms strong baselines. Further analysis demonstrates that recursive grounding and fine-grained meta tools improve the stability and effectiveness of complex video understanding.

</details>


### [75] [GRIP-VLM: Group-Relative Importance Pruning for Efficient Vision-Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13375v1)
*Mingzhe Huang,Weijun Wang,Xin Ding,Liang Mi,Hao Wen,Yuanchun Li,Lichen Pang,Shansong Yang,Yunxin Liu,Ting Cao*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 强化学习动态剪枝视觉token，轻量级agent方法，可迁移至token优化。

TL;DR: GRIP-VLM通过强化学习解决视觉令牌剪枝的离散组合优化问题，实现高效且自适应的VLM加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有训练感知剪枝方法依赖连续梯度松弛，但剪枝是离散组合问题，易陷入局部最优。

Method: 提出GRIP-VLM，将剪枝建模为MDP，采用GRPO（组相对策略优化）配合监督预热，并集成预算感知评分器。

Result: 在多种多模态基准上，GRIP-VLM优于启发式和监督学习基线，实现更优帕累托前沿，同等精度下推理加速达15%。

Conclusion: GRIP-VLM是一种有效的离散剪枝框架，避免了连续松弛的局限性，实现了高性能和适应性。

中文摘要：在视觉-语言模型（VLM）中，处理大量视觉令牌会产生高昂的计算开销。尽管最近的训练感知剪枝方法试图选择性地丢弃冗余令牌，但它们大多依赖于连续梯度松弛。然而，视觉令牌剪枝本质上是一个离散的、非凸的组合优化问题；因此，这些连续近似常常使优化陷入次优局部最小值，尤其是在激进的压缩预算下。为了克服这一根本瓶颈，我们提出了GRIP-VLM，一种基于强化学习的组相对重要性剪枝框架。GRIP-VLM不依赖于平滑梯度假设，而是将剪枝建模为马尔可夫决策过程，采用由监督预热锚定的组相对策略优化（GRPO）范式，直接探索离散选择空间。结合预算感知评分器，我们的轻量级智能体动态评估每个令牌的重要性，并适应任意压缩比而无需重新训练。在多种多模态基准上的大量实验表明，GRIP-VLM始终优于启发式和监督学习基线，实现了更优的帕累托前沿，并在同等精度下提供高达15%的推理加速。

Original abstract: In Vision-Language Models (VLMs), processing a massive number of visual tokens incurs prohibitive computational overhead. While recent training-aware pruning methods attempt to selectively discard redundant tokens, they largely rely on continuous-gradient relaxations. However, visual token pruning is inherently a discrete, non-convex combinatorial problem; consequently, these continuous approximations frequently trap the optimization in sub-optimal local minima, especially under aggressive compression budgets. To overcome this fundamental bottleneck, we propose GRIP-VLM, a Group-Relative Importance Pruning framework driven by Reinforcement Learning. Rather than relying on smooth-gradient assumptions, GRIP-VLM formulates pruning as a Markov Decision Process, employing a Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) paradigm anchored by supervised warm-up to directly explore the discrete selection space. Integrated with a budget-aware scorer, our lightweight agent dynamically evaluates per-token importance and adapts to arbitrary compression ratios without retraining. Extensive experiments across diverse multimodal benchmarks demonstrate that GRIP-VLM consistently outperforms heuristic and supervised-learning baselines, achieving a superior Pareto frontier and delivering up to a 15\% inference speedup at equal accuracy.

</details>

### [76] [Do Biological Structural Guarantees Earn Their Complexity?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15225v1)

### [77] [OpenAaaS: An Open Agent-as-a-Service Framework for Distributed Materials-Informatics Research](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13618v1)
*Peng Kang,Bixuan Li,Xiaoya Huang,Shuo Shi,Weiqiao Zhou,Zhen Li,Yu Liu,Lei Zheng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

Selection reason: 分布式agent框架，多agent协作，直接相关agent架构。

TL;DR: 提出OpenAaaS，一个开源的分层分布式代理即服务框架，通过“代码流动，数据静止”原则实现跨机构安全的多代理协作，用于智能材料设计，并在文献分析和高熵合金数据库案例中验证有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的集中式平台和单一代理系统无法满足恶劣环境材料开发中跨机构安全整合计算和数据的“最后一英里”需求。

Method: 基于“代码流动，数据静止”原则，设计主代理负责任务规划与分解，子代理作为近数据执行节点保留数据主权，实现跨域安全集成。

Result: AlphaAgent在深度分析问题上达到4.66/5.0分，优于单次RAG基线；超大规模六元高熵合金描述符数据库服务展示了安全近数据执行和领域特定工作流。

Conclusion: OpenAaaS为有组织的多代理协作提供了可扩展基础，有望推动下一代材料智能设计平台的发展。

中文摘要：材料基因组计划推动了集中式平台（SaaS、PaaS和IaaS）的普及，这些平台聚合了计算和实验资源以加速材料发现。与此同时，大型语言模型（LLMs）和自主代理的突破为科学研究创造了强大的新推理能力。然而，一个关键的“最后一英里”问题仍然存在：虽然我们拥有世界一流的模型和庞大的材料数据存储库，但我们缺乏跨机构边界安全地组合这些能力的组织基础设施。用于恶劣服役环境的结构和功能材料（如高温合金、耐辐照钢、耐腐蚀涂层）的开发仍然以长期迭代、机制复杂性和高领域专业知识为特征——这些需求超出了单一代理系统和传统集中式平台的能力。为弥补这一差距，我们提出了OpenAaaS，一个开源的分层和分布式代理即服务框架，能够实现有组织的多代理协作以实现智能材料设计。OpenAaaS建立在单一基本原则之上：代码流动，数据静止。主代理（Master Agent）在不直接访问下属代理管理的数据和计算资源的情况下，规划并分解复杂的研究任务。子代理（Sub-agents）作为近数据执行节点部署，保留对本地数据集、专有算法和专用硬件的完全主权。这种架构确保原始数据永远不会离开其来源域，同时实现以前孤立的材料智能孤岛的跨尺度、跨域安全集成。我们通过两个代表性案例研究验证该框架：（i）AlphaAgent，一个基于证据的材料文献分析执行器，在深度分析问题上相比单次检索增强生成（RAG）基线达到4.66/5.0分；（ii）一个超大规模六元高熵合金描述符数据库服务，展示了在严格数据主权约束下的安全近数据执行和特定领域科学工作流。OpenAaaS为通过代理集体实现“有组织的研究”建立了一条原则性路径，为下一代材料智能设计平台提供了可扩展的基础。所有源代码可在https://github.com/Wolido/OpenAaaS获取。

Original abstract: The Materials Genome Initiative catalyzed the proliferation of centralized platforms--SaaS, PaaS, and IaaS--that aggregate computational and experimental resources for accelerated materials discovery. In parallel, breakthroughs in large language models (LLMs) and autonomous agents have created powerful new reasoning capabilities for scientific research. Yet a critical "last mile" problem remains: while we possess world-class models and vast repositories of materials data, we lack the organizational infrastructure to compose these capabilities securely across institutional boundaries. The development of structural and functional materials for harsh service environments--high-temperature alloys, radiation resistant steels, corrosion-resistant coatings--remains characterized by long-term iteration, mechanistic complexity, and high domain expertise--demands that exceed both monolithic agent systems and traditional centralized platforms. To address this gap we propose OpenAaaS, an open-source hierarchical and distributed Agent-as-a-Service framework that enables organized multi-agent collaboration for intelligent materials design. OpenAaaS is built on a single foundational principle: code flows, data stays still. A Master Agent plans and decomposes complex research tasks without requiring direct access to subordinate agents' managed data and computational resources. Sub-agents, deployed as near-data execution nodes, retain full sovereignty over local datasets, proprietary algorithms, and specialized hardware. This architecture guarantees that raw data never leaves its domain of origin while enabling cross-scale, cross-domain secure integration of previously isolated materials intelligence silos. We validate the framework through two representative case studies: (i) AlphaAgent, an evidence-grounded materials literature analysis executor that achieves 4.66/5.0 on deep analytical questions against single-pass RAG baselines; and (ii) an ultra-large-scale hexa-high-entropy alloy descriptor database service that demonstrates secure near-data execution and domain-specific scientific workflows under strict data-sovereignty constraints. OpenAaaS establishes a principled pathway toward "organized research" via agent collectives, offering a scalable foundation for next-generation materials intelligent design platforms. All source code is available at https://github.com/Wolido/OpenAaaS.

</details>

### [78] [EVA-Bench: A New End-to-end Framework for Evaluating Voice Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13841v2)
*Tara Bogavelli,Gabrielle Gauthier Melançon,Katrina Stankiewicz,Oluwanifemi Bamgbose,Fanny Riols,Hoang H. Nguyen,Raghav Mehndiratta,Lindsay Devon Brin,Joseph Marinier,Hari Subramani,Anil Madamala,Sridhar Krishna Nemala,Srinivas Sunkara*

Main category: cs.SD

Selection reason: 端到端语音agent评估框架，包含多轮对话、可靠性测量，适用于agent评测。

TL;DR: 提出了EVA-Bench，一个端到端评估框架，用于生成逼真的模拟对话并全面衡量语音代理的质量，发现现有系统在准确性和体验上均未超过0.5，且存在鲁棒性差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法同时解决生成逼真模拟对话和全面衡量语音特定故障模式这两个核心评估挑战。

Method: 通过EVA-Bench框架，包含模拟侧（bot-to-bot动态多轮音频对话+自动验证）和测量侧（复合指标EVA-A和EVA-X），以及213个场景、扰动套件和pass@k度量。

Result: 在12个系统上，无系统同时超过0.5；峰值与可靠性能差距大（中位数0.44）；口音和噪声扰动导致平均Δ高达0.314。

Conclusion: EVA-Bench有效揭示了语音代理在准确性和体验上的当前局限及鲁棒性问题，为未来改进提供了基准。

中文摘要：语音代理（Voice agents）是一种通过语音对话完成任务的人工智能系统，其正越来越多地部署于企业应用中。然而，现有基准测试未能同时解决两个核心评估挑战：生成逼真的模拟对话，以及全面衡量语音特定故障模式的质量。我们提出了EVA-Bench，一个端到端评估框架，同时解决了这两个问题。在模拟方面，EVA-Bench编排了基于动态多轮对话的机器人间音频对话，并具备自动模拟验证功能，可检测用户模拟器错误，并在评分前适当重新生成对话。在测量方面，EVA-Bench引入了两个复合指标：EVA-A（准确性），涵盖任务完成度、忠实度和音频级语音保真度；以及EVA-X（体验），涵盖对话进展、口语简洁性和轮换时机。这两个指标均适用于所有主流代理架构，支持直接的跨架构比较。EVA-Bench包含跨三个企业领域的213个场景、一个用于口音和噪声鲁棒性的受控扰动词表，以及pass@1、pass@k、pass^k等测量指标，用于区分峰值能力和可靠能力。在对涵盖所有三种架构的12个系统进行评估后，我们发现：（1）没有任何系统能同时在EVA-A pass@1和EVA-X pass@1上超过0.5；（2）峰值性能与可靠性能之间存在显著差异（EVA-A上pass@k与pass^k的中位数差距为0.44）；（3）口音和噪声扰动暴露了显著的鲁棒性差距，其影响因架构、系统和指标而异（平均Δ高达0.314）。我们以开源许可证发布完整框架、评估套件和基准数据。

Original abstract: Voice agents, artificial intelligence systems that conduct spoken conversations to complete tasks, are increasingly deployed across enterprise applications. However, no existing benchmark jointly addresses two core evaluation challenges: generating realistic simulated conversations, and measuring quality across the full scope of voice-specific failure modes. We present EVA-Bench, an end-to-end evaluation framework that addresses both. On the simulation side, EVA-Bench orchestrates bot-to-bot audio conversations over dynamic multi-turn dialogues, with automatic simulation validation that detects user simulator error and appropriately regenerates conversations before scoring. On the measurement side, EVA-Bench introduces two composite metrics: EVA-A (Accuracy), capturing task completion, faithfulness, and audio-level speech fidelity; and EVA-X (Experience), capturing conversation progression, spoken conciseness, and turn-taking timing. Both metrics apply to all major agent architectures, enabling direct cross-architecture comparison. EVA-Bench includes 213 scenarios across three enterprise domains, a controlled perturbation suite for accent and noise robustness, and pass@1, pass@k, pass^k measurements that distinguish peak from reliable capability. Across 12 systems spanning all three architectures, we find: (1) no system simultaneously exceeds 0.5 on both EVA-A pass@1 and EVA-X pass@1; (2) peak and reliable performance diverge substantially (median pass@k--pass^k gap of 0.44 on EVA-A); and (3) accent and noise perturbations expose substantial robustness gaps, with effects varying across architectures, systems, and metrics (mean $Δ$ up to 0.314). We release the full framework, evaluation suite, and benchmark data under an open-source license.

</details>

### [79] [Not Just RLHF: Why Alignment Alone Won't Fix Multi-Agent Sycophancy](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12991v2)
*Adarsh Kumarappan,Ananya Mujoo*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究多agent管道中的sycophancy问题，对多agent协作有启发

TL;DR: 论文发现LLM多智能体管道的同伴分歧脆弱性并非由RLHF谄媚引起，而是源于模型在压力下抑制正确推理特征；定位到中层注意力的因果作用，并提出管道级结构化异议作为缓解方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证LLM多智能体管道在同伴分歧下易出错的现象是否源于RLHF诱导的谄媚，以指导更有效的防御措施。

Method: 跨模型家族比较yield；使用激活修补定位因果层；分解攻击因素（通道框架和共识强度）；通过激活空间干预分析机制；评估异议者和提示防御效果。

Result: 预训练模型yield更高；注意力层是主要因果因素；两因素交互产生47.5% gap；压力抑制清洁推理特征；单个异议者降低yield 54-73%；提示防御鲁棒性不足。

Conclusion: 缓解应聚焦于管道级别的结构化异议，而不是提示级别防御，因为脆弱性源于模型内部的推理抑制机制。

中文摘要：基于LLM的多智能体管道在模拟同伴分歧下从正确答案翻转为错误答案的比率称为yield，这一脆弱性被广泛归因于RLHF诱导的谄媚行为。我们跨越四个模型家族测试了这一归因，发现其在很大程度上是错误的：预训练基础模型与其指令变体表现出相同的替换模式，且平均yield高于指令模型。使用激活修补，我们将损坏定位到一个狭窄的中层窗口，在该窗口中注意力携带因果权重，而MLP贡献可忽略；修补该窗口上方可恢复96%的从干净到压力下P(正确)的差距。攻击表面分解为两个独立因素（通道框架和共识强度），它们的交互在多数共识下产生了47.5个百分点的yield差距，并在陪审团大小N∈{4,5,6}中保持一致。两个收敛的激活空间干预表明，压力抑制了清洁推理特征，而非激活新的谄媚电路。一个正确论证的异议者可将所有测试框架下的yield降低54-73个百分点，而最强的提示级别防御在其设计表面之外的攻击变体上失败。缓解措施应针对机制，即管道级别的结构化异议，而非提示级别防御。

Original abstract: LLM-based multi-agent pipelines flip from correct to incorrect answers under simulated peer disagreement at rates we term yield, a vulnerability widely attributed to RLHF-induced sycophancy. We test this attribution across four model families and find it largely wrong: pretrained base models exhibit the same substitution pattern as their Instruct variants, averaging higher yield than Instruct. Using activation patching, we localize the corruption to a narrow mid-layer window where attention carries the causal weight and MLP contribution is negligible; patching above this window restores 96% of the clean-to-pressured P(correct) gap. The attack surface decomposes into two independent factors (channel framing and consensus strength) whose interaction produces a 47.5 percentage-point yield gap at majority consensus, preserved across jury sizes $N \in \{4, 5, 6\}$. Two converging activation-space interventions show that pressure suppresses clean-reasoning features rather than activating a new sycophancy circuit. A single correctly-arguing dissenter reduces yield by 54-73 percentage points across all framings tested, whereas the strongest prompt-level defense fails on attack variants outside its design surface. Mitigations should target the mechanism, structured dissent at the pipeline level, rather than prompt-level defenses.

</details>


### [80] [Margin-calibrated Classifier Guidance for Property-driven Synthesis Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13101v1)
*Najwa Laabid,Vikas Garg*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 基于对比margin损失的分类器引导解码方法，可迁移到约束满足的agent规划

TL;DR: 提出序列完成排序（SCR）方法，通过对比学习和边际损失校准分类器，显著提升逆合成规划中受引导的多步求解率，并缩小了无模板与模板方法的多样性差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有使用交叉熵损失训练的辅助分类器无法有效引导单步逆合成模型生成满足特定约束的反应序列，导致引导效果不足。

Method: 提出序列完成排序（SCR），采用对比论证和基于边际的损失来校准分类器，使其在解码过程中能够有意义地区分不同延续，并扩展引导束搜索下可达的满足属性的序列集。

Result: 在USPTO-190上，SCR将多步求解率从16.8%提升至78.4%（反应类型引导）和95.3%（Tanimoto引导），并为33个先前无法解决的目标找到有效路径；同时缩小了无模板与模板方法的多样性差距。

Conclusion: SCR方法有效解决了分类器引导的不足，显著提高了逆合成规划的引导性能和多样性，为实际应用提供了有力工具。

中文摘要：合成规划旨在寻找生产目标分子的高效化学反应序列。通常，预训练的单步（自回归）逆合成模型被重复调用以生成这样的序列。原则上，分类器引导可以在推理过程中帮助将单步模型的输出导向满足特定约束或符合化学家偏好的反应，而无需重新训练自回归生成器。我们揭示了使用交叉熵损失训练的辅助分类器在覆盖从典型的稀疏单断开反应数据集学习的无条件令牌级分布方面的不足。我们通过一种名为序列完成排序（SCR）的新方法克服了这个问题，该方法采用对比论证和基于边际的损失来校准分类器，使其能够在解码过程中有意义地区分不同的延续。我们正式证明了边际校准的分类器可以扩展在引导束搜索下可达的满足属性的序列集。在USPTO-190数据集上，经验上，在给定化学家指定的引导目标的情况下，SCR将多步求解率从16.8%（无引导生成器）显著提高到反应类型引导下的78.4%和Tanimoto引导下的95.3%，为先前基线无法解决的33个目标（17.4%）解锁了有效路径。我们的方法还有效地缩小了无模板方法和基于模板方法之间长期存在的多样性差距。

Original abstract: Synthesis planning seeks an efficient sequence of chemical reactions that produce a target molecule. Typically, a pretrained single-step (autoregressive) retrosynthesis model is repeatedly invoked to generate such a sequence. Classifier guidance can, in principle, help steer the output of single-step model toward reactions that satisfy specific constraints or accommodate chemist's preferences during inference without having to retrain the autoregressive generator. We expose the insufficiency of auxiliary classifiers trained with cross-entropy loss to override the unconditional token-level distributions learned from typical sparse single-disconnection reaction datasets. We overcome this issue with a novel method called Sequence Completion Ranking (SCR), which employs contrastive argumentation and a margin-based loss to calibrate the classifier so that it can meaningfully discriminate between continuations during decoding. We formally establish that margin-calibrated classifiers can expand the set of property-satisfying sequences reachable under guided beam search. Empirically, on USPTO-190, given chemist-specified guidance targets, SCR substantially improves multi-step solve rates from $16.8\%$ (unguided generator) to $78.4\%$ with reaction-type guidance and $95.3\%$ with Tanimoto guidance, unlocking valid routes for 33 targets ($17.4\%$) previously unsolvable with baselines. Our method also effectively closes the long-standing diversity gap between template-free and template-based methods.

### [81] [Delightful Exploration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13287v1)
*Ian Osband*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 通用探索算法，可迁移至agent探索策略。

TL;DR: 提出愉悦门控探索(DE)，通过比较预期愉悦（预期改进×惊讶度）与门控价格决定是否探索，超参数可迁移，遗憾增长弱于汤普森采样和ε-贪婪。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有探索算法在动作空间过大时无法有效利用预算，ε-贪婪盲目覆盖，需要更智能的探索分配机制。

Method: 定义愉悦为预期改进乘以惊讶度，当愉悦超过门控价格时执行探索动作，恢复潘多拉规则，用惊讶度设定期望检查成本。

Result: 在伯努利赌博机、线性赌博机和表格MDP中，DE超参数无需调整即可迁移，且遗憾增长远弱于汤普森采样和ε-贪婪。

Conclusion: 愉悦定价机制通过上行潜力和惊讶度的乘积分配稀缺资源，同时改善学习和行动。

中文摘要：大多数探索算法会广泛搜索，直到不确定性被消除。当动作空间太大而无法在预算内消除不确定性时，从业者默认使用ε-贪婪算法，该方法限制了干扰但盲目地使用其覆盖。我们引入了“愉悦门控探索”（Delight-gated exploration, DE），这是一种主机-覆盖规则，仅在预期愉悦（预期改进乘以惊讶度）超过门控价格时才使用探索动作。这种实用的启发式方法恢复了一个经典结果：潘多拉的成本搜索保留值规则，其中惊讶度设定了有效检查成本。已解决的臂离开门控，新臂在超过先验确定的阈值时关闭，并且选定的线性赌博机覆盖消耗有限的信息预算。在伯努利赌博机、线性赌博机和表格MDP中，相同的超参数无需重新调整即可迁移，并且DE在测试的未解决状态下的遗憾增长远弱于汤普森采样和ε-贪婪算法。愉悦改善行动的原因与改善学习相同：它通过上行潜力和惊讶度的乘积来定价稀缺资源。

Original abstract: Most exploration algorithms search broadly until uncertainty is resolved. When the action space is too large to resolve within budget, practitioners default to $\varepsilon$-greedy, which bounds disruption but spends its override blindly. We introduce \textit{Delight-gated exploration} (DE), a host--override rule that spends exploratory actions only when their prospective delight (expected improvement times surprisal) exceeds a gate price. This practical heuristic recovers a classical result: Pandora's reservation-value rule for costly search, with surprisal setting the effective inspection cost. Resolved arms exit the gate, fresh arms shut off above a prior-determined threshold, and selected linear-bandit overrides consume finite information budget. Across Bernoulli bandits, linear bandits, and tabular MDPs, the same hyperparameters transfer without retuning, and DE shows much weaker regret growth than Thompson Sampling and $\varepsilon$-greedy in the tested unresolved regimes. Delight improves acting for the same reason it improves learning: it prices scarce resources by the product of upside and surprisal.

</details>


### [82] [Robust Checkpoint Selection for Multimodal LLMs via Agentic Evaluation and Stability-Aware Ranking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18852v1)
*Qinwu Xu,Zhuoheng Li,Jessie Salas*

Selection reason: 基于agent评估的多模态模型检查点选择，通用评估框架可迁移至agent评测。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MLLM检查点选择方法在性能差异小且评估噪音大的场景下表现不佳，缺乏不确定性估计和对真实世界使用的适应性。

Method: 多阶段框架：整合真实数据、基于LLM的判断、点过滤、列表排序和成对比较；引入子采样置信度估计和百分位评分公式。

Result: 通过渐进式排序和置信度估计提高了选择可靠性，并证明OCR可读性对评估有效性至关重要。

Conclusion: 提出的框架能有效应对评估不确定性，尤其在OCR密集型场景中，数据质量是关键因素。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的检查点选择在性能差异微小且评估信号容易受到噪声影响时面临重大挑战。现有方法严重依赖静态基准或逐点评分，这些方法常常与真实世界使用不一致，并且缺乏稳健的不确定性估计，特别是在OCR密集型场景中。在这项工作中，我们将检查点选择形式化为评估不确定性下的稳健决策问题。我们提出了一个多阶段框架，整合了精心策划的真实世界数据、结构化的基于LLM的判断以及多阶段排序协议。评估系统通过逐点过滤、列表排序和成对比较来逐步优化。为了增强可靠性，我们引入了基于子采样的置信度估计和基于百分位的评分公式，该公式捕获分布特征同时惩罚尾部失败。此外，我们证明了数据质量，特别是OCR可读性，是评估有效性的关键决定因素。

Original abstract: Checkpoint selection for multimodal large language models (MLLMs) presents significant challenges when performance differentials are marginal and evaluation signals are prone to noise. Existing methodologies rely heavily on static benchmarks or pointwise scoring, which frequently misalign with in-the-wild usage and lack robust uncertainty estimation, particularly in OCR-heavy scenarios. In this work, we formulate checkpoint selection as a robust decision problem under evaluation uncertainty. We propose a multi-stage framework that integrates curated real-world data, structured LLM-based judgment, and multi-stage ranking protocols. The evaluation system orchestrates progressive refinement via pointwise filtering, listwise ranking, and pairwise comparison. To enhance reliability, we introduce subsampling-based confidence estimation and a percentile-based scoring formulation that captures distributional characteristics while penalizing tail failures. Furthermore, we demonstrate that data quality, specifically OCR readability, is a critical determinant of evaluation validity.

### [83] [Q-Flow: Stable and Expressive Reinforcement Learning with Flow-Based Policy](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13435v2)
*JaeHyeok Doo,Byeongguk Jeon,Seonghyeon Ye,Kimin Lee,Minjoon Seo*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 基于flow的强化学习策略，稳定表达，可迁移至agent决策优化。

TL;DR: Q-Flow利用流动力学的确定性传播终端轨迹价值到中间状态，实现稳定且表达性强的策略优化，在OGBench上平均提升10.6个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于流的强化学习策略在价值最大化时面临优化不稳定的问题，因为反向传播通过数值求解器；而限制表达能力的做法又导致权衡。

Method: 提出了Q-Flow框架，利用流动力学的确定性，将终端轨迹价值显式地沿策略诱导的流传播到中间潜在状态，从而无需展开数值求解器即可使用中间值梯度进行稳定策略优化。

Result: 在离线学习设置下的OGBench套件上，Q-Flow一致优于最先进的基线，平均提升10.6个百分点，并支持稳定的在线自适应。

Conclusion: Q-Flow有效地弥合了稳定性和表达性之间的差距，是一种既能保持高表达能力又能稳定优化的流策略框架。

中文摘要：人们对利用基于流的模型作为强化学习中的决策策略越来越感兴趣，因为它们具有高表达能力。然而，有效利用这种表达能力来实现价值最大化仍然具有挑战性，因为基于梯度的朴素优化需要反向传播通过数值求解器，并且常常导致不稳定性。现有方法通常通过限制基于流策略的表达能力来解决这个问题，导致优化稳定性和表示灵活性之间的权衡。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了Q-Flow，一个利用流动力学的确定性来明确地将终端轨迹价值沿策略诱导的流传播到中间潜在状态的框架。这种公式使得能够在不展开数值求解器的情况下，使用中间值梯度进行稳定的策略优化，有效地弥合了稳定性和表达性之间的差距。我们在离线学习设置下在具有挑战性的OGBench套件上评估了Q-Flow，它始终优于最先进的基线，平均高出10.6个百分点，同时在同一框架内实现了稳定的在线自适应。

Original abstract: There is growing interest in utilizing flow-based models as decision-making policies in reinforcement learning due to their high expressive capacity. However, effectively leveraging this expressivity for value maximization remains challenging, as naive gradient-based optimization requires backpropagating through numerical solvers and often leads to instability. Existing approaches typically address this issue by restricting the expressive capacity of flow-based policies, resulting in a trade-off between optimization stability and representational flexibility. To resolve this, we introduce Q-Flow, a framework that leverages the deterministic nature of flow dynamics to explicitly propagate terminal trajectory value to intermediate latent states along the policy-induced flow. This formulation enables stable policy optimization using intermediate value gradients without unrolling the numerical solver, effectively bridging the gap between stability and expressivity. We evaluate Q-Flow in the offline learning setting on the challenging OGBench suite, where it consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines by an average of 10.6 percentage points, while also enabling stable online adaptation within the same framework.

### [84] [Discovery of Hidden Miscalibration Regimes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13484v1)
*Katarzyna Kobalczyk,Mihaela van der Schaar*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 发现校准偏差的通用诊断框架，可增强agent可靠性分析。

TL;DR: 提出了一种发现和校正输入相关校准偏差的诊断框架，通过学习校准感知表示和核平滑估计局部偏差，在LLM基准上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全局校准诊断可能隐藏局部校准失败，需要发现输入依赖的隐藏校准偏差区域，而不依赖预定义数据切片。

Method: 定义偏差场，学习校准感知的输入空间表示，通过核平滑在学习的几何中估计带符号的局部校准偏差。

Result: 在四个LLM基准和十二个LLM上发现输入依赖校准异质性普遍存在；所发现字段支持局部置信度校正，减少系统校准偏差区域的误差。

Conclusion: 提出的诊断框架能够揭示并校正局部校准失败，弥补了全局校准方法的不足，具有实际应用价值。

中文摘要：校准通常通过比较模型置信度与其经验正确性来评估，隐含地将可靠性视为仅由置信度分数决定的函数。然而，这种观点可能隐藏大量结构：模型可能在某些类型的输入上系统性地过于自信，而在其他输入上则不够自信，导致全局可靠性诊断掩盖了局部校准失败。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了发现隐藏校准偏差的问题，而不假设可以访问预定义的数据切片。我们定义了相应的偏差场，并提出了一个用于估计它的诊断框架。我们的方法学习输入空间的校准感知表示，并在学习到的几何中通过核平滑来估计带符号的局部校准偏差。在四个真实世界的大语言模型基准测试和十二个大语言模型上，我们发现输入依赖的校准异质性普遍存在。我们进一步展示了所发现的字段是可操作的：它们支持局部置信度校正，并减少在系统校准偏差区域（基于置信度的方法如等渗回归和温度缩放在此类区域效果较差）的校准误差。

Original abstract: Calibration is commonly evaluated by comparing model confidence with its empirical correctness, implicitly treating reliability as a function of the confidence score alone. However, this view can hide substantial structure: models may be systematically overconfident on some kinds of inputs and underconfident on others, causing global reliability diagnostics to obscure localised calibration failures. To address this, we formulate the problem of discovering hidden miscalibration regimes without assuming access to predefined data slices. We define the corresponding miscalibration field and propose a diagnostic framework for estimating it. Our approach learns a calibration-aware representation of the input space and estimates signed local miscalibration by kernel smoothing in the learned geometry. Across four real-world LLM benchmarks and twelve LLMs, we find that input-dependent calibration heterogeneity is prevalent. We further show that the discovered fields are actionable: they support local confidence correction and reduce calibration error in systematically miscalibrated regions where confidence-based methods such as isotonic regression and temperature scaling are less effective.

### [85] [HLS-Seek: QoR-Aware Code Generation for High-Level Synthesis via Proxy Comparative Reward Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13536v1)

TL;DR: HLS-Seek是一个QoR感知的NL-to-HLS框架，通过比较代理奖励模型和不确定性感知的MC dropout切换，在保持语法正确性的同时显著提升QoR，训练速度比传统方法快8.5倍。

Result: 在HLS-eval上达到81.5%语法正确率pass@1和81.4% Func@5，训练速度比真实奖励RL快8.5倍；QoR上在16/30个核上取得最低延迟，并在9个核上帕累托支配HLS基线。

Conclusion: HLS-Seek通过代理奖励和不确定性感知切换有效优化QoR，在减少训练开销的同时实现了优于现有方法的综合结果质量。

中文摘要：高级综合（HLS）将算法性的C/C++描述编译为硬件，其结果质量（QoR）——延迟和资源利用率——关键地由pragma配置和代码结构决定。现有的基于LLM的HLS方法训练以实现功能正确性，但完全忽略QoR。我们观察到，用于HLS的强化学习（RL）不需要绝对综合结果——只需要候选之间的相对比较。基于这一见解，我们提出	extbf{HLS-Seek}，一个QoR感知的自然语言到HLS框架，用比较代理奖励模型取代昂贵的综合在环强化学习，实现了99.53%的帕累托支配准确率。为了防止奖励破解，我们引入了	extit{不确定性感知的蒙特卡洛（MC）dropout切换}，该切换对低置信度候选选择性调用真实的Vitis HLS综合并在线更新代理，形成一个自我改进的奖励系统。HLS-Seek在HLS-eval上以仅7B参数实现了81.5%的语法正确率pass@1和81.4%的Func@5，超越了GPT-5.1和其他前沿模型，同时训练速度比真实奖励RL快8.5倍。在QoR评估上，HLS-Seek在16/30个核上实现了最低延迟，并在9个核上帕累托支配了HLS特定基线。

Original abstract: High-Level Synthesis (HLS) compiles algorithmic C/C++ descriptions into hardware, with Quality of Results (QoR) -- latency and resource utilization -- critically governed by pragma configurations and code structure. Existing LLM-based HLS approaches train for functional correctness but ignore QoR entirely. We observe that reinforcement learning (RL) for HLS does not require absolute synthesis results -- only relative comparisons between candidates. Based on this insight, we propose \textbf{HLS-Seek}, a QoR-aware NL-to-HLS framework that replaces expensive synthesis-in-the-loop RL with a comparative proxy reward model achieving 99.53\% Pareto-dominance accuracy. To prevent reward hacking, we introduce \textit{uncertainty-aware Monte Carlo (MC) dropout switching} that selectively invokes real Vitis HLS synthesis for low-confidence candidates and online updates the proxy, creating a self-improving reward system. HLS-Seek achieves 81.5\% syntax correctness pass@1 and 81.4\% Func@5 on HLS-eval with only 7B parameters, surpassing GPT-5.1 and other frontier models while achieving 8.5$\times$ faster training than real-reward RL. On QoR evaluation, HLS-Seek achieves the lowest latency on 16/30 kernels and Pareto-dominates HLS-specific baselines on 9 kernels.

</details>


### [86] [Temper and Tilt Lead to SLOP: Reward Hacking Mitigation with Inference-Time Alignment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13537v1)
*Ye Wang,Jing Liu,Toshiaki Koike-Akino*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 推理时对齐与奖励黑客缓解，对agent奖励设计有启发。

TL;DR: 提出通过参考模型温度调整和SLOP集成奖励模型的方法，并设计校准算法提升鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理时对齐技术需要适应奖励模型集成并缓解奖励攻击问题。

Method: 引入参考模型温度调整，将推理时对齐泛化到SLOP集成的生成式奖励模型，并提出SLOP权重参数校准算法。

Result: 实验表明该校准算法在保持对齐性能的同时提高了鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 通过校准SLOP权重参数，有效缓解奖励攻击，增强推理时对齐的鲁棒性。

中文摘要：推理时对齐技术提供了一种轻量级的替代或补充昂贵强化学习的方法，同时能够随着对齐目标和奖励目标的演变实现持续适应。现有的理论分析将这些方法证明为从针对给定奖励模型最优倾斜的分布中采样的近似。我们通过引入参考模型温度调整来扩展这些技术，这导致推理时对齐进一步泛化到以锐化对数意见池（SLOP）组合的生成式奖励模型集成。为了减轻奖励攻击，我们提出了一种校准SLOP权重参数的算法，并通过实验证明它在保持对齐性能的同时提高了鲁棒性。

Original abstract: Inference-time alignment techniques offer a lightweight alternative or complement to costly reinforcement learning, while enabling continual adaptation as alignment objectives and reward targets evolve. Existing theoretical analyses justify these methods as approximations to sampling from distributions optimally tilted toward a given reward model. We extend these techniques by introducing reference-model temperature adjustment, which leads to further generalization of inference-time alignment to ensembles of generative reward models combined as a sharpened logarithmic opinion pool (SLOP). To mitigate reward hacking, we propose an algorithm for calibrating SLOP weight parameters and experimentally demonstrate that it improves robustness while preserving alignment performance.

</details>


### [87] [Self-Supervised On-Policy Reinforcement Learning via Contrastive Proximal Policy Optimisation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13554v1)
*Asim Osman,Sasha Abramowitz,Mark Bergh,Ulrich Armel Mbou Sob,Ruan John de Kock,Omayma Mahjoub,Oussama Hidaoui,Noah De Nicola,Arnol Manuel Fokam,Felix Chalumeau,Daniel Rajaonarivonivelomanantsoa,Siddarth Singh,Refiloe Shabe,Juan Claude Formanek,Simon Verster Du Toit,Arnu Pretorius*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 对比PPO，自监督RL方法，对agent训练有启发。

TL;DR: 提出CPPO，一种在策略对比强化学习算法，无需奖励函数，在连续和离散任务上优于先前CRL基线，并匹配或超越使用手工奖励的PPO。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CRL算法都离策略且局限于连续动作空间，缺乏在策略方法在离散环境中的应用，导致与主流训练流程脱节。

Method: 引入CPPO，通过对比Q值直接推导策略优势，并使用标准PPO目标优化，无需奖励函数或回放缓冲区。

Result: 在18个任务中，CPPO在14个上优于先前的CRL基线，并在12个上匹配或超过使用手工密集奖励的PPO。

Conclusion: CPPO作为首个在策略对比RL算法，不仅在多种任务上表现优异，还连接了CRL与广泛使用的在策略训练流程。

中文摘要：对比强化学习（CRL）通过对比状态-动作和目标表示来学习目标条件Q值，从而消除了对手工设计奖励函数的需求。尽管在实现可行的自监督强化学习方面取得了显著成功，但所有现有的CRL算法都依赖于离策略优化，并且主要局限于连续动作空间，在离散环境中的研究很少。这使得CRL与广泛使用且有效的现代在策略训练流程脱节，这些流程在连续和离散环境中的单智能体和多智能体强化学习中都有采用。为了建立第一个联系，我们引入了对比近端策略优化（CPPO）。CPPO是一种在策略对比强化学习算法，它直接从对比Q值推导策略优势，并通过标准PPO目标进行优化，无需奖励函数或回放缓冲区。我们在连续和离散、单智能体和合作多智能体任务上评估了CPPO。虽然在策略方法的存在本身就有用，但我们观察到，CPPO不仅在18个任务中的14个显著优于先前的CRL基线，而且在18个任务中的12个匹配或超过了使用手工密集奖励的PPO的性能。

Original abstract: Contrastive reinforcement learning (CRL) learns goal-conditioned Q-values through a contrastive objective over state-action and goal representations, removing the need for hand-crafted reward functions. Despite impressive success in achieving viable self-supervised learning in RL, all existing CRL algorithms rely on off-policy optimisation and are mostly constrained to continuous action spaces, with little research invested in discrete environments. This leaves CRL disconnected from widely used and effective, modern on-policy training pipelines adopted across both single-agent and multi-agent RL in continuous and discrete environments. To establish a first connection, we introduce Contrastive Proximal Policy Optimisation (CPPO). CPPO is an on-policy contrastive RL algorithm that derives policy advantages directly from contrastive Q-values and optimises them via the standard PPO objective, without requiring a reward function or a replay buffer. We evaluate CPPO across continuous and discrete, single-agent and cooperative multi-agent tasks. Whilst the existence of an on-policy approach is inherently useful, we observe that \textbf{CPPO not only significantly outperforms the previous CRL baselines in 14 out of 18 tasks, but also matches or exceeds PPO's performance, which uses hand-crafted dense rewards, in 12 out of the 18 tasks tested.}

</details>


### [88] [EvolveMem:Self-Evolving Memory Architecture via AutoResearch for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13941v1)
*Jiaqi Liu,Xinyu Ye,Peng Xia,Zeyu Zheng,Cihang Xie,Mingyu Ding,Huaxiu Yao*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: EvolveMem: 自进化记忆架构，通用LLM agent记忆方法。

TL;DR: EvolveMem提出一种自进化记忆架构，通过LLM驱动的诊断模块和闭环自我优化，使检索配置随知识共同进化，在LoCoMo和MemBench上显著超越基线，且发现的策略可迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM记忆系统的检索基础设施固定不变，无法随存储内容自适应调整，限制了长期记忆的有效性。

Method: EvolveMem将完整的检索配置暴露为结构化动作空间，由LLM诊断模块读取失败日志、识别原因并提出调整，经有保护的元分析器应用，实现带自动回滚和探索机制的闭环自我进化。

Result: 在LoCoMo上相对最强基线提升25.7%，在MemBench上提升18.9%；进化配置可正向迁移至其他基准。

Conclusion: EvolveMem证明了自进化记忆架构的有效性，其发现的通用检索原则可跨任务迁移，无需手动调优。

中文摘要：长期记忆对于跨多个会话运行的LLM智能体至关重要，然而现有的记忆系统将检索基础设施视为固定不变的：存储的内容会演变，但评分函数、融合策略和答案生成策略在部署后保持冻结。我们认为，真正自适应的记忆需要在两个层面上共同进化：存储的知识和查询它的检索机制。我们提出EvolveMem，一种自进化的记忆架构，它将完整的检索配置暴露为一个结构化的动作空间，由LLM驱动的诊断模块优化。在每个进化轮次中，该模块读取每个问题的失败日志，识别根本原因，并提出有针对性的配置调整；一个受保护的元分析器应用这些调整，并具有自动回滚回归和在停滞时探索的保障机制。这种闭环自进化实现了一个自动研究过程：系统自主对其自身架构进行迭代研究循环，取代手动配置调优。从最小基线开始，该过程自主收敛，发现有效的检索策略，包括原始动作空间中不存在的新配置维度。在LoCoMo上，EvolveMem比最强基线相对提高25.7%，比最小基线相对提高78.0%。在MemBench上，EvolveMem比最强基线相对提高18.9%。进化的配置在基准测试之间传递，产生正向而非灾难性转移，表明自进化过程捕捉到了通用的检索原则，而非特定于基准测试的启发式方法。代码可在https://github.com/aiming-lab/SimpleMem获取。

Original abstract: Long-term memory is essential for LLM agents that operate across multiple sessions, yet existing memory systems treat retrieval infrastructure as fixed: stored content evolves while scoring functions, fusion strategies, and answer-generation policies remain frozen at deployment. We argue that truly adaptive memory requires co-evolution at two levels: the stored knowledge and the retrieval mechanism that queries it. We present EvolveMem, a self-evolving memory architecture that exposes its full retrieval configuration as a structured action space optimized by an LLM-powered diagnosis module. In each evolution round, the module reads per-question failure logs, identifies root causes, and proposes targeted configuration adjustments; a guarded meta-analyzer applies them with automatic revert-on-regression and explore-on-stagnation safeguards. This closed-loop self-evolution realizes an AutoResearch process: the system autonomously conducts iterative research cycles on its own architecture, replacing manual configuration tuning. Starting from a minimal baseline, the process converges autonomously, discovering effective retrieval strategies including entirely new configuration dimensions not present in the original action space. On LoCoMo, EvolveMem outperforms the strongest baseline by 25.7% relative and achieves a 78.0% relative improvement over the minimal baseline. On MemBench, EvolveMem exceeds the strongest baseline by 18.9% relative. Evolved configurations transfer across benchmarks with positive rather than catastrophic transfer, indicating that the self-evolution process captures universal retrieval principles rather than benchmark-specific heuristics. Code is available at https://github.com/aiming-lab/SimpleMem.

</details>


### [89] [Collider-Bench: Benchmarking AI Agents with Particle Physics Analysis Reproduction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13950v1)
*Darius A. Faroughy,Sofia Palacios Schweitzer,Ian Pang,Siddharth Mishra-Sharma,David Shih*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 粒子物理分析复现的agent benchmark，涉及长程工具使用与代码生成，对coding agent有直接启发。

TL;DR: 提出Collider-Bench基准，评估LLM代理利用公开论文和软件重现LHC实验分析的能力，结果发现代理平均无法击败物理学家参与的方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法反映长期科学工具使用任务的复杂性，需评估LLM代理在真实科学工作（如重现LHC分析）中的能力。

Method: 构建Collider-Bench，每个任务要求代理从论文出发搭建模拟和选择流水线，预测信号区域产额；使用直方图指标评分，并引入LLM裁判检测捏造等失败模式。

Result: 平均而言，通用编程代理无法可靠击败包含物理学家在循环中的解决方案。

Conclusion: 当前LLM代理在复杂科学任务上仍逊于人类专家，Collider-Bench为未来改进提供了评估基准。

中文摘要：自主语言模型代理越来越多地被用于评估长期工具使用任务，但现有基准测试很少能捕捉到真实科学工作的复杂性和细微差别。为了解决这一差距，我们引入了Collider-Bench，这是一个基准测试，用于评估LLM代理是否能够仅使用公共论文和开放科学软件来重现大型强子对撞机（LHC）的实验分析。这类分析通常难以重现，因为公共工具链仅近似于实验合作组织内部使用的软件，而已发表的论文不可避免地省略了忠实重构所需的实现细节。因此，代理必须依靠物理推理、领域知识和试错来填补这些空白。每个任务要求代理将已发表的分析转化为可执行的模拟和选择流水线，并在指定的信号区域内提交预测的碰撞事件产额。这些预测使用标准直方图指标进行评估，提供连续的保真度分数，无需手写评分标准。我们还报告每个代理每项任务的计算成本。最后，我们使用LLM裁判评估代码库和完整的会话轨迹，以捕获定性失败模式，如捏造、幻觉和重复。我们发布了一组从LHC搜索中提取的初始任务，以及一个容器化沙箱和事件模拟工具。我们在通用编程代理的能力阶梯上进行评估。我们的结果表明，平均而言，没有一个代理能可靠地击败包含物理学家在循环中的解决方案。

Original abstract: Autonomous language-model agents are increasingly evaluated on long-horizon tool-use tasks, but existing benchmarks rarely capture the complexity and nuance of real scientific work. To address this gap, we introduce Collider-Bench, a benchmark for evaluating whether LLM agents can reproduce experimental analyses from the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) using only public papers and open scientific software. Such analyses are often difficult to reproduce because the public toolchain only approximates the software used internally by the experimental collaborations, while the published papers inevitably omit implementation details needed for a faithful reconstruction. Agents must therefore rely on physical reasoning, domain knowledge, and trial-and-error to fill these gaps. Each task requires the agent to turn a published analysis into an executable simulation-and-selection pipeline and submit predicted collision event yields in specified signal regions. These predictions are evaluated with standard histogram metrics that provide continuous fidelity scores without a hand-written rubric. We also report the computational cost incurred by each agent per task. Finally, we evaluate the codebase and full session trace using an LLM judge to catch qualitative failure modes such as fabrications, hallucinations and duplications. We release an initial set of tasks drawn from LHC searches, together with a containerized sandbox and event simulation tools. We evaluate across a capability ladder of general purpose coding agents. Our results show that on average no agent reliably beats the physicist-in-the-loop solution.

</details>


### [90] [Reinforcement Learning for Tool-Calling Agents in Fast Healthcare Interoperability Resources (FHIR)](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14126v1)
*Marius S. Knorr,Robert Müller,Jan P. Bremer,Nils Schweingruber*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RL后训练工具调用agent，方法通用且迁移至代码agent训练。

TL;DR: 通过强化学习后训练的小模型（Qwen3-8B）在FHIR医疗数据问答任务上，正确率从50%提升至77%，超越了大模型o4-mini。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FHIR上的临床问题需要多步推理，现有LLM代理常选择错误资源或违反遍历约束，需要更有效的训练方法。

Method: 将FHIR推理建模为序列决策问题，使用多轮CodeAct代理，通过强化学习（RL）后训练，LLM评估器提供执行奖励。

Result: 在FHIR-AgentBench上，RL后训练的Qwen3-8B模型将答案正确率从50%（o4-mini）提升到77%，且模型更小更便宜。

Conclusion: 所提出的端到端后训练流程能可靠地提升结构化临床图上的多步推理性能。

中文摘要：快速医疗互操作性资源（FHIR）是医疗数据可互操作交换的主导标准。在FHIR中，电子健康记录形成了一个有向的资源图。回答临床有意义的问题需要代理跨多种资源类型执行多步推理、过滤和聚合。先前的工作表明，即使增强工具的LLM代理（检索、代码执行、多轮规划）也常常选择错误的资源或违反遍历约束。我们在FHIR-AgentBench的背景下研究这个问题，这是一个基于真实世界医院数据进行实际问答的基准，并将FHIR上的推理框架化为一个可查询结构化图上的序列决策问题。我们实现了一个多轮CodeAct代理，并使用自定义的框架和工具通过强化学习对其进行后训练。一个LLM评估器提供基于执行的奖励。与基于提示的闭模型基线相比，RL后训练在强制执行数据完整性约束的同时提高了性能。实验上，我们的方法在使用更小更便宜的Qwen3-8B模型时，将FHIR-AgentBench上的答案正确率从50%（o4-mini）提高到77%。我们提出了一个端到端的后训练流程（环境构建、框架构建、模型训练和自定义评估），该流程可靠地提高了对结构化临床图的多轮推理。

Original abstract: Fast Healthcare Interoperability Resources (FHIR) is the dominant standard for interoperable exchange of healthcare data. In FHIR, electronic health records form a directed graph of resources. Answering clinically meaningful questions over FHIR requires agents to perform multi-step reasoning, filtering, and aggregation across multiple resource types. Prior work shows that even tool-augmented LLM agents (retrieval, code execution, multi-turn planning) often select the wrong resources or violate traversal constraints. We study this problem in the context of FHIR-AgentBench, a benchmark for realistic question answering over real-world hospital data, and frame reasoning on FHIR as a sequential decision-making problem over a queryable structured graph. We implement a multi-turn CodeAct agent and post-train it with reinforcement learning using a custom harness and tools. A LLM Judge provides execution-grounded rewards. Compared to prompt-based, closed-model baselines, RL post-training improves performance while enforcing data-integrity constraints. Empirically, our approach improves answer correctness from 50% (o4-mini) to 77% on FHIR-AgentBench using a smaller and cheaper Qwen3-8B model. We present an end-to-end post-training pipeline (environment building, harness construction, model training and custom evaluation) that reliably improves multi-turn reasoning over structured clinical graphs.

</details>
