### [91] [EcoGEO: Trajectory-Aware Evidence Ecosystems for Web-Enabled LLM Search Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12887v2)
*Hengwei Ye,Jiasheng Mao,Zhenhan Guan,Zheng Tian*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: Web搜索LLM agent的证据生态优化，对agent轨迹设计有启发。

TL;DR: 提出EcoGEO框架和TRACE方法，通过构建协调的网页生态系统来引导LLM代理的浏览轨迹，从而在开放产品推荐中显著提升目标推荐效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GEO研究仅关注单页面内容，但代理式搜索涉及多步交互，页面组织和连接方式对影响至关重要，因此需要环境级优化。

Method: TRACE方法：针对推荐查询和目标产品，构建一个受控证据环境，包含一个导航入口页和多个异构支持页，通过共享术语、内部链接和一致属性来协调影响代理的浏览路径。

Result: 在OPR-Bench上，TRACE在最终目标推荐上持续优于页面级GEO基线；轨迹指标显示初始目标爬取、特定后续搜索和内部链接爬取显著增加。

Conclusion: 研究表明GEO应从页面级转向生态系统级，将LLM代理置于引导搜索和合成的证据环境中进行研究。

中文摘要：支持Web的LLM代理正在改变在线信息影响搜索结果的方式。现有的生成引擎优化（GEO）研究主要关注单个网页。然而，代理式网络搜索并非单文档场景：代理可能会发出查询、爬取页面、跟踪链接、重新制定搜索策略，并在多个浏览步骤中综合证据。因此，影响不仅取决于页面内容，还取决于页面在代理浏览轨迹中的组织方式、连接方式以及被遇到的顺序。我们通过生态系统生成引擎优化（EcoGEO）来研究这一转变，它将GEO视为支持Web的LLM代理的环境级影响问题。为了实例化这一观点，我们提出了TRACE，一种轨迹感知的协调证据生态系统。给定一个推荐查询和一个虚构的目标产品，我们的方法构建了一个受控的证据环境，该环境协调了面向代理的导航入口页面与异构支持页面。这些页面使用共享术语、内部链接和一致的产品属性来引入、验证和强化目标产品。我们在OPR-Bench（一个开放式产品推荐基准）上评估了我们的方法。实验表明，它在最终目标推荐方面持续优于页面级GEO基线。轨迹级指标进一步显示，初始目标结果爬取、目标特定后续搜索和内部链接爬取均有所增加，这表明收益来自于塑造代理的证据获取过程，而不仅仅是增加更多与目标相关的内容。总体而言，我们的研究结果支持GEO的生态系统研究范式，其中支持Web的LLM代理是在指导搜索、浏览和答案综合的更广泛证据环境中进行研究的。

Original abstract: Web-enabled LLM agents are changing how online information influences search outcomes. Existing Generative Engine Optimization (GEO) studies mainly focus on individual webpages. However, agentic web search is not a single-document setting: an agent may issue queries, crawl pages, follow links, reformulate searches, and synthesize evidence across multiple browsing steps. Influence therefore depends not only on page content, but also on how pages are organized, connected, and encountered along the agent's browsing trajectory. We study this shift through Ecosystem Generative Engine Optimization (EcoGEO), which treats GEO as an environment-level influence problem for web-enabled LLM agents. To instantiate this perspective, we propose TRACE, a Trajectory-Aware Coordinated Evidence Ecosystem. Given a recommendation query and a fictional target product, our method builds a controlled evidence environment that coordinates an agent-facing navigation entry page with heterogeneous support pages. These pages use shared terminology, internal links, and consistent product attributes to introduce, verify, and reinforce the target product. We evaluate our method on OPR-Bench, a benchmark for open-ended product recommendation. Experiments show that it consistently outperforms page-level GEO baselines in final target recommendation. Trajectory-level metrics further show increased initial target-result crawls, target-specific follow-up searches, and internal-link crawls, suggesting that the gains come from shaping the agent's evidence-acquisition process rather than merely adding more target-related content. Overall, our findings support an ecosystem research paradigm for GEO, where web-enabled LLM agents are studied in relation to the broader evidence environments that guide search, browsing, and answer synthesis.

</details>


### [92] [LeanSearch v2: Global Premise Retrieval for Lean 4 Theorem Proving](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13137v2)
*Guoxiong Gao,Zeming Sun,Jiedong Jiang,Yutong Wang,Jingda Xu,Peihao Wu,Bryan Dai,Bin Dong*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 定理证明前提检索系统，涉及检索增强agent与基准

TL;DR: LeanSearch v2是一个双模式检索系统，用于Lean 4定理证明中的全局前提检索，通过嵌入-重排器流水线和迭代草图-检索-反思循环，显著提升了前提检索和证明生成的成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语义搜索引擎和前提选择系统分别针对单个声明检索和逐个策略步骤的前提预测，但无法恢复整个定理所需的所有前提集合，因此需要一种能够进行全局前提检索的系统。

Method: 提出LeanSearch v2，包含标准模式和推理模式。标准模式使用层次非正式化的Mathlib语料库和嵌入-重排器流水线进行单查询检索；推理模式基于标准模式，通过迭代草图-检索-反思循环实现全局前提检索。

Result: 在69个研究级Mathlib定理查询基准上，标准模式nDCG@10达0.62（优于次优系统的0.53），推理模式在10个候选中恢复46.1%的真实前提组（优于强推理检索系统的38.0%和前提选择基线的9.3%）。下游证明成功率20%（次优系统16%，无检索4%）。

Conclusion: LeanSearch v2在全局前提检索任务上取得了最先进的性能，并且检索质量能有效提升下游定理证明的成功率。所有代码、数据和基准已开源，标准模式提供公开API访问。

中文摘要：在Lean 4中证明定理通常需要识别一组分散的库引理，这些引理的联合使用能够实现简洁的证明——我们将此任务称为全局前提检索。现有工具解决邻近问题：语义搜索引擎找到与查询匹配的单个声明，而前提选择系统逐个策略步骤预测有用的引理。两者都无法恢复整个定理所需的前提集合。我们提出LeanSearch v2，一个针对此任务的双模式检索系统。其标准模式应用一个层次非正式化的Mathlib语料库，采用嵌入-重排器流水线，在无需领域特定微调的情况下实现了最先进的单查询检索（nDCG@10为0.62，而次优系统为0.53）。其推理模式以标准模式作为检索基础，通过迭代草图-检索-反思循环针对全局前提检索。在一个包含69个研究级Mathlib定理查询的基准测试中，推理模式在10个检索候选中恢复了46.1%的真实前提组，优于强推理检索系统（38.0%）和前提选择基线（9.3%）。在固定证明循环的受控下游评估中，用LeanSearch v2替代其他检索器获得了最高的证明成功率（20%，而次优系统为16%，无检索为4%），证实了检索质量可传播至证明生成。我们已开源所有代码、数据和基准测试。代码和数据：https://github.com/frenzymath/LeanSearch-v2 。标准模式可通过API公开访问：https://leansearch.net/。

Original abstract: Proving theorems in Lean 4 often requires identifying a scattered set of library lemmas whose joint use enables a concise proof -- a task we call global premise retrieval. Existing tools address adjacent problems: semantic search engines find individual declarations matching a query, while premise-selection systems predict useful lemmas one tactic step at a time. Neither recovers the full premise set an entire theorem requires. We present LeanSearch v2, a two-mode retrieval system for this task. Its standard mode applies a hierarchy-informalized Mathlib corpus with an embedding-reranker pipeline, achieving state-of-the-art single-query retrieval without domain-specific fine-tuning (nDCG@10 of 0.62 vs. 0.53 for the next-best system). Its reasoning mode builds on standard mode as its retrieval substrate, targeting global premise retrieval through iterative sketch-retrieve-reflect cycles. On a 69-query benchmark of research-level Mathlib theorems, reasoning mode recovers 46.1% of ground-truth premise groups within 10 retrieved candidates, outperforming strong reasoning retrieval systems (38.0%) and premise-selection baselines (9.3%) on the same benchmark. In a controlled downstream evaluation with a fixed prover loop, replacing alternative retrievers with LeanSearch v2 yields the highest proof success (20% vs. 16% for the next-best system and 4% without retrieval), confirming that retrieval quality propagates to proof generation. We have open-sourced all code, data, and benchmarks. Code and data: https://github.com/frenzymath/LeanSearch-v2 . The standard mode is publicly available with API access at https://leansearch.net/ .

</details>


### [93] [Thinking Ahead: Prospection-Guided Retrieval of Memory with Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14177v1)
*Harshita Chopra,Krishna Kant Chintalapudi,Suman Nath,Ryen W. White,Chirag Shah*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 前瞻引导检索结合Tree-of-Thought规划，提升长程检索，可迁移至agent记忆与规划

TL;DR: 提出前瞻引导检索（PGR），通过将用户查询扩展为思维树或线性链作为检索探针，迭代地发现相关记忆，在长期个性化检索中显著提升召回率和响应质量，在MemoryQuest上召回率提升近3倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准RAG和GraphRAG系统依赖嵌入相似性或固定图遍历，容易遗漏在嵌入空间中远离查询但对用户重要的相关事实，导致长期个性化检索效果不佳。

Method: PGR首先将用户查询扩展为一个简短的思维树（ToT）或线性链，生成合理的下一步作为检索探针；利用这些探针检索到的事实个性化下一轮的前瞻，从而迭代发现额外相关记忆。

Result: 在3个数据集的185个用户配置文件的1,625个查询上，PGR-TOT显著提升检索性能，在MemoryQuest上召回率相比最强基线提升近3倍；成对LLM评判中PGR响应在89-98%查询中被优先选择，人工标注也显示相同趋势。

Conclusion: 显式前瞻相比仅基于相似性的基线在长期检索和响应质量上带来巨大提升。

中文摘要：长期个性化要求对话助手从扩展的交互历史中检索用户特定的事实。在实践中，许多相关事实在密集检索下与查询的语义相似度往往较低。标准的检索增强生成（RAG）和GraphRAG系统在很大程度上仍然是回顾性的：它们依赖于与查询的嵌入相似性或固定的图遍历，因此常常遗漏对用户需求重要但在嵌入空间中远离查询的事实。受“前瞻”——人类利用想象的未来作为回忆线索的能力——的启发，我们引入了前瞻引导检索（PGR），它将检索与记忆存储方式解耦。给定一个用户查询，PGR首先将目标扩展为一个简短的思维树（ToT）或线性链，包含合理的下一步，并使用这些步骤作为检索探针，而不是仅依赖原始查询。这些探针检索到的事实随后被用于个性化下一轮的前瞻，使得PGR能够发现只有在模拟基于用户历史后才变得相关的额外记忆。我们还引入了MemoryQuest，一个具有挑战性的多会话基准测试，其中每个查询都标注了3-5个带日期的参考事实，且受到低查询-参考相似度的约束。在涵盖来自3个公开数据集的185个用户配置文件的1,625个查询中，PGR-TOT显著提高了检索性能，包括在MemoryQuest上相比最强基线的近3倍召回率。在与基线进行的成对LLM作为评判者的比较中，PGR生成的响应在89-98%的查询中被优先选择，而对保留子集的盲人标注也显示了相同的趋势。总体而言，结果表明，相对于仅基于相似性的基线，显式前瞻在长期检索和响应质量上带来了巨大提升。

Original abstract: Long-horizon personalization requires dialogue assistants to retrieve user-specific facts from extended interaction histories. In practice, many relevant facts often have low semanticsimilarity to the query under dense retrieval. Standard Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) and GraphRAG systems are still largely retrospective: they rely on embedding similarity to the query or on fixed graph traversals, so they often miss facts that matter for the user's needs but lie far from the query in embedding space. Inspired by prospection, the human ability to use imagined futures as cues for recall, we introduce Prospection-Guided Retrieval (PGR), which decouples retrieval from how memories are stored. Given a user query, PGR first expands the goal into a short Tree-of-Thought (ToT) or linear chain of plausible next steps, and uses these steps as retrieval probes rather than relying on the original query alone. The facts retrieved by these probes are then used to personalize the next round of prospection, enabling PGR to uncover additional memories that become relevant only after the simulation is grounded in the user's history. We also introduce MemoryQuest, a challenging multi-session benchmark in which each query is annotated with 3--5 dated reference facts subject to a low query-reference similarity constraint. Across 1,625 queries spanning 185 user profiles from 3 publicly available datasets, PGR-TOT substantially improves retrieval, including nearly 3x recall on MemoryQuest over the strongest baseline. In pairwise LLM-as-judge comparisons against baselines, PGR-generated responses are preferred on 89--98% of queries, with blinded human annotations on held-out subsets showing the same trend. Overall, the results demonstrate that explicit prospection yields large gains in long-horizon retrieval and response quality relative to similarity-only baselines.

</details>

### [94] [When Should an AI Workflow Release? Always-Valid Inference for Black-Box Generate-Verify Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12947v1)
*Young Hyun Cho,Will Wei Sun*

Main category: stat.ML

Selection reason: 提出generate-verify工作流的释放决策包装器，提供统计保障，可迁移至coding agent的验证与可靠性

TL;DR: 针对LLM工作流的迭代生成-评估-修改循环，提出一种始终有效的发布封装器，通过构建硬负例参考池和e-过程控制发布时机，确保对不可行任务的有限样本控制并允许可行任务发布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM工作流迭代产生候选结果时，存在何时停止并输出的发布决策。由于部署时评估得分是自适应且反复监控的，无法使用传统统计校准方法，亟需一种在可选停止下仍有效的发布控制方法。

Method: 提出始终有效的发布封装器：构建硬负例参考池（高分失败案例），用其对部署时评估得分进行校准，并通过e-过程累积证据，分离参考池的保守转化和e-过程的统计有效性。

Result: 理论上，保守参考池可在有限样本下控制对不可行任务的发布概率，并给出在可行任务上仍能非平凡发布的条件。案例研究（MBPP+编码智能体）显示，与基线停止规则相比，减少了过早错误发布，同时保持对可行任务的发布。

Conclusion: 该封装器有效平衡了LLM工作流中发布决策的风险与收益，为可选的迭代停止提供统计保障。

中文摘要：基于LLM的AI工作流日益通过迭代的生成-评估-修改循环产生输出。每次迭代可以改进候选结果，但也产生了一个发布决策：何时停止并输出当前结果？这带来了统计挑战，因为部署时的评估器得分是自适应生成并反复监控的，但通常用于校准的似然模型或可交换性假设却不可用。我们为现有的生成器-评估器流水线提出了一种始终有效的发布封装器。该封装器构建了一个由高分失败案例组成的硬负例参考池，将部署时的评估器得分与这个参考池进行校准，并通过e-过程累积由此产生的证据。这分离了两个角色：参考池将黑盒得分转化为保守证据，而e-过程在可选停止下提供有效性。理论上，我们证明保守的参考池可以在有限样本上控制对不可行任务（即给定工作流无法产生可靠解决方案的任务）发布概率。我们还描述了相同保守规则在可行任务上仍能实现非平凡发布的条件。在一个MBPP+编码智能体案例研究中，相对于基准停止规则，该封装器减少了过早的错误发布，同时仍在工作流反复累积适度支持证据的任务上发布。

Original abstract: LLM-enabled AI workflows increasingly produce outputs through iterative generate-evaluate-revise loops. Each iteration can improve the candidate, but it also creates a release decision: when to stop and output the current result? This raises a statistical challenge because deployment-time evaluator scores are adaptively generated and repeatedly monitored, yet the likelihood models or exchangeability assumptions typically used for calibration are unavailable. We propose an always-valid release wrapper for existing generator-evaluator pipelines. The wrapper builds a hard-negative reference pool of high-scoring failures, calibrates deployment-time evaluator scores against this pool, and accumulates the resulting evidence with an e-process. This separates two roles: the reference pool turns black-box scores into conservative evidence, while the e-process provides validity under optional stopping. In theory, we show that a conservative reference pool yields finite-sample control of the probability of releasing on infeasible tasks, that is, tasks for which the given workflow is not capable of producing a reliable solution. We also characterize conditions under which the same conservative rule still achieves nontrivial release on feasible tasks. In an MBPP+ coding-agent case study, the wrapper reduces premature incorrect release relative to baseline stopping rules while still releasing on tasks for which the workflow repeatedly accumulates moderate supporting evidence.

</details>

### [95] [No Attack Required: Semantic Fuzzing for Specification Violations in Agent Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13044v1)
*Ying Li,Hongbo Wen,Yanju Chen,Hanzhi Liu,Yuan Tian,Yu Feng*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 针对agent skill的语义fuzzing方法，发现规范违反，对agent安全评估有借鉴意义。

TL;DR: 提出Sefz框架，通过语义模糊测试自动发现LLM代理技能中的规范违反，在402个技能中发现29.9%存在违反，包括26个新的可利用漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法检测代理技能中因规范语义不完整或实现忽略约束而导致的规范违反，这些违反破坏用户信任且造成安全风险。

Method: Sefz将护栏转化为执行轨迹上的可达性目标，使用LLM变异器生成逼近违反模式的良性输入，并用多臂老虎机基于目标接近度引导搜索。

Result: 在402个真实技能中，Sefz发现120个（29.9%）存在规范违反，其中26个为以前未知的可利用护栏违反，并识别出六个常见规范陷阱。

Conclusion: Sefz能有效发现规范违反，其揭示的陷阱为设计更安全的代理技能提供了具体原则。

中文摘要：基于LLM的代理可以在用户日常请求下静默删除文档、泄露凭证或转移资金，这不是因为代理受到攻击，而是因为它调用的技能违反了自己声明的安全规则。我们称这些为规范违反：良性输入导致技能违反其自身规范中的自然语言护栏，通常是因为护栏的语义对于自主执行未定义，或者因为实现静默忽略了文档化的约束。这些违反对于静态分析器、传统模糊测试工具和提示注入防御都是不可见的，然而它们破坏了用户安装技能时所信任的契约。我们提出了Sefz，一个目标导向的语义模糊测试框架，能够自动发现代理技能中的规范违反。Sefz将每个护栏转化为带注释的执行轨迹上的可达性目标，将违反检查简化为确定性图查询。基于LLM的变异器生成良性输入，其轨迹逐步接近违反模式，由多臂老虎机引导，该老虎机使用目标接近度作为奖励信号。在来自最大公共代理技能市场的402个真实世界技能上，Sefz在120个（29.9%）中发现了规范违反，包括在已部署技能中发现的26个以前未知的可利用护栏违反。六个反复出现的规范陷阱解释了大部分失败，为更安全的技能设计提供了具体原则。

Original abstract: LLM-powered agents can silently delete documents, leak credentials, or transfer funds on a routine user request, not because the agent was attacked, but because the skill it invoked broke its own declared safety rules. We call these specification violations: benign inputs cause a skill to breach the natural-language guardrails in its own specification, typically because the guardrail's semantics are undefined for autonomous execution, or because the implementation silently ignores the documented constraint. These violations are invisible to static analyzers, traditional fuzzers, and prompt-injection defenses alike, yet they undermine the very contract a user trusts when installing a skill.
  We present Sefz, a goal-directed semantic fuzzing framework that automatically discovers specification violations in agent skills. Sefz translates each guardrail into a reachability goal over an annotated execution trace, reducing violation checking to a deterministic graph query. An LLM-based mutator generates benign inputs whose traces progressively approach the violation patterns, guided by a multi-armed bandit that uses goal-proximity as its reward signal.
  On 402 real-world skills from the largest public agent-skill marketplace, Sefz finds specification violations in 120 (29.9%), including 26 previously unknown exploitable guardrail violations in deployed skills. Six recurring specification pitfalls explain the bulk of the failures, suggesting concrete principles for safer skill design.

</details>


### [96] [Security Incentivization: An Empirical Study of how Micropayments Impact Code Security](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13100v1)
*Stefan Rass,Martin Pinzger,Rainer W. Alexandrowicz,Georg Sengstbratl,Johann Glock,Alexander Lercher,Fabian Oraze,Christoph Wedenig*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过团队级激励与自动化安全指标挂钩，在课程实验中显著降低了代码安全缺陷密度，且非代码量增加所致，为实践提供可行方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安全投入不足，因为不直接产生可见价值，需要评估团队激励措施的效果。

Method: 半自动化机制聚合静态分析工具结果，计算安全缺陷密度，基于相对改进比例奖励；在84名学生14个团队的课程实验中进行对照比较。

Result: 激励组安全缺陷密度显著降低（β = -0.396, p = 0.0342），存在前后端异质性，代码行数无显著差异，工具链可脚本化。

Conclusion: 与自动化安全指标对齐的奖励可改善代码安全性，建议在专业和长期开发中进一步验证。

中文摘要：安全通常得不到开发人员的足够关注，因为它不能直接产生可见的价值，导致实践中投入不足。我们评估了一种通过团队级激励与可衡量的安全改进挂钩的应对措施。我们的半自动化机制汇总了来自 Bearer、Detekt 和 mobsfscan 的静态分析结果，计算安全缺陷密度，并根据团队在迭代间的相对改进比例给予奖励，从而实现可重复、可脚本化的大规模报告。在 84 名来自 14 个团队的学生参与的受控课程实验中，我们将安全激励条件（奖励分数与安全扫描结果挂钩）与具有相同评分方案的控制条件进行了比较。实验组总体实现了显著更低的安全缺陷密度（β 回归：β = -0.396，p = 0.0342），表明在激励下可衡量的安全性得到改善。在控制平台后，我们观察到明显的前端/后端差异：后端在激励下显示出更少的缺陷和更高的改进比例，突出了不同技术栈层之间的异质性效应。值得注意的是，这些收益并非代码量膨胀的副产品，因为代码行数在两组间随时间增加情况相似。测量流水线和工具链被证明适合脚本化和自动化，支持在实践中规模化采用。我们的结果表明，将奖励与自动化安全指标对齐可以切实改善代码安全性，值得在专业环境和更长的开发周期中进一步跟进。

Original abstract: Security often receives insufficient developer attention because it does not directly generate visible value, leading to underinvestment in practice. We evaluate a countermeasure by team-level incentives tied to measurable security improvements over time. Our semi-automated mechanism aggregates static analysis findings from Bearer, Detekt, and mobsfscan, computes security issue density, and rewards teams based on the relative improvement ratio across sprints, enabling repeatable, scriptable reporting at scale.
  In a controlled course experiment with 84 students across 14 teams, we compared a security-incentivized condition, in which bonus points were linked to security scanner results, against a control condition with an otherwise identical grading scheme. The treatment group achieved significantly lower security issue density overall (beta regression: $β= -0.396, p = 0.0342$), indicating improved measurable security under incentivization. After controlling for platform, we observed a marked front-end/back-end disparity, with back-ends showing fewer issues and higher improvement ratios under incentives, highlighting heterogeneous effects across stack layers. Notably, these gains were not the byproduct of inflated code volume, as lines of code increased similarly across groups over time. The measurement pipeline and toolchain proved feasible for scripting and automation, supporting scalable adoption in practice.
  Our results suggest that aligning rewards with automated security metrics can measurably improve code security and merit follow-up in professional contexts and longer development lifecycles.

</details>


### [97] [Automatic Detection of Reference Counting Bugs in Linux Kernel Drivers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13246v2)
*Joe Hattori,Naoki Kobayashi,Ken Sakayori*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: DrvHorn是一个自动化工具，通过将引用计数验证转化为断言检查，高效检测Linux内核驱动中的引用计数错误，发现了大量新错误并提交了补丁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Linux内核驱动中的引用计数错误会导致严重的资源管理不善和安全漏洞，亟需高效的自动化检测工具。

Method: 将引用计数验证简化为利用Linux驱动接口的断言检查问题，结合对Linux内核的高效建模和积极的程序切片。

Result: 在v6.6 Linux内核的所有平台驱动中检测到545个错误，其中424个为之前未知，假阳性率为29.9%，提交的补丁中有45个已被合并。

Conclusion: DrvHorn能够有效检测和帮助修复Linux内核驱动中的引用计数错误，具有较低假阳性率，实用性强。

中文摘要：Linux内核驱动中的引用计数错误可能导致严重的资源管理不善和安全漏洞。我们引入了DrvHorn，一种新颖的自动化工具，通过将引用计数验证简化为利用Linux驱动接口的断言检查问题来检测这些错误。通过对Linux内核的高效建模和积极的程序切片，DrvHorn在v6.6 Linux内核的所有平台驱动中发现了545个错误，其中424个是先前未知的，并且与先前的研究相比，其假阳性率较低，为29.9%。为了解决这些新发现错误的根本原因，我们向Linux内核提交了补丁，其中45个已被合并。

Original abstract: Reference counting bugs in Linux kernel drivers can lead to severe resource mismanagement and security vulnerabilities. We introduce DrvHorn, a novel automated tool to detect these bugs by reducing reference counting verification to an assertion checking problem leveraging the Linux driver interface. Through efficient modeling of the Linux kernel and aggressive program slicing, DrvHorn discovered 545 bugs, of which 424 were previously unknown, across all platform drivers in v6.6 Linux kernel, with a lower false positive rate of 29.9% compared to prior studies. To address the root causes of these newly discovered bugs, we submitted patches to the Linux kernel, and 45 of them were merged.

### [98] [AgentTrap: Measuring Runtime Trust Failures in Third-Party Agent Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13940v1)
*Haomin Zhuang,Hanwen Xing,Yujun Zhou,Yuchen Ma,Yue Huang,Yili Shen,Yufei Han,Xiangliang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: AgentTrap: 第三方agent技能运行时安全基准，直接相关agent安全与评测。

TL;DR: 提出AgentTrap基准测试，评估LLM智能体使用第三方技能时的安全性，发现模型常将恶意副作用视为正常流程，而非简单越狱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 第三方技能带来安全威胁，恶意技能可伪装成常规工作流被执行，现有评估不足，需动态基准测试运行时安全性。

Method: 构建包含141个任务（91恶意、50良性）的AgentTrap基准，覆盖16个安全维度，在沙盒环境中执行并分析完整轨迹。

Result: 模型常完成用户任务但忽略技能引入的副作用，失败非简单越狱，需运行时评估。

Conclusion: 应重视具体模型-框架-工作区环境下的运行时评估，以防范第三方技能的安全风险。

中文摘要：第三方技能正成为LLM智能体的包生态系统。它们将自然语言指令、辅助脚本、模板、文档和服务配置打包成可重用工作流。这使得技能非常有用，但也引入了一个新的安全问题：恶意技能无需要求模型执行明显有害的操作。相反，它可以伪装有害行为作为例行工作流的一部分，依靠智能体以高价值权限和有限人工监督来执行该工作流。我们引入了AgentTrap，这是一个动态基准测试，用于评估LLM智能体是否能在使用第三方技能的同时抵抗恶意运行时行为。AgentTrap包含141个任务：91个恶意任务和50个良性实用任务，覆盖了基于智能体技能供应链威胁的16个安全影响维度。在每个任务中，智能体接收普通的用户请求，运行已安装的、可能包含恶意工作流元素的技能，并在沙盒环境中执行。AgentTrap然后根据完整轨迹判断攻击成功、阻止或拒绝的行为、未触发攻击的情况以及无攻击证据的结果。我们的核心发现是，最具信息性的失败并非简单的越狱。模型通常完成可见的用户任务，同时将技能引入的不安全副作用视为正常工作流的一部分。这激发了对用户实际委托工作的具体模型-框架-工作区环境的运行时评估。代码和数据可在https://github.com/zhmzm/AgentTrap和https://huggingface.co/datasets/zhmzm/AgentTrap获取。

Original abstract: Third-party skills are becoming the package ecosystem for LLM agents. They package natural-language instructions, helper scripts, templates, documents, and service configuration into reusable workflows. This makes skills useful, but it also introduces a new security problem: a malicious skill does not need to ask the model to perform an obviously harmful action. Instead, it can disguise the harmful behavior as part of a routine workflow, relying on the agent to execute that workflow with high-value permissions and limited human supervision.
  We introduce AgentTrap, a dynamic benchmark for evaluating whether LLM agents can use third-party skills while resisting malicious runtime behavior. AgentTrap contains 141 tasks: 91 malicious tasks and 50 benign utility tasks, covering 16 security-impact dimensions grounded in agent-skill supply-chain threats. In each task, the agent receives an ordinary user request, runs with installed skills that may contain malicious workflow elements, and is executed in a sandboxed environment. AgentTrap then judges complete trajectories for attack success, blocked or refused behavior, attack-not-triggered cases, and no-attack-evidence outcomes. Our central finding is that the most informative failures are not simple jailbreaks. Models often complete the visible user task while treating unsafe side effects introduced by the skill as part of the normal workflow. This motivates runtime evaluation of the concrete model--framework--workspace environment in which users actually delegate work. Code and data are available at https://github.com/zhmzm/AgentTrap and https://huggingface.co/datasets/zhmzm/AgentTrap.

</details>


### [99] [ExploitBench: A Capability Ladder Benchmark for LLM Cybersecurity Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14153v1)
*Seunghyun Lee,David Brumley*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: LLM agent能力阶梯基准，聚焦漏洞利用，为agent评测和工具使用提供参考

TL;DR: ExploitBench将利用分解为16个分级能力，应用于V8漏洞，揭示了公开模型与私有模型在实现任意代码执行上的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准将利用视为二元事件（崩溃与否），忽略了从触发漏洞到完全控制的中间关键步骤，需要更细粒度的能力评估。

Method: 设计ExploitBench，包含16个能力标志，通过确定性预言机（随机化挑战-响应、差异执行、信号处理器证明）验证。在41个V8漏洞上测试，设置三个实验分支：<模型,环境>、<模型,环境,自适应辅导>和<模型,环境,框架>。

Result: 公开模型普遍能触发崩溃，但极少实现任意代码执行；私有模型在约一半漏洞上实现了任意代码执行，表明存在显著能力差距。

Conclusion: 针对加固目标的利用构建是一项新兴的前沿能力，私有模型在该能力上领先于公开模型。

中文摘要：利用不是二元事件。它是一个获取渐进能力的阶梯，从执行单个有缺陷的代码行到完全控制目标。然而，现有的LLM安全基准将崩溃视为利用成功。这种单一的二元结果忽略了利用的难点：从触发漏洞到构建可重用原语和控制的过渡。我们提出了ExploitBench，一个能力分级的基准，它将利用分解为16个可测量的标志，从覆盖率和崩溃到沙箱原语、任意读写、控制流劫持和任意代码执行。每个能力都由确定性预言机验证，该预言机使用每次运行随机化的挑战-响应原语、针对地面真实二进制文件的差异执行来测量进度，以及用于代码执行的信号处理器证明。我们在41个V8漏洞上实例化了ExploitBench，因为V8既广泛部署又经过了利用加固。我们报告了三个分支：<模型，环境>作为模型-环境能力的主要测量，<模型，环境，自适应辅导>作为添加自适应辅导以测试定向反馈是否改变结果的次要分支，以及<模型，环境，框架>作为消融实验，替换为模型的原生CLI，以检查供应商端优化是否增加了利用能力。我们的结果显示，公开部署的前沿模型与私有前沿模型之间存在显著的能力差距。在测试的8个公开部署的模型中，到达易受攻击的代码并触发崩溃是常规操作，但任意代码执行则不是。私有模型在约一半的情况下实现了任意代码执行。总体而言，结果表明针对加固目标的利用构建是一项新兴的前沿能力。

Original abstract: Exploitation is not a binary event. It is a ladder of acquiring progressive capabilities, from executing a single buggy line of code to taking full control of the target. However, existing LLM security benchmarks treat a crash as exploitation success. That single binary outcome collapses the hard parts of exploitation: the transition from triggering a bug to constructing reusable primitives and control.
  We present ExploitBench, a capability-graded benchmark that decomposes exploitation into 16 measurable flags, from coverage and crash through sandbox primitives, arbitrary read/write, control-flow hijack, and arbitrary code execution. Each capability is verified by a deterministic oracle that uses a per-run randomized challenge-response for primitives, differential execution against ground-truth binaries to measure progress, and a signal-handler proof for code execution.
  We instantiate ExploitBench on 41 V8 bugs because V8 is both widely deployed and exploitation-hardened. We report three arms: <model,env> as the primary measurement of model-environment capability, <model,env, adaptive coaching> as a secondary arm that adds adaptive coaching to test whether targeted feedback shifts outcomes, and <model,env,harness> as an ablation that swaps in the model's native CLI to check whether vendor-side optimizations increase exploitation capabilities.
  Our results show a sharp capability split between publicly deployed frontier models and the private frontier. Across the 8 publicly deployed models tested, reaching the vulnerable code and triggering a crash is routine, but arbitrary code execution is not. The private model shows arbitrary code execution on approximately half. Overall, results suggest that exploit construction against hardened targets is an emerging frontier capability.

</details>

# cs.AR [[Back]](#toc)

### [100] [Is Agentic AI Ready for Real-World Hardware Engineering? A Deep Dive with Phoenix-bench](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15226v1)
*Qingyun Zou,Feng Yu,Hongshi Tan,Bingsheng He,WengFai Wong*

Main category: cs.AR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了Phoenix-bench基准测试，用于评估AI智能体在硬件工程中的表现，发现软件和硬件任务存在根本差异，硬件错误需要跨层级信号流跟踪，而测试用例反馈能显著提升解决率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有硬件LLM基准测试仅孤立处理子任务，缺乏能联合评估仓库导航、层级感知定位、EDA验证和补丁维护能力的完整基准；同时软件调优的智能体在硬件任务上表现不佳，需要专门评估。

Method: 构建包含511个Verilator实例的Phoenix-bench语料库，每个实例附带开发者补丁、设计流程标签、多个测试台和Docker固定的EDA环境。统一评估4个商业和8个开源智能体结构，使用4种LLM骨干，并进行文件级定位预言和测试台日志反馈两种诊断性干预。

Result: 发现：(i) 智能体从软件到硬件任务性能下降37-58%，原因是硬件错误通过信号流传播而非调用图；(ii) 失败主要集中在控制流/FSM错误、测试台错误和跨层级信号流跟踪；(iii) 文件级定位仅提升1.4%，而一轮测试反馈提升42-45%。

Conclusion: 硬件工程需要与软件工程不同的智能体能力，测试用例反馈是提升硬件修复率的关键，而精准定位本身不足以带来显著改进。

中文摘要：我们探究为软件工程构建的智能AI系统是否能迁移到现实的硬件工程中。现有的硬件大语言模型基准测试孤立地处理子任务，但没有一个能同时要求仓库导航、层级感知定位、电子设计自动化（EDA）可执行验证和维护风格的补丁。我们提出了Phoenix-bench，一个同步的语料库，包含来自114个GitHub仓库的511个经过验证的Verilator实例，每个实例都附带了开发者补丁、设计流程标签、失败到通过和通过到通过的测试台，以及一个Docker固定的EDA环境，使得解决率差异反映的是智能体行为而非工具链可用性。利用Phoenix-bench，我们对四个商业智能体和八个开源智能体结构进行了统一评估，涉及四个大语言模型骨干，外加两种诊断性干预（文件级定位预言和一轮测试台日志反馈）。出现了三个发现。(i) 软件和硬件本质上是不同的工程任务：同一智能体从SWE-bench Verified到Phoenix-bench性能下降了37%到58%，因为硬件错误通过信号流在并行实例化的模块间传播，而非沿着软件风格的调用图，并且软件调优的智能体会停在症状文件处，而不是通过实例化链回溯。(ii) 失败集中在设计控制流/有限状态机（FSM）错误、验证测试台错误，以及需要跨层级信号流跟踪和协调多文件编辑的困难案例。(iii) 定位粒度比定位本身重要得多：完美的文件级预言仅提升1.4%，因为智能体会破坏无需编辑的文件，而一轮测试用例反馈将解决率提高42%到45%，因为测试用例告知了错误的位置以及修复必须采取的形式。

Original abstract: We ask whether agentic AI systems built for software engineering transfer to realistic hardware engineering. Existing hardware LLM benchmarks isolate sub-tasks but none jointly requires repository navigation, hierarchy-aware localization, Electronic Design Automation (EDA) executable verification, and maintenance-style patching. We introduce \textbf{Phoenix-bench}, a synchronized corpus of 511 verified Verilator instances from 114 GitHub repositories, each shipped with the developer patch, design-flow labels, fail-to-pass and pass-to-pass testbenches, and a Docker-pinned EDA environment so resolved-rate differences reflect agent behavior rather than toolchain availability. Using Phoenix-bench we run a uniform evaluation of four commercial agents and eight open-source agentic structures across four LLM backbones, plus two diagnostic interventions (file-level oracle localization and one round of testbench-log feedback). Three findings emerge. (i)~Software and hardware are fundamentally different engineering tasks: the same agent loses 37\% to 58\% from SWE-bench Verified to Phoenix-bench because hardware bugs propagate across parallel instantiated modules through signal flow rather than along a software-style call graph, and software-tuned agents stop at the symptom file instead of tracing back through the instantiation chain. (ii)~Failures concentrate on design control-flow / finite state machine (FSM) bugs, verification testbench bugs, and hard cases that demand cross-hierarchy signal-flow tracking and coordinated multi-file edits. (iii)~Localization granularity matters far more than localization itself: a perfect file-level oracle yields only $+1.4$\% because the agent then breaks files that did not need editing, while a single round of test case feedback lifts resolved rate by $42$\% to $45$\% because the test case tells \emph{where} the bug is and \emph{what} the fix has to look like.

</details>

# cs.MA [[Back]](#toc)

### [101] [ChipMATE: Multi-Agent Training via Reinforcement Learning for Enhanced RTL Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12857v1)
*Zhongkai Yu,Yichen Lin,Chenyang Zhou,Yuwei Zhang,Kun Zhou,Junxia Cui,Haotian Ye,Zhengding Hu,Zaifeng Pan,Ruiyi Wang,Yujie Zhao,Hejia Zhang,Jingbo Shang,Jishen Zhao,Yufei Ding*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent框架用于RTL代码生成，直接相关coding agent与代码优化。

TL;DR: ChipMATE是一个自训练的多智能体框架，通过Verilog智能体和Python参考模型智能体相互验证，实现了优于现有模型（包括大规模闭源模型）的RTL代码生成性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有API-based智能体系统假设黄金测试平台、依赖闭源API、无法利用专有数据，而自训练模型是单轮生成器，忽略了验证在工业流程中的关键作用。

Method: 提出ChipMATE，包含Verilog智能体和Python参考模型智能体对，通过回溯推理工作流防止错误传播，采用两阶段训练（先单独训练各智能体，再联合训练）和混合数据生成框架（产生64.4K训练样本）。

Result: 在VerilogEval V2上，4B和9B基础模型分别达到75.0%和80.1% pass@1，超越所有现有自训练模型及DeepSeek V4（1600B参数）。

Conclusion: ChipMATE展示了自训练多智能体框架在RTL生成中的有效性，弥合了现有方法与工业实践之间的差距，代码和模型权重已开源。

中文摘要：现有的基于API的RTL代码生成智能体系统从根本上与工业实践不一致：它们假设在生成时存在一个黄金测试平台，依赖于与芯片供应商气隙安全要求不兼容的闭源API，并且无法在供应商的专有RTL代码库上进行训练，使得宝贵的内部数据未被利用。最近的自训练模型解决了部署限制，但仍然是单轮生成器，忽略了验证在真实工业流程中的关键作用。为了弥合这些差距，我们提出了ChipMATE，这是第一个用于RTL生成的自训练多智能体框架。受工业实践的启发，其中正确性来自于独立编写的RTL模块和参考模型之间的交叉比较，ChipMATE将一个Verilog智能体与一个Python参考模型智能体配对，这两个智能体在没有任何黄金标准的情况下相互验证对方的输出。我们设计了一个基于回溯的推理工作流，以防止错误在轮次之间传播，以及一个两阶段训练流程，首先单独训练每个智能体以饱和其代码生成能力，然后联合训练团队以有效协作。为了支持训练，我们进一步构建了一个混合数据生成框架，产生了64.4K高质量参考模型训练样本。ChipMATE在VerilogEval V2上使用4B和9B基础模型分别实现了75.0%和80.1%的pass@1，优于所有现有的自训练模型，甚至优于拥有1600B参数的DeepSeek V4。我们的代码和模型权重在https://github.com/zhongkaiyu/ChipMATE上公开。

Original abstract: Existing API-based agentic systems for RTL code generation are fundamentally misaligned with industrial practice: they assume a golden testbench is available at generation time, rely on closed-source APIs incompatible with chip vendors' air-gapped security requirements, and cannot be trained on vendors' proprietary RTL codebases, leaving valuable internal data unused. Recent self-trained models address the deployment constraint but remain single-turn generators that overlook the critical role of verification in real industrial flows.
  To bridge these gaps, we present ChipMATE, the first self-trained multi-agent framework for RTL generation. Inspired by industrial practice where correctness emerges from cross-comparison between independently written RTL modules and reference models, ChipMATE pairs a Verilog agent with a Python reference-model agent that mutually verify each other's outputs without any golden oracle. We design a backtrack-based inference workflow to prevent error propagation across turns, and a two-stage training pipeline that first trains each agent individually to saturate its code-generation capability, then trains the team jointly to collaborate effectively. To support the training, we further build a hybrid data-generation framework that produces 64.4K high-quality reference model training samples. ChipMATE achieves 75.0\% and 80.1\% pass@1 on VerilogEval V2 with 4B and 9B base models, outperforming all existing self-trained models and even DeepSeek V4 with 1600B parameters. Our code and model weights are publicly available in https://github.com/zhongkaiyu/ChipMATE.

</details>


### [102] [Embodied Multi-Agent Coordination by Aligning World Models Through Dialogue](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12920v3)
*Vardhan Dongre,Dilek Hakkani-Tür*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent对话对齐世界模型，可迁移至协作coding agent。

TL;DR: 本文研究基于LLM的具身智能体在部分可观测环境中的沟通能力，通过扩展PARTNR基准加入对话通道，并提出世界模型对齐度量，实验发现对话减少冲突但降低成功率，揭示了表面协调与真实对齐之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具身智能体协作需要沟通来对齐世界模型，但现有LLM智能体是否真正具备沟通能力未知。

Method: 扩展PARTNR基准增加自然语言对话通道，提出世界模型对齐框架（观察收敛、信息新颖性、信念敏感消息传递），在三个LLM上进行实验。

Result: 对话将动作冲突减少40-83个百分点，但任务成功率低于静默协调。

Conclusion: 当前LLM智能体在对话中实现了部分表面协调，但尚未达到真正的世界模型对齐，存在差距。

中文摘要：具身智能体之间的有效协作不仅需要在共享环境中行动，还需要基于每个智能体不断发展的对世界的理解进行沟通。当智能体只能部分观察其周围环境时，没有沟通的协调被证明是困难的，但原则上，沟通可以通过允许智能体分享观察结果并对其世界模型来弥合这一差距。在这项工作中，我们检查基于LLM的具身智能体是否真正实现了沟通能力。我们扩展了PARTNR（一个协作家庭机器人基准测试），增加了一个自然语言对话通道，使两个具有部分可观测性的智能体能够在任务执行期间进行沟通。为了评估对话是否导致真正的世界模型对齐而非表面协调，我们提出了一个衡量世界模型对齐的框架，该框架基于每个智能体的世界图定义：观察收敛（私有世界模型是否随时间对齐？）、信息新颖性（消息是否传达了合作伙伴缺乏的信息？）以及信念敏感消息传递（智能体是否对其合作伙伴知道什么进行建模？）。我们在三个LLM上的实验表明，与静默协调相比，对话将动作冲突减少了40到83个百分点，但降低了任务成功率。使用我们的指标，我们描述了表面协调与真正世界模型对齐之间的差距，并确定了当前模型在这个谱系中的位置。

Original abstract: Effective collaboration between embodied agents requires more than acting in a shared environment; it demands communication grounded in each agent's evolving understanding of the world. When agents can only partially observe their surroundings, coordination without communication is provably hard, but communication can, in principle, bridge this gap by allowing agents to share observations and align their world models. In this work, we examine whether LLM-based embodied agents actually realize the ability to communicate. We extend PARTNR, a benchmark for collaborative household robotics, with a natural-language dialogue channel that enables two agents with partial observability to communicate during task execution. To evaluate whether dialogue leads to genuine world-model alignment rather than superficial coordination, we propose a framework for measuring world-model alignment defined over per-agent world graphs: observation convergence (do private world models align over time?), information novelty (do messages convey what the partner lacks?), and belief-sensitive messaging (do agents model what their partner knows?). Our experiments across three LLMs reveal that dialogue reduces action conflicts 40 to 83 percentage points but degrades task success relative to silent coordination. Using our metrics, we characterize the gap between superficial coordination and genuine world-model alignment, and identify where current models fall on this spectrum. Project Website: https://uiuc-conversational-ai-lab.github.io/partnr-dial-wmd/

</details>


### [103] [Counterfactual Reasoning for Causal Responsibility Attribution in Probabilistic Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13077v1)
*Chunyan Mu,Muhammad Najib*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent系统中反事实责任归因，涉及策略推理与责任分配，对agent协作有参考意义。

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于沙普利值的追溯性反事实责任分配方法，用于并发随机博弈中的多智能体系统，并构建了支持验证和策略推理的形式化框架，同时展示了在纳什均衡下如何计算兼顾责任与预期奖励的稳定策略配置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统中智能体对结果的责任分配是设计和分析中的基本挑战，现有方法缺乏对责任与奖励权衡的考虑。

Method: 将系统建模为并发随机多玩家博弈；引入追溯性反事实责任概念量化责任；利用沙普利值分配责任并证明其性质；采用纳什均衡作为解概念计算稳定策略配置。

Result: 证明了沙普利值方法满足公平性和一致性；提出了一个支持验证和策略推理的形式化框架；成功计算了纳什均衡下的稳定策略配置。

Conclusion: 该方法能够公平一致地分配责任，并为多智能体系统中责任与奖励的权衡提供了理论依据和计算框架。

中文摘要：责任分配——确定智能体对结果负责的程度——是多智能体系统设计和分析中的一个基本挑战。在这项工作中，我们将此类系统建模为并发随机多玩家博弈，并引入了一种追溯性（向后）反事实责任的概念，该概念量化了给定策略配置下智能体对结果的责任。为了在智能体之间分配责任，我们利用沙普利值，并形式化地证明了该方法满足关键期望性质，包括公平性和一致性。在此基础上，我们提出了一个形式化框架，支持责任感知多智能体系统中的验证和策略推理。此外，通过采用纳什均衡作为解概念，我们展示了如何计算稳定的策略配置，其中智能体在责任和预期奖励之间进行权衡。

Original abstract: Responsibility allocation -- determining the extent to which agents are accountable for outcomes -- is a fundamental challenge in the design and analysis of multi-agent systems. In this work, we model such systems as concurrent stochastic multi-player games and introduce a notion of retrospective (backward) counterfactual responsibility, which quantifies an agent's accountability for outcomes resulting from a given strategy profile. To allocate responsibility among agents, we utilise the Shapley value and formally show that this method satisfies key desirable properties, including fairness and consistency. Building on this foundation, we propose a formal framework that supports both verification and strategic reasoning in responsibility-aware multi-agent systems. Furthermore, by adopting Nash equilibrium as the solution concept, we demonstrate how to compute stable strategy profiles in which agents trade off responsibility against expected reward.

</details>


### [104] [When Does Hierarchy Help? Benchmarking Agent Coordination in Event-Driven Industrial Scheduling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13172v1)
*Ziqi Wang,Yuhao Yang,Zhiwei Ling,Wenzhuo Qian,Hailiang Zhao*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 事件驱动多agent协调基准，评估不同协调范式的权衡

TL;DR: 提出了DESBench基准，用于评估层级事件驱动调度中的四种协调范式，揭示了集中式、层级式、异层级式和全息式协调之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准主要在弱耦合环境中评估任务完成，缺乏对共享动态演化系统中层级和耦合约束下协调范式何时成功或失败的研究。

Method: 构建基于工业调度共享离散事件驱动环境的DESBench基准，定义多时间尺度决策、部分可观测性和动态耦合约束的任务与指标，评估集中式、层级式、异层级式和全息式四种协调范式。

Result: 集中式协调鲁棒且通信高效但扩展性差；层级式协调通过分解提高效率但存在跨层级错位；异层级式协调灵活但通信开销大；全息式协调约束满足好但失去全局鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 协调设计从根本上塑造了复杂环境中智能体系统的行为，揭示了仅由结果指标无法捕获的结构性权衡，未来需要更自适应、有原则和动态的协调机制。

中文摘要：近期在智能体与多智能体系统方面的进展在工具使用、推理和协作任务上表现强劲。然而，现有基准大多在弱耦合环境中评估任务完成情况，对于在具有层级和耦合约束的共享动态演化系统中协调的研究支持有限。这留下了一个重要的未探索问题：不同的协调范式何时成功或失败？我们提出了分布式事件驱动调度基准（DESBench），一个用于评估层级事件驱动调度中智能体协调的基准。基于工业调度中的共享离散事件驱动环境，我们的基准捕捉了多时间尺度决策、部分可观测性和动态耦合约束。我们定义了评估有效性、约束对齐、协调效率和鲁棒性的任务和指标，并聚焦于四种代表性协调范式：集中式、层级式、异层级式和全息式。这些范式对应于信息流、决策权和冲突解决的不同机制。我们的对照评估揭示了清晰的协调权衡：集中式协调鲁棒且通信高效，但随难度增加扩展性差；层级式协调通过分解提高了效率，但面临跨层级错位；异层级式协调灵活但通信开销大；全息式协调约束满足良好但失去了全局鲁棒性。这些发现表明，协调设计从根本上塑造了复杂环境中智能体系统的行为，揭示了无法仅由结果指标捕获的结构性权衡，并强调了未来多智能体系统研究中更自适应、有原则和动态协调机制的必要性。

Original abstract: Recent advances in agent and multi-agent systems have shown strong performance on tool use, reasoning, and collaborative tasks. However, existing benchmarks mostly evaluate task completion in weakly coupled environments, and provide limited support for studying coordination in shared, dynamically evolving systems with hierarchy and coupled constraints. This leaves an important question underexplored: when do different coordination paradigms succeed or fail? We introduce Distributed Event-driven Scheduling Benchmark (DESBench), a benchmark for evaluating agent coordination in hierarchical event-driven scheduling. Built on a shared discrete-event driven environment in industrial scheduling, our benchmark captures multi-timescale decision making, partial observability, and dynamically coupled constraints. We define tasks and metrics that evaluate effectiveness, constraint alignment, coordination efficiency, and robustness, and focus on four representative coordination paradigms: centralized, hierarchical, heterarchical, and holonic. These paradigms correspond to distinct mechanisms of information flow, decision authority, and conflict resolution. Our controlled evaluations reveal clear coordination trade-offs: centralized coordination is robust and communication-efficient but scales poorly with difficulty; hierarchical coordination improves efficiency through decomposition but suffers from cross-level misalignment; heterarchical coordination is flexible but communication-heavy; and holonic coordination satisfies constraints well but loses global robustness. These findings demonstrate that coordination design fundamentally shapes agent system behavior in complex environments, revealing structural trade-offs that cannot be captured by outcome metrics alone and underscoring the imperative for more adaptive, principled, and dynamic coordination mechanisms in future MAS research.

</details>

### [105] [Context Training with Active Information Seeking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13050v2)
*Zeyu Huang,Adhiguna Kuncoro,Qixuan Feng,Jiajun Shen,Lucio Dery,Arthur Szlam,Marc'Aurelio Ranzato*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 使用工具主动搜索优化LLM上下文，对agent工具使用和上下文优化有启发。

TL;DR: 通过为LLM上下文优化器添加主动信息检索工具并结合基于搜索的候选上下文训练，显著提升了模型在多种任务上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM适应方法成本高且依赖内在知识，需要更高效、能利用外部信息的适应方案。

Method: 在上下文优化框架中集成Wikipedia搜索和浏览器工具，并采用基于搜索的训练过程维护和修剪多个候选上下文。

Result: 在低资源翻译、健康任务和推理任务上取得一致且显著的性能提升，且方法数据高效、鲁棒性好。

Conclusion: 主动信息检索结合搜索训练能有效提升LLM下游任务适应能力，且生成上下文具有模型泛化性。

中文摘要：现有的大多数大型语言模型（LLM）在部署后适应成本高昂，尤其是当任务需要新产生的信息或小众领域知识时。近期研究表明，通过操纵和优化其上下文，可以在不更新权重的情况下使LLM适应下游任务。然而，现有大多数方法仍然是闭环的，仅依赖模型的内在知识。在本文中，我们为这些上下文优化器配备了维基百科搜索和浏览器工具，以进行主动信息检索。我们发现，将这些工具简单地添加到标准的顺序上下文优化流程中，实际上可能比基线方法降低性能。然而，当与一种基于搜索的训练过程相结合，该过程维护和修剪多个候选上下文时，主动信息检索能够带来一致且显著的性能提升。我们在不同领域展示了这些改进，包括低资源翻译（Flores+）、健康场景（HealthBench）以及推理密集型任务（LiveCodeBench和Humanity's Last Exam）。此外，我们的方法被证明是数据高效的、对不同超参数具有鲁棒性，并且能够生成在不同模型间泛化良好的有效文本上下文。

Original abstract: Most existing large language models (LLMs) are expensive to adapt after deployment, especially when a task requires newly produced information or niche domain knowledge. Recent work has shown that, by manipulating and optimizing their context, LLMs can be tailored to downstream tasks without updating their weights. However, most existing methods remain closed-loop, relying solely on the model's intrinsic knowledge. In this paper, we equip these context optimizers with Wikipedia search and browser tools for active information seeking. We show that naively adding these tools to a standard sequential context optimization pipeline can actually degrade performance compared to baselines. However, when paired with a search-based training procedure that maintains and prunes multiple candidate contexts, active information seeking delivers consistent and substantial gains. We demonstrate these improvements across diverse domains, including low-resource translation (Flores+), health scenarios (HealthBench), and reasoning-heavy tasks (LiveCodeBench and Humanity's Last Exam). Furthermore, our method proves to be data-efficient, robust across different hyperparameters, and capable of generating effective textual contexts that generalize well across different models.

</details>


### [106] [TruncProof: A Guardrail for LLM-based JSON Generation under Token-Length Constraints](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13076v3)
*Yoshio Kato,Shuhei Tarashima*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: TruncProof是一种语法约束生成方法，能在严格令牌限制下生成有效的JSON输出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法严格强制执行最大令牌数，导致无限生成或截断输出，引起系统故障。

Method: 提出TruncProof，利用LL(1)解析器的特性，在每一步解码时高效地近似完成语法有效输出所需的最小令牌数。

Result: 在Text-to-JSON任务上，即使在严格令牌约束下也能生成语法正确的输出，且能与高级解码策略结合实现语义准确。

Conclusion: TruncProof解决了令牌限制问题，实现了语法有效且语义准确的JSON生成。

中文摘要：基于LLM的机器可读输出（如JSON）的生成因其与外部系统的集成而受到广泛关注。然而，现有方法无法严格强制执行要生成的最大令牌数，导致无限生成或截断输出，从而引起系统故障。为解决这一限制，我们提出了TruncProof，一种新颖的语法约束生成方法，使LLM能够在遵守预定义令牌限制的同时生成语法有效的JSON。通过利用LL(1)解析器的特性，TruncProof在每一步解码时高效地近似完成语法有效输出所需的最小令牌数。在Text-to-JSON指令任务上的实验表明，TruncProof即使在严格的令牌约束下也能成功生成语法正确的输出。此外，我们展示了TruncProof可以与先进的解码策略有效结合，生成不仅语法有效而且语义准确的输出。源代码公开于https://github.com/Yosshi999/TruncProof

Original abstract: The LLM-based generation of machine-readable outputs such as JSON has attracted significant attention for integration with external systems. However, existing approaches cannot strictly enforce the maximum number of tokens to be generated, leading to infinite generation or truncated outputs that cause a system malfunction. To address this limitation, we propose TruncProof, a novel grammar-constrained generation method that enables LLMs to produce grammatically valid JSONs while adhering to a predefined token limit. By leveraging the properties of LL(1) parsers, TruncProof efficiently approximates the minimum number of tokens required to complete a grammatically valid output at each decoding step. Experiments on the Text-to-JSON instruction tasks demonstrate that TruncProof successfully generates syntactically correct outputs even under strict token constraints. Furthermore, we show that TruncProof can be effectively combined with advanced decoding strategies, resulting in outputs that are not only grammatically valid but also semantically accurate. The source code is public at https://github.com/Yosshi999/TruncProof

</details>


### [107] [AcquisitionSynthesis: Targeted Data Generation using Acquisition Functions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13149v1)
*Ishika Agarwal,Sofia Stoica,Emre Can Acikgoz,Pradeep Natarajan,Mahdi Namazifar,Jiaqi Ma,Dilek Hakkani-Tür*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 基于采集函数的合成数据生成方法，可迁移到agent自我改进

TL;DR: 提出AcquisitionSynthesis方法，将主动学习中的采集函数作为奖励模型，训练语言模型生成更高质量的合成数据，在数学、医学问答和编程任务上获得2-7%的性能提升，并增强对灾难性遗忘的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有合成数据生成方法缺乏定量评估生成样本对下游模型影响的机制，而主动学习的采集函数能提供这种量化信号，从而指导更有效的数据生成。

Method: 利用采集函数作为奖励模型，通过强化学习训练语言模型生成合成数据，使生成的数据对下游学生模型更具信息量和影响力。

Result: 在数学、医学问答和编程任务上，使用AcquisitionSynthesis数据训练的学生模型在分布内任务上性能提升2-7%，且对灾难性遗忘更鲁棒；该方法可跨模型和资源范式迁移。

Conclusion: AcquisitionSynthesis提供了一种原则性的模型感知自我改进路径，超越了静态数据集。

中文摘要：数据质量仍然是开发能力强、有竞争力的模型的关键瓶颈。研究人员探索了许多生成高质量样本的方法。一些工作依赖拒绝采样：生成大量合成样本并过滤掉低质量样本。其他工作依赖更大规模或闭源模型来提取模型弱点、必要技能或课程，以此为基础进行数据生成。这些工作有一个共同的局限性：没有定量方法来衡量生成样本对下游学习者的影响。主动学习文献正好提供了这种方法，即采集函数。采集函数衡量数据的信息量和/或影响力，提供可解释的、以模型为中心的信号。受此启发，我们提出AcquisitionSynthesis：使用采集函数作为奖励模型来训练语言模型生成更高质量的合成数据。我们在数学、医学问答和编程等经典可验证任务上进行了实验。我们的实验结果表明：（1）使用AcquisitionSynthesis数据训练的学生模型在分布内任务上表现良好（提升2-7%），并且对灾难性遗忘更具鲁棒性；（2）AcquisitionSynthesis模型可以为其他模型以及从低资源到高资源的训练范式生成数据。通过利用采集奖励，我们试图展示一条超越静态数据集的、原则性的模型感知自我改进路径。

Original abstract: Data quality remains a critical bottleneck in developing capable, competitive models. Researchers have explored many ways to generate top quality samples. Some works rely on rejection sampling: generating lots of synthetic samples and filtering out low-quality samples. Other works rely on larger or closed-source models to extract model weaknesses, necessary skills, or a curriculum off of which to base data generation. These works have one common limitation: there is no quantitative approach to measure the impact of the generated samples on the downstream learner. Active learning literature provides exactly this, in the form of acquisition functions. Acquisition functions measure the informativeness and/or influence of data, providing interpretable, model-centric signals. Inspired by this, we propose AcquisitionSynthesis: using acquisition functions as reward models to train language models to generate higher-quality synthetic data. We conduct experiments on classic verifiable tasks of math, medical question-answering, and coding. Our experimental results indicate that (1) student models trained with AcquisitionSynthesis data achieve good performance on in-distribution tasks (2-7% gain) and is more robust to catastrophic forgetting, and (2) AcquisitionSynthesis models can generate data for other models and for low-to-high resource training paradigms. By leveraging acquisition rewards, we seek to demonstrate a principled path toward model-aware self-improvement that surpasses static datasets.

</details>


### [108] [GAGPO: Generalized Advantage Grouped Policy Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13217v1)
*Siyuan Zhu,Chao Yu,Rongxin Yang,Zongkai Liu,Jinjun Hu,Qiwen Chen,Yibo Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出GAGPO，无评论家RL方法用于多轮agent信用分配，可迁移至代码优化agent长期轨迹学习。

TL;DR: 提出GAGPO，一种无评论家的强化学习方法，通过非参数化分组价值代理实现多轮环境中的精确信用分配，显著优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮强化学习中信用分配困难，智能体仅获得稀疏的轨迹级奖励，难以确定中间动作的贡献，且现有方法依赖昂贵的辅助价值模型。

Method: GAGPO通过从采样轨迹构建非参数化分组价值代理，计算TD/GAE风格的时间优势，递归传播结果监督，并结合分组优势归一化和动作级重要性比率，实现稳定的局部优化信号提取。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebShop上，GAGPO优于强强化学习基线，并展现出更快的早期学习、更高的交互效率和更平滑的优化动态。

Conclusion: GAGPO为多轮智能体强化学习提供了一个简单有效的框架，解决了无评论家情况下的信用分配问题。

中文摘要：强化学习已成为对大型语言模型智能体进行后训练的强大范式，但在多轮环境中的信用分配仍然是一个挑战。智能体通常仅在回合结束时获得稀疏的轨迹级奖励，这使得难以确定哪些中间动作促成了成功或失败。因此，在不依赖昂贵的辅助价值模型的情况下，将延迟的结果传播回单个决策步骤仍然是一个开放问题。我们提出了广义优势分组策略优化（GAGPO），这是一种无评论家的强化学习方法，用于精确的、步骤对齐的时间信用分配。GAGPO从采样轨迹中构建非参数化的分组价值代理，并利用它计算TD/GAE风格的时间优势，递归地将结果监督向后传播。结合分组优势归一化和动作级重要性比率，GAGPO直接从多轮轨迹中提取稳定的局部优化信号。在ALFWorld和WebShop上的实验表明，GAGPO优于强强化学习基线。进一步的分析显示，其早期学习更快、交互效率更高、优化动态更平滑，表明GAGPO为多轮智能体强化学习提供了一个简单而有效的框架。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning has become a powerful paradigm for post-training large language model agents, yet credit assignment in multi-turn environments remains a challenge. Agents often receive sparse, trajectory-level rewards only at the end of an episode, making it difficult to determine which intermediate actions contributed to success or failure. As a result, propagating delayed outcomes back to individual decision steps without relying on costly auxiliary value models remains an open problem. We propose Generalized Advantage Grouped Policy Optimization (GAGPO), a critic-free reinforcement learning method for precise, step-aligned temporal credit assignment. GAGPO constructs a non-parametric grouped value proxy from sampled rollouts and uses it to compute TD/GAE-style temporal advantages, recursively propagating outcome supervision backward through time. Combined with group-wise advantage normalization and an action-level importance ratio, GAGPO extracts stable, localized optimization signals directly from multi-turn trajectories. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop show that GAGPO outperforms strong reinforcement learning baselines. Further analyses demonstrate faster early-stage learning, improved interaction efficiency, and smoother optimization dynamics, suggesting that GAGPO offers a simple yet effective framework for multi-turn agentic reinforcement learning.

### [109] [CANTANTE: Optimizing Agentic Systems via Contrastive Credit Attribution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13295v1)
*Tom Zehle*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent系统优化框架，直接相关coding agent配置优化。

TL;DR: CANTANTE通过对比多个联合配置的轨迹将系统级奖励分解为每个智能体更新信号，从而优化多智能体系统的提示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动化配置基于LLM的多智能体系统面临挑战，因为分数仅在系统层面可用而参数局部，因此需要解决信用分配问题。

Method: 提出CANTANTE框架，通过对比同一查询下多个联合配置的轨迹，将系统级奖励分解为每个智能体的更新信号，并实例化用于提示优化。

Result: 在MBPP、GSM8K和HotpotQA上，CANTANTE取得最佳平均排名，优于未优化提示，在MBPP上比最强基线提高18.9个百分点，在GSM8K上提高12.5个百分点，推理成本更低，并在HotpotQA上保持竞争力。信用分析确认归因器产生有意义的每智能体信号。

Conclusion: CANTANTE通过将系统级奖励分解为每个智能体的更新信号，有效解决了多智能体系统中的信用分配问题，在多个基准上取得优异性能并降低推理成本。

中文摘要：基于LLM的多智能体系统在复杂现实任务中表现出强大性能，例如软件工程、预测建模和检索增强生成。然而，自动化配置这些系统仍是一个结构性挑战，因为分数仅在系统层面可用，而控制智能体行为的参数是局部的。我们认为优化这些系统本质上是一个信用分配问题。因此，我们引入了CANTANTE，一个通过对比同一查询下多个联合配置的轨迹，将系统级奖励分解为每个智能体更新信号的框架。我们将其实例化用于提示优化，将智能体提示视为可学习的系统参数。我们在编程（MBPP）、数学推理（GSM8K）和多跳问答（HotpotQA）上评估了CANTANTE与GEPA和MIPROv2。在这些基准测试中，CANTANTE在所有评估的优化器中取得了最佳平均排名，并且始终优于未优化的提示。它在MBPP上比最强基线提高了18.9个百分点，在GSM8K上提高了12.5个百分点，同时推理成本更低。在HotpotQA上，它保持在最强基线的一个标准差范围内。关键是，我们的信用相关性分析证实，归因器产生了有意义的每个智能体信号，而不是简单地重复全局系统分数。

Original abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems have demonstrated strong performance across complex real-world tasks, such as software engineering, predictive modeling, and retrieval-augmented generation. Yet automating their configuration remains a structural challenge, as scores are available only at the system level, whereas the parameters governing agent behavior are local. We argue that optimizing these systems is fundamentally a credit-assignment problem. We therefore introduce CANTANTE, a framework that decomposes system-level rewards into per-agent update signals by contrasting rollouts of multiple joint configurations on the same query. We instantiate it for prompt optimization, treating agent prompts as learnable system parameters. We evaluate CANTANTE against GEPA and MIPROv2 on programming (MBPP), mathematical reasoning (GSM8K), and multi-hop question answering (HotpotQA). Across these benchmarks, CANTANTE achieves the best average rank among all evaluated optimizers and consistently outperforms unoptimized prompts. It improves over the strongest baseline by +18.9 percentage points on MBPP and +12.5 percentage points on GSM8K, while incurring a lower inference cost. It remains within one standard deviation of the strongest baseline on HotpotQA. Crucially, our credit correlation analysis confirms that the attributer produces meaningful per-agent signals rather than echoing the global system score.

### [110] [Query-Conditioned Test-Time Self-Training for Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13369v2)
*Chaehee Song,Minseok Seo,Yeeun Seong,Doyi Kim,Changick Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 测试时自训练，查询特定适应，可迁移至agent的自我改进机制。

TL;DR: 提出QueST，通过输入查询自身构造监督信号进行测试时微调，无需外部数据，在数学和科学推理基准上超越基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时缩放无法纠正模型错误或适应查询结构，而测试时优化方法依赖外部数据或缺乏查询对齐，需一种无需外部数据且针对查询特性的适应方法。

Method: 利用输入查询编码的潜在信号构造查询条件的问题-解决方案对，作为监督信号对模型进行参数高效微调，实现查询特定适应。

Result: 在七个数学推理基准和GPQA-Diamond科学推理基准上，QueST一致优于强测试时优化基线。

Conclusion: 查询条件自训练是LLMs测试时适应的有效且实用范式。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）通常以固定参数部署，其性能通常通过增加推理时的计算量来提升。虽然这种测试时缩放可能有效，但它无法纠正模型错误观念或使模型适应单个查询的具体结构。测试时优化通过允许在推理过程中更新参数来解决这一限制，但现有方法要么依赖外部数据，要么优化缺乏查询特定对齐的通用自监督目标。在这项工作中，我们提出了查询条件测试时自训练（QueST），这是一个在推理过程中使用直接从输入查询导出的监督信号来调整模型参数的框架。我们的关键见解是，输入查询本身编码了足够的潜在信号，可用于构建结构相关的“问题-解决方案”对。基于此，QueST生成这些查询条件对，并将其用作测试时参数高效微调的监督信号。然后，调整后的模型用于生成最终答案，实现无需任何外部数据的查询特定适应。在七个数学推理基准和GPQA-Diamond科学推理基准上，QueST始终优于强测试时优化基线。这些结果表明，查询条件自训练是LLMs测试时适应的有效且实用的范式。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are typically deployed with fixed parameters, and their performance is often improved by allocating more computation at inference time. While such test-time scaling can be effective, it cannot correct model misconceptions or adapt the model to the specific structure of an individual query. Test-time optimization addresses this limitation by enabling parameter updates during inference, but existing approaches either rely on external data or optimize generic self-supervised objectives that lack query-specific alignment. In this work, we propose Query-Conditioned Test-Time Self-Training (QueST), a framework that adapts model parameters during inference using supervision derived directly from the input query. Our key insight is that the input query itself encodes latent signals sufficient for constructing structurally related problem--solution pairs. Based on this, QueST generates such query-conditioned pairs and uses them as supervision for parameter-efficient fine-tuning at test time. The adapted model is then used to produce the final answer, enabling query-specific adaptation without any external data. Across seven mathematical reasoning benchmarks and the GPQA-Diamond scientific reasoning benchmark, QueST consistently outperforms strong test-time optimization baselines. These results demonstrate that query-conditioned self-training is an effective and practical paradigm for test-time adaptation in LLMs. Code is available at https://chssong.github.io/Query-Conditioned-TTST/.

### [111] [Many-Shot CoT-ICL: Making In-Context Learning Truly Learn](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13511v3)
*Tsz Ting Chung,Lemao Liu,Mo Yu,Dit-Yan Yeung*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多示例链式思维学习，结构化课程，可迁移至agent情境学习。

TL;DR: 本研究将多示例思维链上下文学习视为上下文中的测试时学习，提出示例应易于理解并按概念进展排序，所提CDS方法在数学任务上取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 识别独特特性，CDS方法在数学任务上提升5.42个百分点。

Conclusion: 将长上下文重新定义为用于测试时学习的结构化课程。

中文摘要：尽管多示例上下文学习（many-shot ICL）取得了显著性能，但先前关于其缩放行为的研究主要关注非推理任务。在这项工作中，我们研究推理任务上的多示例上下文学习，特别关注多示例思维链上下文学习（CoT-ICL）。通过跨非推理和推理任务以及跨非推理导向和推理导向的大型语言模型进行分析，我们识别了多示例 CoT-ICL 的几个独特特性。我们进一步将这些发现解释为多示例 CoT-ICL 是上下文中的测试时学习而非缩放模式匹配，并提出两个原则：（i）示例应易于目标模型理解，（ii）示例应排序以支持平滑的概念进展。在这些原则的指导下，我们提出了曲线示例选择（CDS），一种简单的排序方法，在包含64个示例的数学任务上取得了高达5.42个百分点的提升。总体而言，我们的结果将长上下文窗口从检索缓冲区重新定义为用于上下文测试时学习的结构化课程。

Original abstract: While many-shot ICL achieves remarkable performance, prior studies of its scaling behavior have mainly focused on non-reasoning tasks. In this work, we study many-shot ICL on reasoning tasks, with a particular focus on many-shot chain-of-thought in-context learning (CoT-ICL). Analyzing across non-reasoning and reasoning tasks and across non-reasoning and reasoning-oriented LLMs, we identify several distinctive properties of many-shot CoT-ICL. We further interpret these findings by viewing many-shot CoT-ICL as in-context test-time learning rather than scaled pattern matching, and suggest two principles: (i) demonstrations should be easy for the target model to understand, and (ii) they should be ordered to support a smooth conceptual progression. Guided by the principle, we propose Curvilinear Demonstration Selection (CDS), a simple ordering method that yields up to a 5.42 percentage-point gain on a math task with 64 demonstrations. Overall, our results reframe the long context window from a retrieval buffer into a structured curriculum for in-context test-time learning.

### [112] [RTLC -- Research, Teach-to-Learn, Critique: A three-stage prompting paradigm inspired by the Feynman Learning Technique that lifts LLM-as-judge accuracy on JudgeBench with no fine-tuning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13695v1)
*Andrea Morandi*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: RTLC提示范式提升LLM评判准确性，可用于agent自我反思或评估。

TL;DR: 提出RTLC三阶段提示方法，通过教学脚手架和批判机制显著提升LLM作为评判者的准确性，在JudgeBench上取得14个百分点的绝对提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-as-a-judge在JudgeBench等基准上性能接近随机，需要无需微调或外部工具的方法来提升其判断准确性。

Method: RTLC包含三个阶段：阶段1（Research）将输入包装为费曼学习技术的教学脚手架；阶段2（Teach-to-Learn）以温度0.4生成N=10个独立候选判定；阶段3（Critique）以温度0对候选集进行交叉比较并输出一个批判后的判定。

Result: 在JudgeBench-GPT上，Claude 3.7 Sonnet的成对准确率从64.6%提升至78.6%，优于自我一致性（77.7%）和零样本基线（74.0%）；消融实验表明Teach-to-Learn贡献+9.4pp，N=10边际化贡献+3.7pp，显式批判贡献+0.9pp。

Conclusion: RTLC有效提升了LLM评判准确性，且与事后校准正交组合可带来乘法效应，在成本-准确率前沿上优于自我一致性。

中文摘要：LLM-as-a-judge（以大语言模型作为评判者）现在是开放式生成的默认测量工具，但在公开的JudgeBench基准测试上，即使是经过强指令微调的评判者在客观正确性的成对项目上也仅略高于随机水平。我们提出了RTLC，一种三阶段提示（Prompting）方法——研究（Research）、教以致学（Teach-to-Learn）、批判（Critique）——它将单个黑盒LLM提升为思维集成评判者，无需微调、检索或外部工具。阶段1将输入包裹在一个固定的教学脚手架中，将费曼学习技术（学习→教授→发现差距→简化）移植到LLM提示中。阶段2以温度0.4抽取N=10个独立候选判定。阶段3扮演自身批评者，将候选集与原始问题进行交叉比较，以温度0输出一个被批判的判定。在JudgeBench-GPT（350个困难成对项目）上，Claude 3.7 Sonnet的成对准确率从64.6%（单次简单提示）提升到78.6%（RTLC 10个候选批判）——绝对提升14.0个百分点。RTLC还击败了N=10的自我一致性多数投票（77.7%）和零样本首个候选（74.0%）。一个清晰的三步消融实验将+9.4个百分点归因于教以致学脚手架，+3.7个百分点归因于N=10的边际化，+0.9个百分点归因于显式批判。我们讨论了成本-准确率前沿（RTLC在每个工作点上都高于自我一致性），四个JudgeBench类别（知识、推理、数学、编码）的错误预算分解，以及RTLC如何与事后评判者分数校准正交组合，两种干预在实践中相乘叠加。

Original abstract: LLM-as-a-judge is now the default measurement instrument for open-ended generation, but on the public JudgeBench benchmark even strong instruction-tuned judges barely scrape past random on objective-correctness pairwise items. We introduce RTLC, a three-stage prompting recipe -- Research, Teach-to-Learn, Critique -- that promotes a single black-box LLM into an ensemble-of-thought judge with no fine-tuning, retrieval, or external tools. Stage 1 wraps the input in a fixed pedagogical scaffold porting the Feynman Learning Technique (study $\to$ teach $\to$ find gaps $\to$ simplify) into LLM prompting. Stage 2 draws N=10 independent candidate verdicts at temperature 0.4. Stage 3 acts as its own critic, cross-comparing the candidate set against the original question to emit one critiqued verdict at temperature 0. On JudgeBench-GPT (350 hard pairwise items), Claude 3.7 Sonnet's pairwise accuracy climbs from 64.6% (single-shot vanilla prompt) to 78.6% (RTLC critique-of-10) -- an absolute 14.0-percentage-point gain. RTLC also beats N=10 self-consistency majority voting (77.7%) and a zero-shot first candidate (74.0%). A clean three-step ablation attributes +9.4 pp to the Teach-to-Learn scaffold, +3.7 pp to N=10 marginalisation, and +0.9 pp to explicit critique. We discuss the cost-accuracy frontier (RTLC sits above self-consistency at every working point), the error-budget breakdown across the four JudgeBench categories (knowledge, reasoning, math, coding), and how RTLC composes orthogonally with post-hoc judge-score calibration, with the two interventions compounding multiplicatively in practice.

### [113] [Generative Floor Plan Design with LLMs via Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14117v1)
*Luis Lara,Aristides Milios,Zhi Hao Luo,Aditya Sharma,Ge Ya Luo,Christopher Beckham,Florian Golemo,Christopher Pal*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: RLVR微调LLM满足约束，方法可迁移至代码优化中约束满足任务。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于LLM和RLVR的文本平面图生成方法，满足拓扑和数值约束，在兼容性等指标上大幅提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成方法仅支持连通性约束，无法处理数值约束（如房间尺寸和面积），而专业平面图设计需要同时满足两类约束。

Method: 微调大语言模型（LLM）于真实平面图，然后应用带可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）优化拓扑和数值约束，并设计约束遵守度指标进行系统评估。

Result: 模型生成满足连通性和数值约束的平面图，在真实感、兼容性和多样性上优于现有方法，兼容性相对降低至少94%。

Conclusion: LLM能有效处理平面图设计中的约束任务，为文本生成建模的广泛应用提供可能。

中文摘要：用于专业平面图设计的AI系统必须精确控制房间尺寸和面积，同时尊重房间之间的期望连通性，并保持功能和美学质量。现有的生成方法主要侧重于尊重房间之间的请求连通性，但不支持生成满足数值约束的平面图。我们提出了一种基于文本的平面图生成方法，该方法在真实平面图上微调大型语言模型（LLM），然后应用具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）来提高对拓扑和数值约束的遵守度，同时抑制无效或重叠的输出。此外，我们设计了一组约束遵守度指标，以系统地衡量生成的平面图与用户定义约束的一致性。我们的模型生成的平面图满足用户定义的连通性和数值约束，并在真实感、兼容性和多样性指标上优于现有方法。在所有任务中，我们的方法相比现有方法在兼容性上实现了至少94%的相对降低。我们的结果表明，LLM可以在此设置中有效处理约束，表明文本生成建模具有更广泛的应用前景。

Original abstract: An AI system for professional floor plan design must precisely control room dimensions and areas while respecting the desired connectivity between rooms and maintaining functional and aesthetic quality. Existing generative approaches focus primarily on respecting the requested connectivity between rooms, but do not support generating floor plans that respect numerical constraints. We introduce a text-based floor plan generation approach that fine-tunes a large language model (LLM) on real plans and then applies reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) to improve adherence to topological and numerical constraints while discouraging invalid or overlapping outputs. Furthermore, we design a set of constraint adherence metrics to systematically measure how generated floor plans align with user-defined constraints. Our model generates floor plans that satisfy user-defined connectivity and numerical constraints and outperforms existing methods on Realism, Compatibility, and Diversity metrics. Across all tasks, our approach achieves at least a 94% relative reduction in Compatibility compared with existing methods. Our results demonstrate that LLMs can effectively handle constraints in this setting, suggesting broader applications for text-based generative modeling.

</details>


### [114] [Why Retrieval-Augmented Generation Fails: A Graph Perspective](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14192v1)
*Kai Guo,Xinnan Dai,Zhibo Zhang,Nuohan Lin,Shenglai Zeng,Jie Ren,Haoyu Han,Jiliang Tang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 从图视角分析RAG失败原因，为agent检索增强生成提供诊断方法

TL;DR: 通过电路追踪构建归因图，发现RAG正确与错误预测在推理路径和证据流结构上存在差异，并据此开发了错误检测和干预方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RAG系统尽管能访问外部信息，但仍会出错，但其失败原因尚不明确，需要从模型内部理解证据整合机制。

Method: 使用电路追踪构建归因图，分析Transformer层间信息流；基于归因图拓扑特征开发错误检测框架，并通过强化问题约束的证据基础进行干预。

Result: 正确预测具有更深推理路径、更分布式证据流和更结构化局部连接；错误预测则表现为浅层、碎片化和过度集中的证据流；干预能提升证据整合效果。

Conclusion: 归因图揭示了RAG失败的结构性原因，并提供了基于图拓扑的错误检测和干预手段，有助于提高RAG系统的可靠性。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）已成为一种强大且广泛使用的方法，通过将生成过程基于检索到的证据来改进大型语言模型。然而，RAG系统在许多情况下仍会产生错误答案。为什么RAG在能够访问外部信息的情况下仍然失败，这一点目前尚不清楚。我们提出了一项关于检索增强生成的模型内部研究，探讨检索到的证据如何影响答案生成。通过电路追踪，我们构建了归因图，模拟解码过程中信息在Transformer层间的流动。这些图表示了检索到的上下文、中间模型激活和生成词元之间的相互作用，提供了外部证据如何被整合到模型推理过程中的图级电路视角。在多个问答基准测试中，我们观察到一致的结构性差异：正确的预测表现出更深的推理路径、更分布的证据流以及更结构化的局部连接模式，而失败的预测则表现出更浅、碎片化且过度集中的证据流。基于这些发现，我们开发了一个基于图的错误检测框架，利用归因图的拓扑特征。此外，我们证明了归因图能够实现有针对性的干预。通过强化受问题约束的证据基础，我们重新调整内部路由，使得答案生成始终由问题引导，从而更有效地整合检索到的信息并减少错误。

Original abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has become a powerful and widely used approach for improving large language models by grounding generation in retrieved evidence. However, RAG systems still produce incorrect answers in many cases. Why RAG fails despite having access to external information remains poorly understood. We present a model-internal study of retrieval-augmented generation that examines how retrieved evidence influences answer generation. Using circuit tracing, we construct attribution graphs that model the flow of information through transformer layers during decoding. These graphs represent interactions among retrieved context, intermediate model activations, and generated tokens, providing a graph, circuit-level view of how external evidence is integrated into the model's reasoning process across multiple question answering benchmarks, we observe consistent structural differences: correct predictions exhibit deeper reasoning paths, more distributed evidence flow, and a more structured pattern of local connectivity, while failed predictions show shallower, fragmented, and overly concentrated evidence flow. Building on these findings, we develop a graph-based error detection framework that uses attribution-graph topology features. Furthermore, we show that attribution graphs enable targeted interventions. By reinforcing question-constrained evidence grounding, we reshape internal routing so that answer generation remains guided by the question, leading to more effective integration of retrieved information and fewer errors.

</details>

### [115] [Metacognition Should Be the Scientific Framework for Bounded and Effective Self-Governance in Generative AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23981v1)
*Eugene Yu Ji,Igor Grossmann,Amir-Hossein Karimi*

Main category: q-bio.NC

Selection reason: 提出元认知框架用于生成式AI自我治理，对agent自我改进有潜在启发

TL;DR: 本文提出元认知作为生成式AI自我治理的科学框架，要求计算、算法和生态三个层面的对齐，从而统一能力与治理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI面临在高不确定性、证据缺失或上下文不足时维持并管理自身生成活动的共同问题，需要有效的自我治理框架。

Method: 基于立场论文形式，从计算、算法和生态三个层面论证元认知对齐的必要性和实现路径。

Result: 提出了元认知对齐框架：计算层定义监控、评估、控制和适应等元级功能；算法层通过引出、迭代和模块化实现功能；生态层使元认知信号在界面、工作流和问责中可操作。

Conclusion: 元认知使生成式AI既能胜任又能良好治理，而非将能力与治理视为对立目标。

中文摘要：生成式人工智能研究日益面临一个共同问题：系统必须在高不确定性、证据缺失或上下文不足的情况下维持并管理其自身的生成活动。本立场论文认为，元认知应成为生成式人工智能中有界且有效的自我治理的科学框架，其中输出生成得到适当评估，同时生成系统导航和调节自身活动的能力也得到评估。我们通过表明有界且有效的AI自我治理需要在计算、算法和生态层面实现元认知对齐来推进这一立场。在计算层面，元认知规定了系统应服务的元级功能，如监控、评估、控制和适应。在算法层面，这些功能通过诸如引出、迭代和模块化等程序实现。在生态层面，元认知信号在界面、工作流和问责安排中变得有意义、可操作和可问责。因此，元认知使得将生成式人工智能视为既有能力又治理良好的成为可能，而不是将能力和治理视为相互竞争的目标。

Original abstract: Generative AI research increasingly confronts a shared problem: systems must sustain yet govern their own generative activity when uncertainty is high, evidence is missing, or context is insufficient. This position paper argues that metacognition should become the scientific framework for bounded and effective self governance in generative AI, where output generation is properly evaluated together with the capacities through which generative systems navigate and regulate their own activity. We advance this position by showing that bounded and effective AI self-governance requires metacognitive alignment across computational, algorithmic, and ecological levels. At the computational level, metacognition specifies the meta-level functions a system is meant to serve, such as monitoring, evaluation, control, and adaptation. At the algorithmic level, these functions are realized through procedures such as elicitation, iteration, and modularization. At the ecological level, metacognitive signals become meaningful, actionable, and accountable within the interface, workflow, and accountability arrangements. Metacognition thus makes it possible to conceive generative AI as both capable and well-governed, rather than treating capability and governance as competing aims.

</details>

### [116] [Turning Intent into Specifications: A Benchmark and an Interactive User-Assistant Agent](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20585v1)
*Hao Wang,Ligong Han,Kai Xu,Akash Srivastava*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 用户意图转规范基准与交互agent，直接相关coding agent协作。

TL;DR: 提出SpecBench基准和Buddy智能体，通过结构化分解用户意图和模拟用户评估，改善智能体与用户的协作规范制定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体无法有效处理模糊用户意图，要么过早执行，要么过度提问，缺乏主动协作能力。

Method: SpecBench评估智能体将用户意图转化为结构化规范的能力；Buddy采用形态分析分解意图，创建模拟用户评估候选选择，再与真实用户确认。

Result: 现有智能体表现出两种极端行为，而Buddy通过结构化工作流改进了协作效率。

Conclusion: 强调智能体-用户协作（而非仅代码生成）是未来智能体设计的关键前沿。

中文摘要：当今的智能体在执行范围明确的软件设计计划方面非常高效，但用户意图往往模糊不清，存在多个同样有效的解决方案。在本文中，我们引入了SpecBench，这是一个新的基准测试，用于评估智能体将用户意图转化为符合用户偏好的结构化、可执行规范的能力。智能体可以访问过去的用户对话，并可以在固定轮次内与用户交互以提出澄清性问题。我们发现现有智能体表现出两种极端行为：（i）难以主动与用户协作，过早进入执行模式，同时高估自己对用户偏好的理解；（ii）通过询问每一个模糊的设计选择来耗尽问题预算。为了解决这一限制，我们引入了一个用户辅助智能体：Buddy。它遵循受经典形态分析启发的工作流程，将用户意图分解为设计维度和候选选择的结构化空间。然后，它创建模拟用户来评估这些选择，再与真实用户互动以解决剩余歧义并最终确定规范。通过将重点从执行转移到规范，SpecBench和Buddy强调智能体与用户的协作（而不仅仅是代码生成）是未来智能体设计的关键前沿。

Original abstract: Today's agents are highly effective at implementing well-scoped software design plans, but user intent is often vague and admits multiple equally valid solutions. In this paper, we introduce SpecBench, a new benchmark for evaluating an agent's ability to translate user intent into a structured, executable specification that aligns with user preferences. The agent is given access to past user conversations and may interact with the user for a fixed number of rounds to ask clarifying questions. We find that existing agents exhibit two extreme behaviors: they either (i) struggle to collaborate proactively with users, entering implementation mode too quickly while overestimating their understanding of user preferences, or (ii) exhaust their question budget by asking about every ambiguous design choice. To address this limitation, we introduce a user-assistant agent: Buddy. It follows a workflow inspired by classical morphological analysis, decomposing user intent into a structured space of design dimensions and candidate choices. It then creates simulated users to evaluate these choices, before engaging the real user to resolve remaining ambiguities and finalize the specification. By shifting the focus from execution to specification, SpecBench and Buddy emphasize agent-user collaboration (not just code generation) as a key frontier in future agent design.

</details>
